# Welcome | Plugin API

Welcome to the Tebex Plugin API documentation.

The Plugin API is for implementing command execution on game servers - an example of this would be the official Tebex Minecraft Plugin.

circle-info

If you've created an SDK please send an email to support@tebex.io and we'd be happy to showcase it on this site.

[NextRate Limitschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/rate-limits)

Last updated 1 year ago

This site uses cookies to deliver its service and to analyze traffic. By browsing this site, you accept the [privacy policy](https://policies.gitbook.com/privacy/cookies)
.

close

# Rate Limits | Plugin API

The Plugin API enforces a rate limit of up to 500 requests **over a period of 5 minutes**, determined by your secret key.

[PreviousWelcomechevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin)
[NextAuthenticationchevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/authentication)

Last updated 1 year ago

---

# Authentication | Plugin API

To access the API all requests need to be authenticated via a Game Server's secret key. To obtain a secret key please navigate to [https://creator.tebex.io/game-serversarrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/game-servers)
, and click _Edit_ on the relevant server.

Supply the secret key by setting the `X-Tebex-Secret` header in all requests to the API.

circle-info

Please note that all requests to the API must be sent via HTTPS.

[PreviousRate Limitschevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/rate-limits)
[NextError Handlingchevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/error-handling)

Last updated 1 year ago

---

# Error Handling | Plugin API

Errors are JSON format and are based around the standard HTTP status codes.

For example when an invalid secret key is provided the HTTP status code `403 Forbidden` will be returned along with a JSON body containing further information.

The `error_message` object will always be user friendly and should be shown directly to the client.

[PreviousAuthenticationchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/authentication)
[NextOfficial Pluginschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/official-plugins)

Last updated 6 years ago

---

# RPC | Plugin API

Our API design follows a **RESTful** architecture. In some cases, you may be unable to create a proper request due to limitations of the game or framework you are working with.

To work around this, you may use an implementation of jsonRPC (remote procedure call) to interact with the Plugin API.

Send a **POST** to the **/rpc** endpoint with information about the API request you want to make. It will be rebuilt into a RESTful request, forwarded to the plugin API, and the associated response will be returned to you.

**You must include a forward slash at the end of the URL when using RPC.**

*   ✅**Correct**: `https://plugin.tebex.io/rpc/`
    
*   ❌**Incorrect**: `https://plugin.tebex.io/rpc`
    

Below is an example request to get a store's information via RPC.

Copy

    {
        "method": "GET",
        "params": {
            "SecretKey": "your-secret-key-here",
            "Path": "/information"
        }
    }

Here is an example of a POST request using RPC.

Copy

    {
        "method": "POST",
        "params": {
            "SecretKey": "your-secret-key-here",
            "Path": "/checkout",
            "Body": {
                "package_id": "12345",
                "username": "foo"
            }
        }
    }

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/rpc#make-an-rpc-request)

Make an RPC request


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`POST` `https://plugin.tebex.io/rpc/`

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/rpc#request-body)

Request Body

Name

Type

Description

method\*

String

HTTP verb to use for the request (GET, POST, PUT, DELETE)

params\*

Object

Object describing the request to be made

params.SecretKey\*

String

Your store's secret key.

params.Path\*

String

Your desired endpoint on the Plugin API

params.Body

Object

JSON body to send to Plugin API

200: OK Forwarded response code from Plugin API

ellipsis

See relevant **Endpoint** for specific response information.

Copy

    {
        "error_code": 400,
        "error_message": "'Path' is required in 'params'"
    }

See relevant **Endpoint** for specific response information.

See relevant **Endpoint** for specific response information.

[PreviousOfficial Pluginschevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/official-plugins)
[NextInformationchevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/endpoints/information)

Last updated 2 years ago

# Command Queue | Plugin API

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/endpoints/command-queue#get-due-players)

Get due players


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`GET` `https://plugin.tebex.io/queue`

List the players who have commands due to be executed when they next login to the game server. This endpoint also returns any offline commands to be processed and the amount of seconds to wait before performing the queue check again. All clients should strictly follow the response of `next_check`, failure to do so would result in your secret key being revoked or IP address being banned from accessing the API. NOTE: The \`player.id\` field is an internal ID, sometimes referred to as the 'plugin username ID'. This is the value to use to retrieve online commands for a player (see below). the \`player.uuid\` field is the actual username ID value, depending on the username type (a Steam64ID for steam games, an XUID for Xbox Live etc), and is the value that should be used to replace the \`{id}\` placeholder in commands.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/endpoints/command-queue#headers)

Headers

Name

Type

Description

X-Tebex-Secret

string

The secret key of the server.

200

Copy

    {
      "meta": {
        "execute_offline": false,
        "next_check": 90,
        "more": false
      },
      "players": [\
        {\
          "id": 1,\
          "name": "Notch",\
          "uuid": "365bfa21803249ee9b634fe890c9d43f"\
        },\
        {\
          "id": 2,\
          "name": "7n",\
          "uuid": "ef01f2da1b284ad6ba8ba2aaf4432e22"\
        },\
        {\
          "id": 3,\
          "name": "hfmx",\
          "uuid": "897a2737777a4776909a0148919c376a"\
        }\
      ]
    }

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/endpoints/command-queue#get-offline-commands)

Get offline commands


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`GET` `https://plugin.tebex.io/queue/offline-commands`

Get the offline commands which are due to be executed. These commands should be executed immediately and no checks are required against the related players. NOTE: The \`player.id\` field is an internal ID, sometimes referred to as the 'plugin username ID', and isn't needed for offline commands. The \`player.uuid\` field is the actual username ID value, depending on the username type (a Steam64ID for steam games, an XUID for Xbox Live etc), and is the value that should be used to replace the \`{id}\` placeholder in commands.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/endpoints/command-queue#headers-1)

Headers

Name

Type

Description

X-Tebex-Secret

string

The secret key of the server.

200

Copy

    {
      "meta": {
        "limited": false
      },
      "commands": [\
        {\
          "id": 1,\
          "command": "say Thank you for purchasing, {name}.",\
          "payment": 123,\
          "package": 123,\
          "conditions": {\
            "delay": 60\
          },\
          "player": {\
            "id": 1,\
            "name": "Notch",\
            "uuid": "365bfa21803249ee9b634fe890c9d43f"\
          }\
        },\
        {\
          "id": 2,\
          "command": "say Thank you for purchasing, {name}.",\
          "payment": 123,\
          "package": 123,\
          "conditions": {\
            "delay": 0\
          },\
          "player": {\
            "id": 2,\
            "name": "7n",\
            "uuid": "ef01f2da1b284ad6ba8ba2aaf4432e22"\
          }\
        },\
        {\
          "id": 3,\
          "command": "say Thank you for purchasing, {name}.",\
          "payment": 123,\
          "package": 123,\
          "conditions": {\
            "delay": 0\
          },\
          "player": {\
            "id": 3,\
            "name": "hfmx",\
            "uuid": "897a2737777a4776909a0148919c376a"\
          }\
        }\
      ]
    }

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/endpoints/command-queue#get-online-commands)

Get online commands


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`GET` `https://plugin.tebex.io/queue/online-commands/{player-id}`

List the due online commands for a specific player. These commands should only be executed when the player is online and all the conditions have been met (such as if the player has the required amount of inventory slots).

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/endpoints/command-queue#path-parameters)

Path Parameters

Name

Type

Description

player-id

string

The ID of the player you want to retrieve the online commands for.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/endpoints/command-queue#headers-2)

Headers

Name

Type

Description

X-Tebex-Secret

string

The secret key of the server.

200

Copy

    {
      "commands": [\
        {\
          "id": 1,\
          "command": "give {name} TNT",\
          "payment": 123,\
          "package": 123,\
          "conditions": {\
            "delay": 0,\
            "slots": 0\
          }\
        },\
        {\
          "id": 2,\
          "command": "give {name} DIRT",\
          "payment": 123,\
          "package": 123,\
          "conditions": {\
            "delay": 0,\
            "slots": 0\
          }\
        },\
        {\
          "id": 3,\
          "command": "give {name} STONE",\
          "payment": 123,\
          "package": 123,\
          "conditions": {\
            "delay": 0,\
            "slots": 0\
          }\
        }\
      ]
    }

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/endpoints/command-queue#delete-commands)

Delete commands


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`DELETE` `https://plugin.tebex.io/queue`

Delete one or more commands which have been executed on the game server. An empty response with the status code of`204 No Content` will be returned on completion.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/endpoints/command-queue#headers-3)

Headers

Name

Type

Description

X-Tebex-Secret

string

The secret key of the server.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/endpoints/command-queue#request-body)

Request Body

Name

Type

Description

ids

array

An array of one or more command IDs to delete.

204

Copy

[PreviousInformationchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/endpoints/information)
[NextListingchevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/endpoints/listing)

Last updated 5 years ago

# Community Goals | Plugin API

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/endpoints/community-goals#get-all-community-goals)

Get all community goals


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`GET` `https://plugin.tebex.io/community_goals`

Retrieve all community goals created on your account.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/endpoints/community-goals#headers)

Headers

Name

Type

Description

X-Tebex-Secret

string

The secret key of a server.

200

Copy

    [\
       {\
           "id": 4,\
           "created_at": "2019-03-13 13:11:57",\
           "updated_at": "2019-04-09 10:59:26",\
           "account": 55,\
           "name": "Demo Community Goal",\
           "description": "<p>Demo Community Goal</p>",\
           "image": "",\
           "target": "100.00",\
           "current": "72.00",\
           "repeatable": 0,\
           "last_achieved": null,\
           "times_achieved": 0,\
           "status": "active",\
           "sale": 0\

Name

Type

Description

X-Tebex-Secret

string

The secret key of a server.

Request Body

Name

Type

Description

expires\_at

string

The gift card's expiry date in the format _yyyy-mm-dd hh:mm:ss_.

note

string

The note that will be stored against the gift card.

amount

number

The currency value of the gift card should have upon creation.

200

Copy

    {
      "data": {
        "id": 40,
        "code": "094006746161",
        "balance": {
          "starting": "60.00",
          "remaining": "60.00",
          "currency": "GBP"
        },
        "note": "My note",
        "void": false
      }
    }

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/endpoints/payments#create-a-payment)

Create a payment


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`POST` `https://plugin.tebex.io/payments`

Create a manual payment in the same way as is possible from the control panel. One or more packages should be added to the payment, and the package commands will be processed in the same way as would be for a standard manual payment.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/endpoints/payments#headers-3)

Headers

Name

Type

Description

X-Tebex-Secret

string

The secret key of a server.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/endpoints/payments#request-body)

Request Body

Name

Type

Description

note

string

A note to assign to the payment.

packages\[\]\[options\]

object

An object of key => value pairs for the required option fields (as retrieved from the /fields endpoint).

packages\[\]\[id\]

number

The ID of the package.

packages

array

Array of packages to add to the payment.

price

integer

The price of the payment.

ign

string

The username of the user to apply the payment to.

204

Copy

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/endpoints/payments#update-a-payment)

# Coupons | Plugin API

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/endpoints/coupons#get-all-coupons)

Get all coupons


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`GET` `https://plugin.tebex.io/coupons`

Return a paginated list of coupons on your account.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/endpoints/coupons#headers)

Headers

Name

Type

Description

X-Tebex-Secret

string

The secret key of a server.

200

Copy

    {
     "pagination": {
            "totalResults": 157,
            "currentPage": 1,
            "lastPage": 7,
            "previous": null,
            "next": "https://plugin.tebex.io/coupons?page=2"
      },
      "data": [\
        {\
          "id": 2,\
          "code": "mycode-123",\
          "effective": {\
            "type": "cart",\
            "packages": [],\
            "categories": []\
          },\
          "discount": {\
            "type": "value",\
            "percentage": 0,\
            "value": 2\
          },\
          "expire": {\
            "redeem_unlimited": "false",\
            "expire_never": "true",\
            "limit": 0,\
            "date": "1901-12-13T20:45:52+0000"\
          },\
          "basket_type": "single",\
          "start_date": "2017-01-01T00:00:00+0000",\
          "user_limit": 1,\
          "minimum": 5,\
          "username": "Notch",\
          "note": "Coupon note"\
        }\
      ]
    }

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/endpoints/coupons#get-a-coupon)

Get a coupon


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`GET` `https://plugin.tebex.io/coupons/{id}`

Get a coupon by ID.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/endpoints/coupons#path-parameters)

Path Parameters

Name

Type

Description

id

string

The coupon ID.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/endpoints/coupons#headers-1)

Headers

Name

Type

Description

X-Tebex-Secret

string

The secret key of a server.

200

Copy

    {
      "data": {
        "id": 2,
        "code": "mycode-123",
        "effective": {
          "type": "cart",
          "packages": [],
          "categories": []
        },
        "discount": {
          "type": "value",
          "percentage": 0,
          "value": 2
        },
        "expire": {
          "redeem_unlimited": "true",
          "expire_never": "true",
          "limit": 0,
          "date": "1901-12-13T20:45:52+0000"
        },
        "basket_type": "single",
        "start_date": "2017-01-01T00:00:00+0000",
        "user_limit": 1,
        "minimum": 5,
        "username": "",
        "note": "Coupon note"
      }
    }

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/endpoints/coupons#create-a-coupon)

Create a coupon


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`POST` `https://plugin.tebex.io/coupons`

Create a coupon code.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/endpoints/coupons#headers-2)

Headers

Name

Type

Description

X-Tebex-Secret

string

The secret key of a server.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/endpoints/coupons#request-body)

Request Body

Name

Type

Description

code

string

The code of the coupon.

effective\_on

string

What this coupon should be effective on, either "package", "category" or "cart".

packages

array

An array of package IDs this coupon should apply to. Only used if effective\_on is "package".

categories

array

An array of category IDs this coupon should apply to. Only used if effective\_on is "category".

discount\_type

string

"percentage" or "value".

discount\_amount

integer

The currency amount to discount.

discount\_percentage

integer

The percentage amount to be discounted.

redeem\_unlimited

boolean

Can the coupon be redeemed an unlimited amount of times.

expire\_never

boolean

Should the coupon ignore the expire\_date.

expire\_limit

number

Only used if redeem\_unlimited is false.

expire\_date

string

Only used if `expire_never` is `false` - formatted in yyyy-mm-dd.

start\_date

string

The start date of the coupon in the format of yyyy-mm-dd.

basket\_type

string

"single", "subscription", or "both".

minimum

number

Minimum value of basket before the coupon can be redeemed.

discount\_application\_method

number

0 = Apply to each package (default), 1 = Apply to basket (before sales), 2 = Apply to basket (after sales)

username

string

The username to restrict the coupon to.

note

string

The note to store against the coupon.

200

Copy

    {
      "data": {
        "id": 3,
        "code": "mycode-123",
        "effective": {
          "type": "cart",
          "packages": [],
          "categories": []
        },
        "discount": {
          "type": "value",
          "percentage": 0,
          "value": 2
        },
        "expire": {
          "redeem_unlimited": "false",
          "expire_never": "true",
          "limit": 0,
          "date": "-0001-11-30T00:00:00+0000"
        },
        "basket_type": "single",
        "start_date": "2017-01-01T00:00:00+0000",
        "user_limit": 1,
        "minimum": 5,
        "discount_application_method" : 0,
        "username": "Notch",
        "note": "Coupon note"
      }
    }

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/endpoints/coupons#delete-a-coupon)

# Introducing Tebex | Creators

Tebex is the go-to platform for selling digital content—whether you're a large game studio, a FiveM asset developer, or a hobbyist launching your first game server. We're the all-in-one monetization solution designed to grow your revenue and empower your success.

This **Documentation** covers everything you need to manage your Tebex store. Looking for technical implementation guides? [Visit our Developer Documentationarrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/developers)
.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/#why-choose-tebex)

**Why Choose Tebex?**

*   **No Hidden Costs** We’re transparent about our pricing—there are no surprises. Our dedicated [Support team arrow-up-right](https://www.tebex.io/support-creator-form)
    is always here to help.
    
*   **Fast 7-Day Payouts** Once your funds are settled, you can enjoy fast withdrawals via PayPal, local bank transfer, or wire—there will be no long waits.
    
*   **Industry-Leading Seller Protection** As your **Merchant of Record**, we handle chargebacks and disputes on your behalf. With our Seller Protection, you’ll never lose money due to a chargeback—even if the dispute isn't resolved in your favour.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/#before-you-get-started)

**Before You Get Started**

Many features and links in this documentation require a Tebex account. [Create one herearrow-up-right](https://accounts.tebex.io/profile)
 to unlock the full experience.

circle-info

Check out the [**Tebex Academy** arrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@tebex/videos)
for resources to help you get started quickly.

[NextWhy Tebex?chevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/master/why-tebex)

# Overview | Developers

The Headless API works with your existing packages, coupons, sales & creator codes.

If you haven't already done so, we recommend having a read of our [quick start guide](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/getting-started)
 before beginning integration.

You can query the Headless API to retrieve your packages/categories, build a basket for a user, and direct them to checkout - all from within your own frontend implementation (be that a website or in-game).

The Headless API can be used with [Tebex.js](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/overview)
 for a fully embedded checkout experience without the user ever leaving your own website.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/overview#headless-api-flow)

Headless API Flow


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Below is the expected flow your application should follow when utilizing the Headless API. For a list of all endpoints, please see the [Endpoints](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/endpoints)
 page.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/overview#packages-and-listings)

Packages & Listings

You can retrieve your store's listings in JSON format and display them however you wish:

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/overview#get-accounts-token-categories)

Gets all categories available in the webstore.

get

https://headless.tebex.io/api/accounts/{token}/categories

Gets all categories from a webstore. This does not include package information. To include package information, add `?includePackages=1` to the URL.

Path parameters

tokenstringRequired

The webstore identifier.

Example: `t66x-7cd928b1e9312709e6810edac6dc1fd1eefc57cb`

Responses

chevron-right

200

Successful response returns a list of category information.

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

get

/accounts/{token}/categories

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

Copy

    GET /api/accounts/{token}/categories HTTP/1.1
    Host: headless.tebex.io
    Accept: */*
    

Test it

200

Successful response returns a list of category information.

Copy

    {
      "data": [\
        {\
          "id": 2678660,\
          "name": "Test",\
          "slug": "text",\
          "parent": {},\
          "description": "text",\
          "packages": [\
            {\
              "id": 6276316,\
              "name": "test package 101",\
              "description": "<p>this is just a test. only a test. nothing more.</p>",\
              "image": null,\
              "type": "single",\
              "category": {\
                "id": 2678660,\
                "name": "Packages"\
              },\
              "base_price": 5,\
              "sales_tax": 0,\
              "total_price": 5,\
              "currency": "USD",\
              "discount": 0,\
              "disable_quantity": false,\
              "disable_gifting": false,\
              "expiration_date": null,\
              "created_at": "2024-05-21T18:09:17+00:00",\
              "updated_at": "2024-05-21T18:09:17+00:00"\
            }\
          ],\
          "order": 1,\
          "display_type": "list"\
        }\
      ]
    }

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/overview#get-accounts-token-categories-includepackages-1)

Gets a store's categories including all package information with them.

get

https://headless.tebex.io/api/accounts/{token}/categories?includePackages=1

Gets all categories from a webstore including packages.

Path parameters

tokenstringRequired

The webstore identifier.

Example: `t66x-7cd928b1e9312709e6810edac6dc1fd1eefc57cb`

Responses

chevron-right

200

Successful response returns a list of category information.

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

get

/accounts/{token}/categories?includePackages=1

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

Copy

    GET /api/accounts/{token}/categories?includePackages=1 HTTP/1.1
    Host: headless.tebex.io
    Accept: */*
    

Test it

200

Successful response returns a list of category information.

Copy

    {
      "data": [\
        {\
          "id": 2678660,\
          "name": "Test",\
          "slug": "text",\
          "parent": {},\
          "description": "text",\
          "packages": [\
            {\
              "id": 6276316,\
              "name": "test package 101",\
              "description": "<p>this is just a test. only a test. nothing more.</p>",\
              "image": null,\
              "type": "single",\
              "category": {\
                "id": 2678660,\
                "name": "Packages"\
              },\
              "base_price": 5,\
              "sales_tax": 0,\
              "total_price": 5,\
              "currency": "USD",\
              "discount": 0,\
              "disable_quantity": false,\
              "disable_gifting": false,\
              "expiration_date": null,\
              "created_at": "2024-05-21T18:09:17+00:00",\
              "updated_at": "2024-05-21T18:09:17+00:00"\
            }\
          ],\
          "order": 1,\
          "display_type": "list"\
        }\
      ]
    }

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/overview#get-accounts-token-categories-categoryid)

Gets information about a specific category

get

https://headless.tebex.io/api/accounts/{token}/categories/{categoryId}

Gets information about a category and returns the packages in that category.

Path parameters

tokenstringRequired

The webstore identifier.

Example: `t66x-7cd928b1e9312709e6810edac6dc1fd1eefc57cb`

categoryIdstringRequired

The ID of the category to fetch.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/overview#creating-baskets)

Creating Baskets

In order to purchase items, a basket must be created for the customer. Create a basket and allow the customer to login with their username or other OAuth login mechanism (e.g Steam or FiveM).

circle-info

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/overview#post-accounts-token-baskets)

Create a new basket

post

https://headless.tebex.io/api/accounts/{token}/baskets

Creates a new basket for use during checkout.

Path parameters

tokenstringRequired

The webstore identifier.

Example: `t66x-7cd928b1e9312709e6810edac6dc1fd1eefc57cb`

Body

application/jsonchevron-down

application/json

complete\_urlstringOptional

A URL the user can return to when checkout is completed.

Example: `https://example.tebex.io/thank-you`

cancel\_urlstringOptional

A URL the user can return to when cancelling checkout.

Example: `https://tebex.io/`

customobjectOptional

Custom data you wish to associate with the basket. This data will be included with webhook responses and GET requests associated with the Basket.

Example: `{"foo":"bar"}`

complete\_auto\_redirectbooleanOptional

True if the user should automatically be redirected to the relevant complete/cancel URL

Example: `true`

Responses

chevron-right

200

Successful response returns the basket information.

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

chevron-right

422

The provided webstore ID is invalid.

post

/accounts/{token}/baskets

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

Copy

    POST /api/accounts/{token}/baskets HTTP/1.1
    Host: headless.tebex.io
    Content-Type: application/json
    Accept: */*
    Content-Length: 139
    
    {
      "complete_url": "https://example.tebex.io/thank-you",
      "cancel_url": "https://tebex.io/",
      "custom": {
        "foo": "bar"
      },
      "complete_auto_redirect": true
    }

Test it

200

Successful response returns the basket information.

chevron-down

Copy

    {
      "data": {
        "id": 244127617,
        "ident": "1a-55fff4107740a1f40d844ff89607557f45bfafb3",
        "complete": false,
        "email": "support@tebex.io",
        "username": null,

          {\
            "coupon_code": "Academy10"\

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/overview#get-accounts-token-baskets-basketident-auth-returnurl-returnurl)

Get authentication links for a basket.

get

https://headless.tebex.io/api/accounts/{token}/baskets/{basketIdent}/auth?returnUrl={returnUrl}

Fetches a basket's auth URL.

Path parameters

tokenstringRequired

The webstore identifier.

Example: `t66x-7cd928b1e9312709e6810edac6dc1fd1eefc57cb`

basketIdentstringRequired

The basket identifier.

Example: `c00244-d2ac2e77418a55b25292a6bc7a719ad9c529ba2c`

returnUrlstringRequired

The URL you would like to redirect the user to after successful basket authentication.

Example: `https://example.tebex.io/`

Responses

chevron-right

200

Successful response returns the basket auth information.

application/json

Responseobject\[\]

chevron-right

The provided webstore ID or basket ID is invalid.

    Host: headless.tebex.io

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/overview#adding-and-removing-packages)

Adding and Removing Packages

You can add or remove packages programmatically to the created basket via the API as needed when the user interacts with your application.

        }
      }
    }

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/overview#post-accounts-token-baskets-basketident-giftcards-remove)

Remove a gift card from the basket.

post

https://headless.tebex.io/api/accounts/{token}/baskets/{basketIdent}/giftcards/remove

Removes a gift card from the basket.

Path parameters

tokenstringRequired

The webstore identifier.

Example: `t66x-7cd928b1e9312709e6810edac6dc1fd1eefc57cb`

basketIdentstringRequired

The basket identifier.

Example: `c00244-d2ac2e77418a55b25292a6bc7a719ad9c529ba2c`

Body

application/jsonchevron-down

application/json

card\_numberstringOptionalExample: `0127 0244 7210 1111`

Responses

chevron-right

200

Gift card removed successfully.

No content

chevron-right

422

The provided request is invalid. The error response will include detail as to which parameter failed validation.

post

/accounts/{token}/baskets/{basketIdent}/giftcards/remove

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

Copy

    POST /api/accounts/{token}/baskets/{basketIdent}/giftcards/remove HTTP/1.1
    Host: headless.tebex.io
    Content-Type: application/json
    Accept: */*
    Content-Length: 37
    
    {
      "card_number": "0127 0244 7210 1111"
    }

Gift card removed successfully.

# Why Tebex? | Creators

Running a game server or launching a game title takes time, resources, and dedication. Whether you're a community creator covering costs or a game studio building scalable revenue streams, **Tebex** gives you the tools to succeed, without technical overhead or operational complexity.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/master/why-tebex#why-creators-and-studios-choose-tebex)

**Why Creators & Studios Choose Tebex**

* * *

**Fast & Easy Store Setup**

Get up and running in minutes with an intuitive interface designed for game monetization. No coding required — just plug Tebex into your server or [integrate itarrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin)
 into your game with full control.

* * *

**Support for Popular Games & Custom Titles**

From Minecraft, Rust, and FiveM to custom server architectures and original IPs — Tebex supports a wide range of environments. Manage one or multiple projects from a single, centralized dashboard.

* * *

**Customizable Storefronts & Themes**

Match your brand or server aesthetic with flexible themes and layout tools. Build a storefront that feels like a seamless extension of your game or community.

* * *

**Multiple Payment Options, Global Reach**

Offer a seamless checkout experience with support for PayPal, credit cards, and local payment methods — all optimized for international buyers.

* * *

**Powerful Package & Subscription Management**

Sell one-time purchases, bundles, recurring subscriptions, in-game perks, DLCs, or early access — all with fine-tuned pricing, availability controls, and automated delivery.

* * *

**Run Discounts, Campaigns & Loyalty Programs**

Drive engagement with coupon codes, limited-time offers, seasonal sales, and loyalty rewards — all easily managed from your dashboard.

* * *

**Advanced Sales & Performance Analytics**

Gain full visibility into your revenue pipeline. Use in-depth sales reporting and real-time insights to make informed business decisions.

* * *

**Automated In-Game Fulfilment**

Orders are fulfilled instantly and securely. Tebex integrates directly with your game to deliver purchases without manual intervention, reducing support load and boosting player satisfaction.

* * *

**Merchant of Record (MoR) Model for Studios**

As your MoR, we handle global tax compliance (including VAT/GST), fraud protection, and chargeback disputes so you can focus on building games instead of processing payments.

* * *

**Enterprise-Ready with Full API Access**

Do you need deep integration? Our flexible API allows studios to connect Tebex with backend systems, custom account flows, and internal dashboards.

* * *

**Dedicated Support & Creator Community**

From individual creators to enterprise teams, we offer personalized support and access to a global network of developers, modders, and game studios sharing tools and success stories.

* * *

> Ready to power your game's economy?
> 
> > **Explore the** [**Creator Documentation**arrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators)
> >  Find in-depth guides on setting up your store, managing packages, customizing themes, and more.
> 
> > **Learn with** [**Tebex Academy**arrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@tebex/videos)
> >  **on YouTube** Subscribe for tutorials, best practices, and walkthroughs — hosted by our team of experts.
> 
> > **Need Help?** [**Contact Creator Support**arrow-up-right](https://www.tebex.io/support-creator)
> >  Our dedicated team is here to assist you with setup, optimization, and ongoing questions.
> 
> > **For Developers:** [**Start Here**arrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/)
> >  Access API references, integration guides, and advanced developer documentation.

[PreviousIntroducing Tebexchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators)
[NextPricing Overviewchevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/pricing-overview)

# Command Troubleshooting | Creators

If commands are not executing on your server you can try our troubleshooting guides below.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/command-troubleshooting#have-you-installed-the-plugin)

Have You Installed The Plugin?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Make sure that you have installed the plugin on your game server by following one of our helpful guides. We have guides available for each game and plugin we support, in addition, YouTube installation and set-up guides are becoming available for our platform - you may find these useful.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/command-troubleshooting#have-you-waited)

Have You Waited?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Commands on average execute instantly however sometimes it could take up to 5 minutes for the customer to receive their packages. Commands are configured by default to only execute once the customer is online - you can change this option by clicking on the settings button next to each command. The option is called "Require the customer to be online", (please note this setting is only available for stores using the plugin only).

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/command-troubleshooting#are-the-commands-setup-properly)

Are The Commands Setup Properly?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Double-check that all the commands in your packages have been entered properly and there are no formatting mistakes. Ensure that you also do not include a **"/"** before the command as this is not needed. If you want more information about commands you can view our [helpful guide](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/an-introduction-to-commands)
. You should also be very familiar with the wikis and commands of the other plugins and mods etc that you are using for your game server - Tebex is not able to assist you with how to use commands for your other plugins.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/command-troubleshooting#check-commands-via-your-console)

Check Commands Via Your Console


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On rare occasions, some commands you normally enter in-game might not work if they are executed via the console (the way commands are executed when setup with Tebex). A good test to see if the command works properly is to simply execute the command yourself in the console and see if it returns any errors. The major cause of commands not working via Tebex is that the actual command itself is not working properly or is incorrect.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/command-troubleshooting#is-the-tebex-plugin-throwing-an-error)

Is the Tebex Plugin Throwing An Error?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you can see errors in your console from a Tebex Store Plugin then please copy these errors and send them to our support team. You can email us via [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.tebex.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#6c1f191c1c031e182c18090e0914420503)
. If you are reporting a console error to Tebex, we will request further information from you including your plugin version, server version, and other additional info. We'll need this information to work out what the problem is and how to solve it!

[PreviousAn Introduction To Commandschevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/an-introduction-to-commands)
[NextResending Commandschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/resending-commands)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [Have You Installed The Plugin?](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/command-troubleshooting#have-you-installed-the-plugin)
    
*   [Have You Waited?](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/command-troubleshooting#have-you-waited)
    
*   [Are The Commands Setup Properly?](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/command-troubleshooting#are-the-commands-setup-properly)
    
*   [Check Commands Via Your Console](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/command-troubleshooting#check-commands-via-your-console)

# Support for Epic Game IDs | Creators

For some games (currently ARK:SE), there is an increasing need to support customers using the Epic Games launcher in addition to Steam or other solutions.

At the time of writing, Epic Games do not provide any solution to allow external parties to authenticate or verify account IDs for Epic Games accounts. They have announced 'Epic Online Services' which includes 'Epic Account Services' to do just this, but there has been no announcement as to when this will be made available for production, as currently it is in preview only.

We're aware that with the increases in popularity in ARK, driven by the recent 'free game' event, that game server owners need a solution as quickly as possible. As such, Tebex have developed an opt-in, temporary solution.

This temporary solution will allow customers to optionally provide an Epic ID when they add an item to their cart. If an Epic ID is provided, then this will be used in place of the standard `{id}` placeholder in commands.

Due to the limitations caused by Epic not providing a way for us to validate these IDs, there are certain limitations:

*   This is currently only available on the ARK:SE gametype
    
*   The customer will still need a Steam account to log-in to your store
    
*   Commands that require the player to be online **will not work** - all commands will need to be set as "Execute the command even if the customer is offline"
    
*   Because Epic Games do not provide a mechanism for doing so, we cannot validate that a provided Epic Games ID is valid, and thus we will pass through the ID exactly as passed to us with no additional checks performed
    

If you wish to enable Epic ID support, this can be done by going to the Game Servers section and enabling the 'Epic Game IDs' option.

Once enabled, when a customer adds an item to their cart, they will be asked if they wish to provide an Epic Games ID:

![](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1152203580-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LuI8PwvsHA79mTA-7bh%252F-MAklWr0nUsIrM5n883o%252F-MAkpJ7bPMtgWbrreTXP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1affca3e-ecac-4685-b8c1-4dca5f911806&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5f434891&sv=2)

If the customer doesn't provide a value here, then the `{id}` placeholder will remain, and will be replaced with their Steam64 ID as standard. Otherwise, if the customer provides an ID at this point, the `{id}` placeholder will be replaced with the value entered here.

[PreviousResending Commandschevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/resending-commands)

Last updated 4 years ago

# FAQs | Creators

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#table-of-contents)

Table of Contents

1.  Account & Subscription
    
2.  Store Configuration
    
3.  Store Operations
    
4.  Customer Payments
    
5.  Compliance & Eligibility
    
6.  Technical Issues
    
7.  Product Management
    
8.  Support & Legal
    
9.  Miscellaneous
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#id-1.-account-and-subscription)

1\. Account & Subscription

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#how-can-i-cancel-my-subscription)

How can I cancel my subscription?

Log in at [https://server.tebex.ioarrow-up-right](https://server.tebex.io/)
, go to **Plans**, and click **Downgrade** under the Starter Plan. You will not be charged again.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#can-i-pay-without-a-subscription)

Can I pay without a subscription?

Yes. On the **Plus Plan**, you can pre-pay for a fixed period. Refunds are not available for unused time.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#will-i-be-charged-automatically-after-the-free-trial)

Will I be charged automatically after the free trial?

No, you are downgraded to the free **Starter Plan** unless you upgrade manually.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#how-do-i-cancel-my-free-trial)

How do I cancel my free trial?

This is not possible. Free trials run their full duration.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#my-subscription-payment-failed.-what-should-i-do)

My subscription payment failed. What should I do?

Tebex retries payment up to 3 times. If all fail, your plan will be downgraded. You can resubscribe manually.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#can-i-get-a-discount)

Can I get a discount?

Yes, if you pre-pay in bulk. You can save up to 20%. No refunds are given for prepaid time.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#how-do-i-rename-my-store)

How do I rename my store?

Visit the **Webstore** section in your dashboard: https://server.tebex.io/webstore

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#are-subscription-plans-account-wide)

Are subscription plans account-wide?

No, they are store-specific.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#how-can-i-change-my-account-details)

How can I change my account details?

Go to Security Settings. For wallet details, contact Creator Support.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#id-2.-store-configuration)

2\. Store Configuration

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#can-i-change-my-store-type-after-setup)

Can I change my store type after setup?

Generally, no. If necessary, contact support to transfer any remaining subscription time.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#can-i-export-my-entire-store)

Can I export my entire store?

No, full exports are not supported.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#are-premium-templates-account-wide)

Are Premium Templates account-wide?

No, they are store-specific and non-transferable.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#can-i-use-buycraft-as-my-subdomain)

Can I use Buycraft as my subdomain?

No. Buycraft has been rebranded to Tebex.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#id-3.-store-operations)

3\. Store Operations

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#how-do-i-write-commands)

How do I write commands?

Refer to the official guide. Tebex does not provide help writing game-specific commands.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#can-i-delete-pending-commands)

Can I delete pending commands?

No, but you can enable automatic expiry intervals at [Game Serversarrow-up-right](https://server.tebex.io/game-servers)
.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#where-can-i-edit-my-terms-and-conditions)

Where can I edit my terms and conditions?

Tebex Checkout stores cannot modify default T&Cs. Create a custom page for additional terms.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#can-i-copy-a-template)

Can I copy a template?

Yes. Go to [Templatesarrow-up-right](https://server.tebex.io/templates/create)
 and select a base to start editing.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#can-i-add-team-accounts)

Can I add team accounts?

Yes. No hard limit. Available on **Plus (Checkout)** or **Ultimate (Legacy)** plans.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#what-plugins-are-shown-on-the-download-page)

What plugins are shown on the download page?

Only plugins relevant to your selected store type.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#id-4.-customer-payments)

4\. Customer Payments

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#how-can-i-test-product-commands)

How can I test product commands?

Create a **manual payment**—never test with real money. Instructions here.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#how-can-a-customer-cancel-their-subscription)

How can a customer cancel their subscription?

Through the cancellation link in the subscription email or via [self-servicearrow-up-right](https://checkout.tebex.io/payment-history/)
.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#where-can-my-customer-view-their-purchase-history)

Where can my customer view their purchase history?

Via the [self-service toolarrow-up-right](https://checkout.tebex.io/payment-history/)
.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#what-happens-if-i-input-the-wrong-paypal-email)

What happens if I input the wrong PayPal email?

If invalid, PayPal will bounce it back in 30 days. If valid, the funds are sent and Tebex cannot recover them.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#id-5.-compliance-and-eligibility)

5\. Compliance & Eligibility

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#how-old-must-i-be-to-open-a-store)

How old must I be to open a store?

You must have full legal capacity (usually 18+). Otherwise, a parent/guardian must register on your behalf.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#is-my-store-eligible-for-the-affiliate-program)

Is my store eligible for the affiliate program?

Only for server hosts or platforms. Not applicable to individual game servers.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#can-tebex-give-legal-or-tax-advice)

Can Tebex give legal or tax advice?

No. You must consult a professional locally.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#id-6.-technical-issues)

6\. Technical Issues

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#discord-bot-isnt-executing-commands)

Discord bot isn’t executing commands.

Ensure it has the **highest role** in your server.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#i-lost-access-to-my-2fa-email-phone)

I lost access to my 2FA email/phone.

Contact [\[email protected\]](https://docs.tebex.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#console-spam-on-minecraft-java)

Console spam on Minecraft Java?

Set `verbose = false` in your Tebex config file.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#invalid-purchase-type-error)

Invalid Purchase Type error?

Ensure you're using the correct package/product settings and supported payment type.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#id-7.-product-management)

7\. Product Management

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#how-can-i-sell-scripts-mods-for-fivem)

How can I sell scripts/mods for FiveM?

Use the **FiveM store type** only. Read Cfx.re rules and the delivery guide.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#can-i-change-store-type-later)

Can I change store type later?

Usually not. Double-check your setup before creation.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#how-do-i-enable-upgrades)

How do I enable upgrades?

Use **Cumulative Packages** in your category settings.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#why-cant-my-package-be-gifted)

Why can’t my package be gifted?

Subscriptions cannot be gifted.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#id-8.-support-and-legal)

8\. Support & Legal

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#how-will-customer-service-be-handled)

How will customer service be handled?

Tebex may ask you to respond to customer inquiries. Use your **Support Email** for visibility. Tebex may step in if no response is provided.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#how-do-i-report-a-store-for-misconduct-or-stolen-content)

How do I report a store for misconduct or stolen content?

Send evidence or a completed **DMCA form** to [\[email protected\]](https://docs.tebex.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#can-tebex-cancel-subscriptions-for-customers)

Can Tebex cancel subscriptions for customers?

Yes, for Checkout stores only. Direct customers to the contact form.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#id-9.-miscellaneous)

9\. Miscellaneous

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#how-do-i-suggest-a-feature)

How do I suggest a feature?

Send ideas via feedback channels. Not all will be implemented, but all are considered.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#how-can-i-use-tebex-with-geyser)

How can I use Tebex with Geyser?

Supported on **Minecraft Offline** store types only. Use `{username}` instead of UUID.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#i-want-to-delete-manual-payments)

I want to delete manual payments.

Only **manual payments** can be deleted. Real customer transactions cannot.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq#why-does-pricing-vary-per-customer)

Why does pricing vary per customer?

VAT and local taxes are applied depending on the user’s location, as required by law.

# Getting Started | Developers

Welcome to your journey of launching your first project with Tebex! This guide will walk you through the essential steps to create, set up, and launch your store, ensuring a seamless experience for your customers. From building your first project in the creator panel to implementing automatic product delivery, we'll cover everything you need to know to get started.

1

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/getting-started#create-a-project)

Create a project

Head over to the [creator panelarrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/)
 and kick things off by creating your first project.

2

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/getting-started#setup-your-store-or-integrate-our-apis)

Setup your store or integrate our APIs

Check out the docs for the [integration method](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/integration-methods)
 you’re going with. If needed, build the APIs into your website or game.

3

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/getting-started#create-your-packages)

Create your packages

If your integration method requires it, [create the packagesarrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/packages)
 your customers can buy.

4

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/getting-started#implement-product-delivery)

Implement product delivery

Make sure your customers get their packages right away after they’ve made a purchase. For game studios, [webhooks](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/webhooks/overview)
 or license keys (like Steam keys) are the way to go. If you’re monetizing a game server, don’t forget to check out our [official plugins](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/game-server-api/overview)
 for that.

5

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/getting-started#make-a-test-payment)

Make a test payment

Before going live, give everything a test run by going through the checkout process using the test payment method. Don’t worry, no real money needed here!

6

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/getting-started#submit-for-review)

Submit for review

Ready to roll? Submit your project for review by our Content & Safety team. We’ll give it a quick check, and if everything looks good, you’ll be ready to launch within a day.

7

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/getting-started#go-live)

Go live

Once you’re approved, you’re all set to go live and start making money from your game! Plus, with us as your Merchant of Record, you’ll get access to worldwide payment methods, tax handling, and fraud protection. Nice! 😎🎉

[PreviousWelcomechevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/developers)
[NextIntegration Methodschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/integration-methods)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Tebex Legends | Creators

![](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1152203580-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LuI8PwvsHA79mTA-7bh%252Fuploads%252FLQlzIGg3iC2mYO1vlplt%252FScreenshot%25202025-01-14%2520at%25208.24.12%25E2%2580%25AFAM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De1459ba0-2d7a-4bd2-be16-e601e7ae652f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a7b7b7c7&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-legends#what-is-the-tebex-legends-program)

What is the Tebex Legends Program?


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Tebex Legends program is all about celebrating success, efforts, and the achievements you have made along the way. Stores that reach certain revenue milestones in the coming year will be opted into the program and sent some exciting, tangible rewards to acknowledge and track your tremendous progress with us.

Think of it as our way of saying "thank you" for being a cornerstone of the Tebex community.

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-legends#heres-how-it-works)

Here’s How It Works:


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-legends#no-sign-up-needed)

**No sign-up needed**

You don’t need to apply or fill out forms. Once your store hits a milestone, we’ll contact you directly (make sure you check your “Master Email” for emails from our team regarding Tebex Legends).

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-legends#revenue-from-fiscal-year-only)

**Revenue from fiscal year only:**

Only revenue generated between January 1 and December 31st of each fiscal year will count.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-legends#milestones-are-store-project-specific)

**Milestones are store/project-specific**.


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you own multiple stores, each is eligible to qualify individually, and achievements are tracked separately per store.

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-legends#tebex-legends-frequently-asked-questions)

Tebex Legends Frequently Asked Questions


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

chevron-rightWhen will I receive 2026 Milestone emails/awards?[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-legends#when-will-i-receive-2026-milestone-emails-awards)

We're using January 2026 as a grace period for Legends 2025, and you won't receive any emails regarding milestones for Legends 2026 until February 1st 2026. _**It should also be noted that 2025 awards can no longer be redeemed after February 1st 2026.**_

chevron-rightWhen will I receive an email for a milestone?[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-legends#when-will-i-receive-an-email-for-a-milestone)

Due to the many moving parts in payment processing, it may take 1 to 2 working weeks to actually receive the email for the corresponding award you have achieved.

chevron-rightI have received a notice that I have to pay a customs fee for the award to be delivered?[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-legends#i-have-received-a-notice-that-i-have-to-pay-a-customs-fee-for-the-award-to-be-delivered)

Unfortunately, we can't control any fees incurred, so if you wish to receive the award, you'll need to cover the associated costs.

If you don't want to pay for it, then they'll destroy the award, and you won't have to worry about it.

chevron-rightI’ve made this much revenue previously via Tebex! Where’s my stuff?[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-legends#ive-made-this-much-revenue-previously-via-tebex-wheres-my-stuff)

The Legends Programme is based on revenue effective from January 1, 2025. Since this is an annual program, previous history is not considered or calculated.

chevron-rightWhat Milestones are there? [hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-legends#what-milestones-are-there)

All Milestones are available [herearrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~/revisions/LL64jrXQqsxUaXjtvAGc/tebex-legends/tebex-legends-milestones)
.

chevron-rightI have more than one store that has reached this threshold. How does that work?[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-legends#i-have-more-than-one-store-that-has-reached-this-threshold.-how-does-that-work)

Milestones are store/project-specific. If you own multiple stores/projects, each is eligible to qualify individually, and achievements are tracked separately per store.

chevron-rightCan I receive multiple awards for the same milestone my store reached?[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-legends#can-i-receive-multiple-awards-for-the-same-milestone-my-store-reached)

1 Award is given per store, per milestone reached. _Duplicate awards for a store are not available._ Awards are manufactured and shipped at different times, so awards may arrive at different times/separately.

chevron-rightHow and when will I receive or expect to receive my physical award(s)?[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-legends#how-and-when-will-i-receive-or-expect-to-receive-my-physical-award-s)

In 4-6 weeks after reaching any milestones, Tebex will email your [**Primary Project Owner's email** arrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/team)
with the subject related to Tebex Legend from [\[email protected\]](https://docs.tebex.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
! This email contains detailed information regarding the reward and milestone your store has reached.

chevron-rightSomething’s wrong with my award (It’s damaged, has incorrect details, is defective) or didn’t arrive - help![hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-legends#somethings-wrong-with-my-award-its-damaged-has-incorrect-details-is-defective-or-didnt-arrive-help)

Please reach out by replying to the email confirming your reward details, and include a summary of what happened and what’s wrong to help you.

chevron-rightI gave the wrong address or moved to a different location before it arrived; how do I redirect the reward?[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-legends#i-gave-the-wrong-address-or-moved-to-a-different-location-before-it-arrived-how-do-i-redirect-the-re)

The address you provide in the email you receive is the one where we will ship your reward. Please notify us via the email provided as soon as possible if there are any changes. **PLEASE NOTE:** We cannot guarantee that the packages will be rerouted if they have already been shipped. If we can change the address on time, you may incur additional charges.

chevron-rightWhich currency is used to calculate the milestones?[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-legends#which-currency-is-used-to-calculate-the-milestones)

All milestone calculations are measured in US Dollars (USD).

chevron-rightHow are milestones calculated?[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-legends#how-are-milestones-calculated)

Milestone calculation **excludes free and manual payments**, **excludes sales tax**, but **includes fees from the payment**. Payments in **non-USD currencies are converted to USD before calculating**.

* * *

circle-info

For additional questions, feel free to email [\[email protected\]](https://docs.tebex.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
 to learn more!

[PreviousFAQschevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq)
[NextTebex Legends Milestoneschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-legends/tebex-legends-milestones)

# Resending Commands | Creators

Sometimes its useful to resend commands once they've already been executed on your game server. This might be due to a data loss or a reset of your game server. We've tried to make it easy for you to do this.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/resending-commands#resend-commands-for-a-single-payment)

Resend Commands For A Single Payment


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you would like to resend the commands for just a single payment, go to the payment you want to resend and scroll to the commands section. Click the **Resend Commands** button and follow the instructions given on that page.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/resending-commands#resending-commands-for-multiple-payments)

Resending Commands For Multiple Payments


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you would like to resend commands for all (or some of) your payments you can do so by following these steps.

1.  Go to **Game Servers** > **Resend Commands**.
    
2.  Click **Resend Commands**.
    
3.  Enter the following options:
    

**Options**

1.  **Start Date** - Only resend commands in payments after this date.
    
2.  **End Date** - Only resend commands in payments before this date.
    
3.  **Payment Statuses** - Only resend commands which have these selected statuses.
    
4.  **Resend Type** \- Additional filter options which allow you to only resend commands for packages which match a certain criteria.
    

Once you have entered the options above, click resend. The commands will now be added to a queue and we will start to resend the commands which match your filters.

circle-info

Please avoid sending large volume of commands in one go as this can occasionally result in the commands not being fully resent.

[PreviousCommand Troubleshootingchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/command-troubleshooting)
[NextSupport for Epic Game IDschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/support-for-epic-game-ids)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [Resend Commands For A Single Payment](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/resending-commands#resend-commands-for-a-single-payment)
    
*   [Resending Commands For Multiple Payments](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/resending-commands#resending-commands-for-multiple-payments)

# An Introduction To Commands | Creators

Manage in-game rewards automatically with Tebex commands. This guide explains how commands work, how to customize them with variables, and how to configure different command types across supported games.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/an-introduction-to-commands#table-of-contents)

Table of Contents

*   How Do Commands Work?
    
*   Finding Commands
    
*   Variables in Commands
    
    *   Universal Variables
        
    *   Game-Specific Variables
        
    
*   Command Types
    
    *   Initial Commands
        
    *   Expiry Commands
        
    *   Renewal Commands
        
    *   Chargeback Commands
        
    *   Refund Commands
        
    
*   Global Commands
    
*   Best Practices
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/an-introduction-to-commands#how-do-commands-work)

How Do Commands Work?

Commands are the core automation method in Tebex. When a customer makes a purchase, Tebex runs pre-defined commands through your plugin or server console to deliver rewards.

For example:

In the above Minecraft command, `{name}` is a variable that automatically populates with the customer's in-game username.

Commands are typically executed 1–3 minutes after the payment is confirmed.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/an-introduction-to-commands#finding-commands)

Finding Commands

Tebex does not maintain a command database due to the variety of games and mods supported. You should consult:

*   Game-specific wikis (e.g., Minecraft, Garry’s Mod)
    
*   Mod/plugin documentation
    
*   Developer forums for third-party scripts
    

> 📌 Always test your commands using Tebex's manual payment feature—**do not make real purchases for testing.**

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/an-introduction-to-commands#variables-in-commands)

Variables in Commands

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/an-introduction-to-commands#universal-variables)

Universal Variables

These can be used in all supported game servers:

Variable

Description

`{id}`

Game-specific primary ID (Steam64, Xbox XUID, UUID, etc.)

`{username}`

Username used during login or purchase

`{transaction}`

Unique transaction ID

`{server}`

Server name

`{price}`

Purchase amount

`{currency}`

Currency used in purchase

`{time}` / `{date}`

Time and date of purchase

`{email}`

Customer’s email address

`{ip}`

Customer’s IP address

`{packageId}` / `{packageName}`

Package identifier and name

`{packagePrice}` / `{packageExpiry}`

Price and expiration period

`{purchaserName}` / `{purchaserUuid}`

Details for gift givers

`{purchaseQuantity}`

Quantity of items purchased

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/an-introduction-to-commands#game-specific-variables)

Game-Specific Variables

**Minecraft: Java Edition**

*   `{name}` — Player username (legacy)
    
*   `{uuid}` — Mojang UUID (legacy)
    

**Garry’s Mod**

*   `{steamid}` — Old Steam ID format
    

**Ark: Survival Evolved**

*   `{ue4id}` — Unreal Engine 4 user ID
    

**FiveM**

*   `{hexid}` — Hexadecimal Steam ID (e.g., steam:110000...) for online commands
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/an-introduction-to-commands#command-types)

Command Types

Tebex allows different command types depending on the payment event lifecycle.

Initial Commands

Executed once payment is confirmed. Example:

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/an-introduction-to-commands#expiry-commands)

Expiry Commands

Executed after the package expires. Useful for temporary items/ranks.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/an-introduction-to-commands#renewal-commands)

Renewal Commands

Executed upon subscription renewal.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/an-introduction-to-commands#chargeback-commands)

Chargeback Commands

Executed when a chargeback is triggered.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/an-introduction-to-commands#refund-commands)

Refund Commands

Executed after a manual refund.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/an-introduction-to-commands#global-commands)

Global Commands

Global commands apply across all packages in your store.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/an-introduction-to-commands#setup-steps)

Setup Steps:

1.  Navigate to **Game Servers > Global Commands** in your control panel.
    
2.  Add your desired command using variables.
    
3.  Click **Update**.
    

> These commands execute per payment—not per package.

> Global commands execute across **all servers**, even if restricted by server tag.

> If a payment’s commands are resent, global commands are re-executed too.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/an-introduction-to-commands#best-practices)

Best Practices

*   **Use variables** instead of hardcoded usernames or IDs.
    
*   **Avoid testing with real money**—use Tebex’s manual payment tool.
    
*   **Group commands** logically per event type for clarity.
    
*   **Document special behavior** in package notes or FAQs.
    
*   **Test on staging server** before going live.
    

* * *

Need help writing commands? Refer to your specific game server’s mod/plugin documentation.

> Tebex does not provide 1:1 assistance writing commands.

# Overwolf Apps | Developers

The Overwolf Subscriptions API enables developers to seamlessly integrate subscription-based monetization into their Overwolf apps using a Tebex Store. This integration provides a complete subscription management system - removing the need to handle payment processing, track subscription statuses, or build complex server-side infrastructure.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/overwolf-apps#get-started-with-overwolf-app-monetization)

Get Started with Overwolf App Monetization

Before implementing subscriptions, review Overwolf’s documentation to understand the available monetization options and how to incorporate them into your app.

**Learn more:** [Overwolf App Monetization Guidearrow-up-right](https://dev.overwolf.com/ow-native/monetization/implementation/)

This guide covers:

*   Supported monetization models in Overwolf
    
*   How Tebex integrates into the Overwolf ecosystem
    
*   Steps for setting up and linking your Tebex Store
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/overwolf-apps#explore-the-overwolf-subscriptions-api-reference)

Explore the Overwolf Subscriptions API Reference

The Overwolf Subscriptions API provides all the endpoints and methods you’ll need to manage your users’ subscriptions through Tebex. It includes details on authentication, subscription lifecycle management, and user entitlement verification.

**View the full API documentation:** [Overwolf Subscriptions API Referencearrow-up-right](https://dev.overwolf.com/ow-native/reference/subscriptions-api)

Use this reference to:

*   Fetch active subscriptions for users
    
*   Verify subscription status within your app
    
*   Manage user access based on entitlement data
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/overwolf-apps#review-the-example-app)

Review the Example App

To see a working implementation, Overwolf provides an example application demonstrating how to use the Tebex Subscriptions API in a sample application.

**Explore the sample app on GitHub:** [Tebex Subscriptions Example Apparrow-up-right](https://github.com/overwolf/tebex-subs-sample)

This repository includes:

*   End-to-end integration examples
    
*   Code samples for handling subscription data
    
*   Reference architecture for production deployments
