# Integration Methods | Developers

Tebex offers multiple integration options tailored to meet different business needs, each equipped with unique features for specific use cases.

There are three integration methods available, as highlighted below. Each method varies in complexity, with the Webstore Builder being the easiest to get started with.

[](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/overview)

**Webstore Builder** _Easiest_

✅ Checkout

✅ Package Management

✅ Hosted Webstore [Webstore Builder Docs](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/overview)

[](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/overview)

**Headless API** _Complex_

✅ Checkout

✅ Package Management

~\* Hosted Webstore~ [Headless API Doc](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/overview)
[s](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/overview)

[](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview)

**Checkout API** _Advanced_

✅ Checkout

~\* Package Management~

~\* Hosted Webstore~ [Checkout API Docs](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview)

**Checkout**: Maximize revenue by utilizing Tebex’s global Merchant of Record platform. With over 100 payment methods, Tebex handles the entire checkout process, offering chargeback protection, fraud monitoring, 14-day payouts, and international sales tax coverage.

**Package Management**: Effortlessly set up and manage packages for sale on your project through the creator panel. You can organize packages into categories and easily define details such as names, descriptions, pricing, and images. You're also able to invite other team members to manage these too.

**Hosted Webstore**: Tebex provides a customizable webstore that allows you to start selling in minutes. This enables you to focus on your business, while we handle the hosting infrastructure & technical requirements for you.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/integration-methods#which-integration-method-is-best-for-me)

Which integration method is best for me?

Take a look at the example scenarios below to get a better understanding of which integration method is best for you. Whatever you choose, all of our integration methods come with access to over 100 payment methods, international sales tax coverage, fraud protection, [webhooks](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/webhooks/overview)
, and seamless inline checkout through [Tebex.js](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/overview)
.

chevron-rightI want to sell packages via a pre-built webstore that's hosted for me[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/integration-methods#i-want-to-sell-packages-via-a-pre-built-webstore-thats-hosted-for-me)

If you're looking for a pre-built, hosted webstore, we recommend using the Tebex [Webstore Builder](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/overview)
. This tool offers comprehensive package management through the Tebex creator panel, a fully customizable webstore displaying all your available packages, and a built-in add-to-cart feature. Webstores are seamlessly integrated with [Tebex.js](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/overview)
, our inline checkout solution. To see an example of a webstore created with the Webstore Builder, visit [example.tebex.ioarrow-up-right](https://example.tebex.io/)
.

chevron-rightI want to sell packages from my own website or in-game[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/integration-methods#i-want-to-sell-packages-from-my-own-website-or-in-game)

If you want to sell packages directly through your own website or in-game, while managing package creation, updates, and configuration via Tebex, the [Headless API](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/overview)
 is the ideal solution. By integrating the Headless API with [Tebex.js](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/overview)
, you can offer a seamless checkout experience, allowing customers to make purchases without leaving your site.

chevron-rightI want to sell packages that are dynamic in nature[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/integration-methods#i-want-to-sell-packages-that-are-dynamic-in-nature)

If your packages require a high level of customization for each customer and cannot be created within the Tebex creator panel, the Checkout API is the ideal solution. For example, this could apply to packages with varying names, descriptions, pricing, or images tailored to individual customers. By integrating the Checkout API with [Tebex.js](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/overview)
, you can provide a smooth purchasing experience, allowing customers to complete transactions without leaving your website.

chevron-rightI want to sell hundreds or thousands of packages through my own backend system[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/integration-methods#i-want-to-sell-hundreds-or-thousands-of-packages-through-my-own-backend-system)

If you manage a large volume of packages that would be impractical to create manually in the Tebex creator panel, or if your package offerings update based on your internal inventory system, the [Checkout API](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview)
 is the optimal solution. By integrating the Checkout API with [Tebex.js](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/overview)
, you can offer a seamless purchasing experience, allowing customers to complete transactions without leaving your website.

chevron-rightI want to sell physical goods or launch a marketplace[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/integration-methods#i-want-to-sell-physical-goods-or-launch-a-marketplace)

Tebex cannot support projects that aim to sell physical goods or provide marketplace services. If you are looking to pursue either of these options, we regret to inform you that we cannot collaborate in this capacity, and you will need to seek a payment partner elsewhere.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/integration-methods#lets-begin)

Let's begin!

Now that you've chosen your integration method, you can begin by exploring the relevant documentation:

*   Learn how to design your own store using the [**Webstore Builder**](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/overview)
    .
    
*   Sell packages directly from your website or in-game with the [**Headless API**](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/overview)
    .
    
*   For more complex integrations, get started with the [**Checkout API**](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview)
    .
    

[PreviousGetting Startedchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/getting-started)
[NextOverwolf Appschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/overwolf-apps)

# Initial Setup Guide | Creators

Welcome to Tebex. Whether you're launching a monetized game server or integrating Tebex into a studio-grade production pipeline, this section walks you through the essential steps to configure your store, verify your identity, and prepare for your first sale.

Tebex acts as your **Merchant of Record**, meaning we handle payment processing, tax compliance, and dispute resolution on your behalf. To maintain legal, operational, and security standards for all users, we require that each store completes a short review and identity verification process.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide#tebex-creator-agreement)

Several steps in this section refer to terms outlined in our [Creator Agreementarrow-up-right](https://www.tebex.io/terms-creator-agreement)
. We recommend reviewing it in full before completing your store setup.

# Developer Plan | Developers

If you're a template developer, you're entitled to receive free Tebex Plus to enable you to freely develop templates for your clients. Stores that receive our developer plan won't be able to transact real payments on their store.

You're also eligible to gain access to the certified Tebex designers club. You'll get insider help guides, access to a private community of other elite designers, feedback sessions with the Tebex product team, and also BETA features that are not yet available to others.

If you'd like to apply to become a Tebex Certified Designer, [please apply herearrow-up-right](https://forms.monday.com/forms/fce1c5555703d90861656cd5571d5543?r=use1)

# Assets | Developers

Assets allow you to upload your own CSS, Javascript, Images or Twig files to your template, which you can later reference in your files.

To create an asset, first upload it from within the template editor. Once you have uploaded the asset, you can retrieve the public URL of the asset by using the`asset()` function. This function will return the full URL of the asset hosted on our global CDN.

For example, you could upload `scripts.js` as an asset, and then include it in your template:

Copy

    <script defer src="{{ asset('scripts.js') }}"></script>

You're also able to create TWIG files that you can later reference in your template. For example, you could create an asset called `navigation.twig`, and then include it using the Twig include tag:

Copy

    {% include "navigation.twig" %}

This allows you to create code that is easily reusable across multiple locations in your template.

[Previousmodule.topdonator.htmlchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/sidebar-modules/module.topdonator.html)
[NextSchemachevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/schema)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Directing to Checkout | Developers

When the user is ready to checkout, you can fetch the current basket and direct the user to its `links.checkout` URL. Here, the user will enter their payment information and complete checkout.

If you'd like the user to stay on your site during checkout, use [Tebex.js](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/overview)
 alongside the Headless API.

circle-exclamation

For most stores, authorizing the user against the basket is required before checkout. You can do this by directing the user to the appropriate link provided by the **/baskets/auth** endpoint. [Read more here](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/creating-a-basket)
.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/directing-to-checkout#get-accounts-token-baskets-basketident)

Fetch a basket from a webstore by its identifier

get

https://headless.tebex.io/api/accounts/{token}/baskets/{basketIdent}

Gets a basket associated with the provided identifier.

Path parameters

tokenstringRequired

The webstore identifier.

Example: `t66x-7cd928b1e9312709e6810edac6dc1fd1eefc57cb`

basketIdentstringRequired

The basket identifier.

Example: `c00244-d2ac2e77418a55b25292a6bc7a719ad9c529ba2c`

Responses

chevron-right

200

Successful response returns the basket information.

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

get

/accounts/{token}/baskets/{basketIdent}

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

Test it

200

Successful response returns the basket information.

[PreviousApplying Discounts / Creator Codeschevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/applying-discounts-creator-codes)
[NextTierschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/tiers)

    GET /api/accounts/{token}/baskets/{basketIdent} HTTP/1.1
    Host: headless.tebex.io
    Accept: */*

# Overview | Developers

The Webstore Builder enables you to fully customise the design of your store using templates & themes, providing your customers with a seamless transition from your existing website when they're making a purchase.

If you haven't already done so, we recommend having a read of our [quick start guide](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/getting-started)
 before continuing.

With the webstore builder, you can:

1.  Use templates to change the HTML structure of each page and implement conditional logic via the [TWIG templating engine](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/twig)
    .
    
2.  Upload custom CSS, Javascript and images via [Assets](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/assets)
    .
    
3.  If you're a template designer, you can offer your customers the ability to customise their templates via [Config Schema](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/schema)
    , and you're also eligible for free Plus via our [Developer Plan](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/developer-plan)
    .
    

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/overview#examples)

# Footer | Developers

Upon creating your store you may notice the footer at the bottom of your store stating that it is powered by Tebex and that we are the reseller & merchant of record.

Hiding the footer on your webstore will void our terms and conditions and will result in us having to disable your store from the public.

As a merchant of record platform we are under strict requirements by the card networks, such as Visa & Mastercard, to ensure customers understand which company they are purchasing from. You are authorising Tebex to operate a webstore on your behalf and sell content that we license from you, thus we need to let customers know about this as clearly as possible.

We don't place the footer for our own marketing/branding benefit - we simply have to do it to be able to provide you with all the benefits you receive as us being the Merchant Of Record, such as:

1.  100 payment method integrations
    
2.  Sales tax collection and remittance worldwide
    
3.  Fraud protection & our chargeback guarantee
    
4.  Easy to integrate product delivery for your game studio & server
    

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/footer#styling-the-footer-to-match-your-own-brand)

Styling the footer to match your own brand


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The colour scheme of the footer by default matches your Tebex Checkout theme. You're able to select between Dark or Light mode by viewing your Checkout settings within the creator panel.

The footer also listens to the following CSS variables which you can define in your template/theme, providing you with further customisation ability:

Variable

\--tebex-legal-footer-background-color

\--tebex-legal-footer-text-color

\--tebex-legal-footer-border-color

\--tebex-legal-footer-max-width

\--tebex-legal-footer-logo-color

An example of setting the CSS variables can be seen below, which you could place in your templates CSS file:

[PreviousDeveloper Planchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/developer-plan)
[NextGuideschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/guides)

Last updated 1 year ago

Copy

    :root {
      --tebex-legal-footer-background-color: #fcba03;
      --tebex-legal-footer-text-color: #4c00ff;
    }

# Headers & Authentication | Developers

If you are creating a basket **on your backend server**, you will need to provide us the IP address of the customer through the [Create a Basket endpoint.arrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/creating-a-basket)
 If you are creating a basket from the user's browser, we will automatically determine the IP from the requesting device.

triangle-exclamation

**Currently we are unable to support IPv6 addresses** being provided in the ip\_address property. While we work on enabling IPv6 support, please provide an IPv4 address for the customer.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/headers-and-authentication#authorization)

Authorization


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you’re being asked for authentication; you'll need to use HTTP BASIC with the following details:

Username **(Public Token)**

Your Public Token (you can get this from [https://creator.tebex.io/developers/api-keysarrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/developers/api-keys)
)

Password **(Private Key)**

Your Private Key (you can get this from [https://creator.tebex.io/developers/api-keysarrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/developers/api-keys)
)

circle-exclamation

Your store's Private Key should **never** be shared publicly. If your key is ever compromised, it can be reset on the API Keys page linked in the table above.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/headers-and-authentication#content-type)

Content Type


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

All requests use `application/json` as the `Content-Type`. Ensure this is set with all requests to our Headless API.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/headers-and-authentication#example-of-an-authenticated-create-basket-request)

Example of an authenticated [create basketarrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/creating-a-basket)
 request


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    const url = "https://headless.tebex.io/api/accounts/{token}/baskets";
    
    const headers = new Headers();
    headers.append('Authorization', 'Basic ' + btoa(username + ':' + password));
    headers.append('Content-Type', 'application/json');
    
    const body = {
     "complete_url": "https://example.tebex.io/thank-you",
     "cancel_url": "https://tebex.io/",
     "custom": {
      "foo": "bar"
     },
     "complete_auto_redirect": true,
     "username": "TebexDev"
    };
    
    const options = {
     method: 'POST',
     headers: headers,
     body: JSON.stringify(body)
    };
    
    const response = await fetch(url, options);

[PreviousOverviewchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/overview)
[NextGetting Your Listingschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/getting-your-listings)

Last updated 2 months ago

*   [Authorization](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/headers-and-authentication#authorization)
    
*   [Content Type](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/headers-and-authentication#content-type)
    
*   [Example of an authenticated create basket request](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/headers-and-authentication#example-of-an-authenticated-create-basket-request)

# Start the Checkout Process | Developers

When you are ready to redirect the customer to checkout, there are two ways of beginning the checkout experience:

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/start-the-checkout-process#id-1.-embedded-via-tebex.js)

1\. Embedded - via Tebex.js


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you'd like the customer to remain on your website to complete their purchase, you're able to integrate **Tebex.js**, which is our embeddable checkout experience.

Head over to the [Tebex.js documentation](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/overview)
 to get started.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/start-the-checkout-process#id-2.-external-via-redirect)

2\. External - via Redirect


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You may also redirect the customer to an external checkout window using the following URL:

`https://pay.tebex.io/{ident}`

This is the same as the `links.checkout` value in a Basket API response. Where `{ident}` is the ident value returned when creating the basket.

circle-exclamation

When a customer starts their payment (is redirected to PayPal, provides their card details etc), a copy of the basket at that point in time is converted to a pending payment.

Any changes made to the basket after this point **will not be reflected** unless the checkout process is re-started.

[PreviousHeaders and Authenticationchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/headers-and-authentication)
[NextCheckout Webhookschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/checkout-webhooks)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [1\. Embedded - via Tebex.js](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/start-the-checkout-process#id-1.-embedded-via-tebex.js)
    
*   [2\. External - via Redirect](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/start-the-checkout-process#id-2.-external-via-redirect)

# Authentication | Developers

To access the Plugin API, all requests need to be authenticated via a Game Server secret key which is found in the [game servers sectionarrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/game-servers)
 of your creator panel.

Supply the secret key by setting the `X-Tebex-Secret` header in all requests to the API.

circle-info

Please note that all requests to the API must be sent via HTTPS.

[PreviousOverviewchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/game-server-api/overview)
[NextError Handlingchevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/game-server-api/error-handling)

Last updated 2 years ago

---

# Checkout Webhooks | Developers

Your server can receive Webhooks from Tebex after events occur on our platform (successful payment, refunds, etc.)

Please see our [Webhooks Overview](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/webhooks/overview)
 for a guide on working with Webhooks.

circle-exclamation

Any webhooks sent to the server will contain the details of the **actual** items purchased (the basket at the point of payment).

If your app manages its own basket, it is important to verify that webhook contents always match the items and amount you are expecting.

[PreviousStart the Checkout Processchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/start-the-checkout-process)
[NextEndpointschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/endpoints)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Twig | Developers

Templates on the Tebex platform are written in the [Twig Templating Enginearrow-up-right](https://twig.symfony.com/)
. Twig allows you to customise your store with control structures, similar to any other language, while maintaining a sandboxed and safe environment for the Tebex infrastructure.

You're able to learn more information about the syntax of Twig by viewing the [official documentationarrow-up-right](https://twig.symfony.com/doc/2.x/templates.html)
.

A common Twig file may look like the following:

Copy

    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
        <head>
            <title>My Webpage</title>
        </head>
        <body>
            <ul id="navigation">
            {% for item in navigation %}
                <li><a href="{{ item.href }}">{{ item.caption }}</a></li>
            {% endfor %}
            </ul>
    
            <h1>My Webpage</h1>
            {{ a_variable }}
        </body>
    </html>

circle-info

If you're interested in becoming a pro at the Twig syntax, you can complete the official [Twig certification programmearrow-up-right](https://certification.symfony.com/exams/twig.html)
.

[PreviousGetting Startedchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/getting-started)
[NextTagschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/twig/tags)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Custom Render Location | Developers

If you don't wish to use a popup, you can choose to render the checkout to an element within your page. To do this, use `Tebex.checkout.render()` instead of `Tebex.checkout.launch()`:

Copy

    Tebex.checkout.init({
        ident: "your checkout request ident goes here",
    });
    
    Tebex.checkout.render(
        // The element to render to
        document.getElementById("some-element");
        // The width of the checkout iframe, in pixels
        500,
        // The height of the checkout iframe, in pixels
        600
        // Boolean indicating whether you want to open a new tab on mobile
        // (defaults to true if unspecified)
        false
    );

[PreviousWeb Componentschevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/web-components)
[NextOverviewchevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/webhooks/overview)

Last updated 1 year ago

---

# Events | Developers

Events are fired by Tebex.js upon specific actions to alert your frontend and enable you to take action when required. These events should **not** be used to confirm actual receipt of payment - you should use [Webhooks](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/webhooks/overview)
 instead.

To add an event callback, use `Tebex.checkout.on()` . The first argument to this function should be the name of the event to listen to, and the second argument should be a function to call when that function is fired:

Copy

    Tebex.checkout.on("payment:complete", (event) => {
        console.log("Payment completed!", event);
    });

Available events are as follows:

Name

Fired Upon

`"open"`

The checkout popup opening.

`"close"`

The checkout popup closing.

`"payment:complete"`

The customer has successfully completed their payment.

`"payment:error"`

The customer experienced an error, such as incorrect card details or insufficient funds, when making a payment.

All events that can be listened to with [`Tebex.checkout.on()`](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/events#events)
 are exposed on the element as custom DOM events, which means you can use addEventListener to subscribe to them:

Copy

    <html>
        <body>
            <tebex-checkout id="checkout"></tebex-checkout>
        </body>
        <script>
            const checkout = document.getElementById("checkout);
            
            checkout.addEventListener("open", () => {
                console.log("checkout opened");
            });
    
            checkout.addEventListener("close", () => {
                console.log("checkout closed");
            });
    
            checkout.addEventListener("payment:complete", (event) => {
                console.log("payment completed", event);
            });
    
            checkout.addEventListener("payment:error", (event) => {
                console.log("payment errored", event);
            });
        </script>
    </html>

[PreviousIntegrationchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/integration)
[NextWeb Componentschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/web-components)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Adding Packages | Developers

When adding packages, there may be certain **Variables** associated with them. These can be filled by providing a `variable_data` object.

Copy

    "variable_data": {
        "variable_identifier": "value"
    }

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/adding-packages#deliverable-types-and-variable-data)

Deliverable Types and Variable Data


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/adding-packages#gift-card)

Gift Card

Packages that deliver a gift card to the user should include `giftcard_to` mapped to the e-mail address that will receive the gift card:

Copy

    {
        "package_id": "6276316",
        "quantity": 1,
        "variable_data": {
            "giftcard_to": "[email protected]"
        }
    }

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/adding-packages#discord-action)

Discord Action

Packages that deliver Discord actions should include the user's `discord_id:`

Copy

    {
        "package_id": "6276316",
        "quantity": 1,
        "variable_data": {
            "discord_id": "000000000000000000"
        }
    }

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/adding-packages#game-server-commands)

Game Server Commands

Packages that deliver game server commands should include the `username_id` of the user, dependent on your store type.

You can get the **username\_id** after creating the basket if you provide the player's username at the time of creation. See **Creating a Basket** for specific details on Game Servers.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/adding-packages#custom-data)

Custom Data

You can also provide custom data when adding packages which can be referenced by the seller as part of the transaction.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/adding-packages#specifying-the-packages-game-server)

Specifying the Package's Game Server

If a package with a **Game Server Command** has the configuration option:

*   `Allow customers to select the game server they want to receive this package on.`
    

You can specify the target game server in the request by including `server_id` in your package's `variable_data`:

A list of your `server_ids` can be found in your [Tebex Control Panelarrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/game-servers)
 by clicking **Edit** beside your relevant game server. The server ID is the number at the end of the URL when editing the game server.

[PreviousCreating a Basketchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/creating-a-basket)
[NextGifting Packageschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/gifting-packages)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [Deliverable Types and Variable Data](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/adding-packages#deliverable-types-and-variable-data)
    
*   [Gift Card](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/adding-packages#gift-card)
    
*   [Discord Action](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/adding-packages#discord-action)
    
*   [Game Server Commands](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/adding-packages#game-server-commands)
    
*   [Custom Data](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/adding-packages#custom-data)
    
*   [Specifying the Package's Game Server](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/adding-packages#specifying-the-packages-game-server)
    

Copy

    {
        "package_id": "6276316",
        "quantity": 1,
        "variable_data": {
            "username_id": "9e65a968ee4743d19a2a4c9969154491"
        }
    }

Copy

    {
        "package_id": "6276316",
        "quantity": 1,
        "variable_data": {
            "username_id": "9e65a968ee4743d19a2a4c9969154491"
        },
        "custom": {
            "key": "value"
        }
    }

Copy

    {
        "package_id": "6276316",
        "quantity": 1,
        "variable_data": {
            "server_id": "127444"
        }
    }

# Errors | Developers

All errors returned by the Tebex Checkout APIs follow the RFC 7807 standard ([https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/html/rfc7807#section-3.1arrow-up-right](https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/html/rfc7807#section-3.1)
).

We also use standardised HTTP response codes to describe each error:

1.  **400 Bad Request** - User data validation error
    
2.  **401 / 403 - Authentication / Authorization** (depending on if it's pre- or post- authentication
    
3.  **404** - Requested resource doesn't exist
    
4.  **5xx** - Server side transitory errors.
    

Copy

    {
      "type": "Not Found",
      "title": "Resource not found",
      "status": 404,
      "detail": "The requested resource does not exist.",
      "instance": "/account/12345"
    }

[PreviousEndpointschevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/endpoints)
[NextOverviewchevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/overview)

Last updated 1 year ago

---

# Overview | Developers

Tebex.js is our solution to enable developers to integrate the checkout experience directly within your own website. Customers do not have to be redirected to an external website, improving conversions and providing a seamless checkout experience.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/overview#demo)

Demo


----------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can experience a live demo of Tebex.js by heading over to [https://js.tebex.ioarrow-up-right](https://js.tebex.io/)
 or taking a look at the gallery below.

![](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F924803319-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FaRz9HUAxrYuZsSDWhYnu%252Fuploads%252Fxl3iF5YKYS0rkZ9wBjIN%252FScreenshot%25202024-02-27%2520at%252012.44.17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfdeb3aeb-3d96-41a5-b86c-7d2ebbd03899&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ba5dcfa6&sv=2)

Upselling

# Creating a Basket | Developers

Depending on the type of Tebex store you are integrating, additional parameters may be necessary before the basket can be successfully created.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/creating-a-basket#authorizing-baskets)

Authorizing Baskets


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For most stores, the user must authorize their account before checkout is completed. This is done via the **/auth** endpoint where we will return the authentication options available for your store.

Provide a `returnUrl` , and after successful authentication the user will be directed back to your site.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/creating-a-basket#get-accounts-token-baskets-basketident-auth-returnurl-returnurl)

Get authentication links for a basket.

get

https://headless.tebex.io/api/accounts/{token}/baskets/{basketIdent}/auth?returnUrl={returnUrl}

Fetches a basket's auth URL.

Path parameters

tokenstringRequired

The webstore identifier.

Example: `t66x-7cd928b1e9312709e6810edac6dc1fd1eefc57cb`

basketIdentstringRequired

The basket identifier.

Example: `c00244-d2ac2e77418a55b25292a6bc7a719ad9c529ba2c`

returnUrlstringRequired

The URL you would like to redirect the user to after successful basket authentication.

Example: `https://example.tebex.io/`

Responses

chevron-right

200

Successful response returns the basket auth information.

application/json

Responseobject\[\]

Show propertiesplus

chevron-right

422

The provided webstore ID or basket ID is invalid.

get

/accounts/{token}/baskets/{basketIdent}/auth?returnUrl={returnUrl}

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

Test it

200

Successful response returns the basket auth information.

chevron-down

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/creating-a-basket#minecraft-and-overwolf-stores)

Minecraft and Overwolf Stores


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You must provide the `username` parameter as part of the basket creation request so that the basket is attributed to the correct user:

circle-exclamation

If you are creating a basket on your **backend server**, you will need to provide us the `ip_address` of the customer.

Currently we are unable to support IPv6 addresses being provided in the `ip_address` property. While we work on enabling IPv6 support, please provide an IPv4 address for the customer.

If you are creating a basket from the user's **browser**, we will automatically determine the IP from the requesting device.

The `Basket` which is returned will include the `username_id` which may be required for certain endpoints.

You should save the **username\_id** as part of the user's session for use later.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/creating-a-basket#universal-stores)

Universal Stores


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

No `username` is required, but depending on your package **Deliverables** you may need to provide `variable_data` so that the package is attributed to the correct user. See [**Adding Packages**](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/adding-packages)
**.**

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/creating-a-basket#post-accounts-token-baskets)

Create a new basket

post

https://headless.tebex.io/api/accounts/{token}/baskets

Creates a new basket for use during checkout.

Path parameters

tokenstringRequired

The webstore identifier.

Example: `t66x-7cd928b1e9312709e6810edac6dc1fd1eefc57cb`

Body

application/jsonchevron-down

application/json

complete\_urlstringOptional

A URL the user can return to when checkout is completed.

Example: `https://example.tebex.io/thank-you`

cancel\_urlstringOptional

A URL the user can return to when cancelling checkout.

Example: `https://tebex.io/`

customobjectOptional

Custom data you wish to associate with the basket. This data will be included with webhook responses and GET requests associated with the Basket.

Example: `{"foo":"bar"}`

complete\_auto\_redirectbooleanOptional

True if the user should automatically be redirected to the relevant complete/cancel URL

Example: `true`

Responses

chevron-right

200

Successful response returns the basket information.

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

chevron-right

422

The provided webstore ID is invalid.

post

/accounts/{token}/baskets

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

Test it

200

Successful response returns the basket information.

chevron-down

# Gifting Packages | Developers

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/gifting-packages#gifting-a-package-to-another-player)

Gifting a Package to Another Player

You can allow players to gift packages to other players. Include `target_username_id` , or `target_username` **when adding the package to the basket** and the package will be delivered to that player rather than the buyer.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/gifting-packages#gifting-example)

Gifting Example

The **target\_username\_id** should be a unique identifier for the player instead of their name (such as a Minecraft UUID or Steam ID):

Copy

    {
        "package_id": "6276316",
        "target_username_id": "069a79f444e94726a5befca90e38aaf5"
    }

circle-exclamation

Bedrock and Geyser stores must provide **target\_username** instead of the UUID due to differences in player IDs between Minecraft: Java Edition and Minecraft: Bedrock Edition.

Copy

    {
        "package_id": "6276316",
        "target_username": "TebexDev"
    }

[PreviousAdding Packageschevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/adding-packages)
[NextApplying Discounts / Creator Codeschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/applying-discounts-creator-codes)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [Gifting a Package to Another Player](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/gifting-packages#gifting-a-package-to-another-player)
    
*   [Gifting Example](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/gifting-packages#gifting-example)

# Webhooks | Developers

You will receive a webhook notification when the customer has created their webstore and their game server is ready to have the Tebex plugin automatically installed. Upon receipt of the webhook you should do the following:

1.  Download the Tebex plugin and install it onto the game server using the provided url.
    
2.  Download the premade config file and install it onto the game server (or manually create the config file depending on the game type, using the secret parameter in the webhook).
    
3.  Restart the game server to allow the Tebex Plugin to notify us that the plugin has been installed and authenticated against the webstore.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/affiliate-api/webhooks#setup-your-webhook-url)

Setup Your Webhook URL

You can specify the url of your webhook handler (such as serverhost.com/tebex.php) within the settings section of your affiliate control panel.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/affiliate-api/webhooks#authentication)

Authentication

To verify that the webhook has been sent from Tebex, we send a X-Tebex-Signature header that contains a HMAC using SHA256 created by the POST body (JSON) using your Webhook Signature Secret as the key.

You can find your Webhook Signature Secret within the setting section of your affiliate panel and example of calculating the signature in PHP is below:

Copy

    $body = file_get_contents("php://stdin");
    $secret = "myagreedsecret";
    $signature = hash_hmac("sha256", $body, $secret);
    
    if ($signature != $_SERVER['HTTP_X_TEBEX_SIGNATURE']) {
        return "Invalid signature";
    }

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/affiliate-api/webhooks#example-webhook-notification)

Example Webhook Notification

[PreviousGame Typeschevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/affiliate-api/game-types)

# Sidebar | Developers

Sidebar modules showcase additional information from the store. Modules are enabled in the store's configuration/The following modules are supported:

Type

Notes

`top_customer`

Shows the top customer of the store.

`textbox`

Renders custom HTML on the sidebar

`recent_payments`

Shows information of most recent payor

`featured_package`

Showcases a particular package

`giftcard_balance`

Shows the user's giftcard balance

`server_status`

Online status of a store's server

`payment_goal`

Progress to completing a payment goal

`community_goal`

Progress to completing a community goal

Use the following endpoint to get all enabled sidebar module data:

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/sidebar#get-accounts-token-sidebar)

Retrieves the available sidebar modules.

get

https://headless.tebex.io/api/accounts/{token}/sidebar

Retrieves the available sidebar modules configured for the store.

Path parameters

tokenstringRequired

The webstore identifier.

Example: `some-uuid`

Responses

chevron-right

200

Successful response.

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

get

/accounts/{token}/sidebar

# Error Handling | Developers

Errors are JSON format and are based around the standard HTTP status codes.

For example when an invalid secret key is provided the HTTP status code `403 Forbidden` will be returned along with a JSON body containing further information.

The `error_message` object will always be user friendly and should be shown directly to the client.

[PreviousAuthenticationchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/game-server-api/authentication)
[NextOverviewchevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/affiliate-api/overview)

Last updated 2 years ago

---

# Overview | Developers

The affiliate API enables you to integrate a one-click setup process for Tebex within your server management panel. A one-click setup process has the following benefits:

*   Removes the complexity of your customers installing the Tebex Plugin
    
*   Increases conversions which will result in more commission paid into your affiliate account.
    
*   You will receive a percentage of any revenue the server earns from their players.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/affiliate-api/overview#integration-example)

Integration Example

1.  Your customers click Install Tebex within your server management panel.
    
2.  You send an API request to Tebex alerting us of the customers request.
    
3.  We send an email to the customer with a link that allows them to create a webstore.
    
4.  Once the customer has created a webstore we will send you a webhook that contains a download url of the plugin, along with a pre-made plugin config file that includes the customers authentication details (their secret key).
    
5.  You install the provided plugin along with its config file and restart your customers game server.
    

A typical integration of this API will take a few hours depending on the experience of your development team.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/affiliate-api/overview#requirements)

Requirements

Please note that the one-click setup process is only available to approved partners of the Tebex Checkout For Server Hosts program. Please [**contact**arrow-up-right](https://www.tebex.io/contact)
 us for any additional questions or application information.

Once your application has been approved, your API key can be found towards the bottom of the [Settings pagearrow-up-right](https://affiliate.tebex.io/settings)
.

To ensure you receive JSON responses, please provide an `Accept: application/json` header with all API requests.

[PreviousError Handlingchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/game-server-api/error-handling)
[NextReferralschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/affiliate-api/referrals)

Last updated 2 years ago

*   [Integration Example](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/affiliate-api/overview#integration-example)
    
*   [Requirements](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/affiliate-api/overview#requirements)

# Schema | Developers

A template schema allows other team members or consumers of your template to change its appearance, for example providing colour pickers to change the colours of your template without the need to edit the CSS or HTML manually. This is especially useful if you are a template designer and you're selling access to your custom template for many different stores to use.

To edit the schema of a template, first open the template editor and select the **Change Schema** page from the navigation on the left. Any config options you add within the schema will appear within the Appearance section of the creator panel when you click edit on the template.

A great example of Schema in action would be to look at the configuration options available with our default template, Exo, which you can view in the [creator panelarrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/templates/187300)
.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/schema#example-schema)

Example Schema


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    {
      "author": "Tebex",
      "support_email": "[email protected]",
      "config": [\
        {\
          "header": "Customize Template",\
          "options": [\
            {\
              "id": "nav-style",\
              "name": "Navigation Style",\
              "description": "Set the location for your navigation.",\
              "type": "select",\
              "default": "Vertical Nav in Sidebar",\
              "values": [\
                "Horizontal Nav in Header",\
                "Vertical Nav in Sidebar"\
              ]\
            },\
            {\
              "id": "server-ip",\
              "name": "Server IP",\
              "default": "",\
              "description": "Enter your server IP - it will be used in the copy server IP section.",\
              "type": "textarea"\
            },\
            {\
              "id": "discord",\
              "name": "Discord",\
              "default": "",\
              "description": "Enter your Discord invite url - it will be used in the header Discord section.",\
              "type": "textarea"\
            }\
          ]\
        }\
      ]
    }

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/schema#available-config-types)

Available Config Types


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You're able to implement several different types of config options within your template schema, from colour pickers to text boxes.

chevron-rightColour Picker[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/schema#colour-picker)

Displays a colour picker for selecting a custom HEX code.

chevron-rightFile Uploader[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/schema#file-uploader)

Display a file upload option, useful for favicons, or other assets.

chevron-rightImage Uploader[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/schema#image-uploader)

Display an image uploader config option.

chevron-rightSelect[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/schema#select)

Display a select dropdown to allow the store to select from multiple options.

chevron-rightSlider[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/schema#slider)

Display a slider to allow the store to select between a range of numbers - useful for customising.

chevron-rightTextarea[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/schema#textarea)

chevron-rightUrl[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/schema#url)

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/schema#accessing-config-options)

Accessing Config Options


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To dynamically access the config option from within your template you can use the [`config()`](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/twig/functions#config)
 Twig function. This will output the entered option value, allowing you to use it however you wish within your template, such as outputting a text area into a specific location or altering CSS via a colour picker.

[PreviousAssetschevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/assets)
[NextDeveloper Planchevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/developer-plan)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [Example Schema](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/schema#example-schema)
    
*   [Available Config Types](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/schema#available-config-types)
    
*   [Accessing Config Options](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/schema#accessing-config-options)
    

Copy

    {
       "id": "primary-colour",
       "name": "Primary Colour",
       "default": "#0000FF",
       "description": "Select your primary colour.",
       "type": "colour-picker"
    }

Copy

    {
       "id": "my-file",
       "name": "My File",
       "default": "",
       "description": "Upload a file.",
       "type": "file"
    }

Copy

    {
       "id": "custom-image",
       "name": "Custom Image",
       "default": "",
       "description": "Upload an image here.",
       "type": "image-uploader"
    }

Copy

    {
       "id": "nav-style",
       "name": "Navigation Style",
       "description": "Set the location for your navigation.",
       "type": "select",
       "default": "Vertical Nav in Sidebar",
       "values": [\
           "Horizontal Nav in Header",\
           "Vertical Nav in Sidebar"\
        ]
    }

       "id": "width",

       "default": "",

       "type": "slider",
       "min": 0,
       "max": 100
    }

       "type": "textarea"
    }

# Game Types | Developers

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/affiliate-api/game-types#get-game-types)

Get Game Types


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# Headers and Authentication | Developers

As a creator using Checkout API, you must authenticate directly with the API as opposed to individual customers authenticating.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/headers-and-authentication#authorization)

Authorization


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We use HTTP BASIC for authorization, and all requests are made over HTTPS so that your credentials are protected.

Username **(Project ID)**

Your Project ID (you can get this from [https://creator.tebex.io/developers/api-keysarrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/developers/api-keys)
)

Password **(Private Key)**

Your Private Key (you can get this from [https://creator.tebex.io/developers/api-keysarrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/developers/api-keys)
)

circle-exclamation

Your store's Private Key should **never** be shared publicly. If your key is ever compromised, it can be reset in your Webstore panel.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/headers-and-authentication#content-type)

Content Type


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

All requests use `application/json` as the `Content-Type`. Ensure this is set with all requests to our Checkout API.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/headers-and-authentication#example)

Example

Copy

    const url = "https://checkout.tebex.io/api/checkout";
    
    const headers = new Headers();
    headers.append('Authorization', 'Basic ' + btoa(username + ':' + password));
    headers.append('Content-Type', 'application/json');
    
    const options = {
            method: 'POST', // Use 'GET', 'POST', 'PUT', etc. as needed
            headers: headers
    };
    
    const response = await fetch(url, options);
    // etc

[PreviousOverviewchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview)
[NextStart the Checkout Processchevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/start-the-checkout-process)

Last updated 2 months ago

*   [Authorization](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/headers-and-authentication#authorization)
    
*   [Content Type](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/headers-and-authentication#content-type)
    
*   [Example](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/headers-and-authentication#example)

# Overview | Developers

The Game Server API is for implementing command execution on game servers - an example of this would be the official Tebex Minecraft Plugin.

If you haven't already done so, we recommend having a read of our [quick start guide](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/getting-started)
 before beginning integration.

circle-info

If you've created an SDK or game server plugin, please send an email to [\[email protected\]](https://docs.tebex.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
 and we'd be happy to showcase it on this site.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/game-server-api/overview#official-game-server-plugins)

Official Game Server Plugins


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can download compiled versions of the official plugins that implement this API from the [Game Serversarrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/game-servers)
 section of the creator panel.

The source code for these plugins can also be found in the following GitHub repositories:

*   [Tebex-Minecraft (Minecraft: Java Edition)arrow-up-right](https://github.com/tebexio/Tebex-Minecraft)
    
*   [Tebex-Hytalearrow-up-right](https://github.com/tebexio/Tebex-Hytale)
    
*   [Tebex-Oxide (Rust, 7 Days To Die and Hurtworld)arrow-up-right](https://github.com/BuycraftPlugin/Tebex-Oxide)
    
*   [Tebex-Ark (ARK: Survival Evolved)arrow-up-right](https://github.com/BuycraftPlugin/Tebex-Ark)
    
*   [Tebex-FiveM (FiveM / GTA V)arrow-up-right](https://github.com/BuycraftPlugin/Tebex-FiveM)
    
*   [Tebex-Forgearrow-up-right](https://github.com/BuycraftPlugin/Tebex-Forge)
    
*   [Tebex-uModarrow-up-right](https://github.com/BuycraftPlugin/Tebex-uMod)
    
*   [Tebex-Atlasarrow-up-right](https://github.com/BuycraftPlugin/Tebex-Atlas)
    
*   [Tebex-TorchAPIarrow-up-right](https://github.com/BuycraftPlugin/Tebex-TorchAPI)

# Web Components | Developers

As an alternative to using the `Tebex.checkout` JavaScript API, Tebex.js also provides a `tebex-checkout` [Web Componentarrow-up-right](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Web_components)
.

With this, you can embed a Tebex Checkout into your page by placing the `<tebex-checkout></tebex-checkout>` HTML tag anywhere in your page's `<body>`, so long as Tebex.js is also loaded into the page:

Copy

    <html>
        <head>
            <script defer src="https://js.tebex.io/v/1.js"></script>
        </head>
        <body>
            <tebex-checkout></tebex-checkout>
        </body>
    </html>

circle-info

Due to Web Component quirks, you must include both opening and closing HTML tags (like `<tebex-checkout></tebex-checkout>`). Using a self-closing tag (`<tebex-checkout/>`) is not valid.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/web-components#modes)

Modes

Two modes are available for `tebex-checkout`:

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/web-components#popup-mode)

Popup Mode

This is the default mode. The component will display nothing initially, but will launch the checkout as a popup when activated, akin to [`Tebex.checkout.launch()`](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/web-components#launch)
.

The simplest way to achieve this is by placing a button inside the `<tebex-checkout>` and `</tebex-checkout>` tags. Tebex.js will automatically attach handlers so that clicking the button will launch the checkout:

Copy

    <tebex-checkout ident="...">
        <button>Open Checkout</button>
    </tebex-checkout>

circle-info

You don't have to use a button here, it could be any HTML - styled however you see fit - as long as it's clickable!

Alternatively, if you would prefer to open the checkout from your code (i.e. instead of having a user click something), you can leave the `tebex-checkout` empty and add the `open` attribute to it whenever you are ready for it to launch:

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/web-components#inline-mode)

Inline Mode

By adding the `inline` attribute to the checkout element, the element will instead be rendered inline within the rest of the page, in a similar way to [`Tebex.checkout.render()`](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/web-components#custom-render-location)
.

It will automatically take up 100% of the width of its container and set its height to a sane default for displaying the iframe checkout content, but you can use the `height` attribute to manually set the height, in CSS pixels:

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/web-components#common-attributes)

Common Attributes

HTML attributes take the place of [`Tebex.checkout.init()`](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/web-components#config)
's config options, along with a couple of extra options:

Attribute

Details

`ident`

**Required.** This should be the checkout request ident received via the [Headless API](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/overview)
 or [Checkout API](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview)
.

`locale`

Default language for checkout text. Specified as an ISO locale code, e.g. `"en_US"` for American English, `"de_DE"` for German, etc. Users can change the language from within the checkout panel UI.

`theme`

Checkout color theme. Must be one of the following options:

*   `"light"`
    
*   `"dark"`
    
*   `"auto"` - applies the theme based on the user's light/dark mode system preference.
    
*   `"default"` - applies the theme option you have selected in your store's settings.
    

`color-primary`

Checkout primary brand color.

`color-secondary`

Checkout secondary brand color.

`popup-on-mobile`

If set, when in popup mode, the checkout will always launch in the current browser window rather than opening a new page, even on mobile devices.

`redirect-on-complete`

If set to a URL, the user will be redirected to this page once the payment has completed.

For example:

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/web-components#framework-integration)

Framework Integration

Web Components such as `tebex-checkout` integrate seamlessly with most modern frontend frameworks without needing any special setup. However, if you are using **Vue**, please note that you may need to adjust your config to [**skip component resolution**arrow-up-right](https://vuejs.org/guide/extras/web-components#skipping-component-resolution)
 for `tebex-checkout`.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/web-components#example)

Example

In Vue, this is how you could include an inline `tebex-checkout` component and call a function when the payment complete event fires:

[PreviousEventschevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/events)
[NextCustom Render Locationchevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/custom-render-location)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [Modes](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/web-components#modes)
    
*   [Common Attributes](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/web-components#common-attributes)
    
*   [Framework Integration](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/web-components#framework-integration)
    

Copy

    <script>
        function openCheckout() {
            const checkout = document.getElementById("checkout");
            checkout.setAttribute("open", "true");
        }
        // call openCheckout() when you want the checkout to launch...
    </script>
    
    <tebex-checkout id="checkout" ident="..."></tebex-checkout>

Copy

    <tebex-checkout inline ident="..." height="800"></tebex-checkout>

Copy

    <tebex-checkout theme="dark" color-primary="#ff0000"></tebex-checkout>

Copy

    <script setup>
       import "@tebexio/tebex.js";
    
        const ident = ref("");
    
        // something to fetch the ident here
        
        function onPaymentComplete() {
            console.log("payment completed");
        }
    </script>
    
    <template>
        <tebex-checkout inline :ident="ident" @payment:complete="onPaymentComplete"></tebex-checkout>
    </template>

# Referrals | Developers

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/affiliate-api/referrals#create-referral)

Create Referral


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`POST` `https://affiliate.tebex.io/api/referrals`

This endpoint should be called when your customer requests that they want to install Tebex on their game server. It will send an email to the customer containing a link which allows them to setup their webstore and ensure your affiliate account is associated with the customer.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/affiliate-api/referrals#headers)

Headers

Name

Type

Description

Authorization

string

Bearer <Your API Key>

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/affiliate-api/referrals#request-body)

Request Body

Name

Type

Description

link

string

The UUID of your referral link within your affiliate panel. You can find this on https://affiliate.tebex.io/links, under your Link name.

reference

string

A unique ID that references the customer's game server within your management panel. You will use this to identify the game server when we send the installation webhook.

game\_type\_id

number

The ID of the game type found within the game types endpoint.

server\_name

string

The name of your customer's game server.

email

string

The email address of the customer.

last\_name

string

The last name of the customer.

first\_name

string

The first name of the customer.

201: Created Affiliate successfully created.

Copy

    {
      "data": {
        "reference": "123456",
        "secret": null,
        "game_type": {
          "id": 1
        },
        "setup_at": null
      }
    }

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/affiliate-api/referrals#get-referral)

Get Referral


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`GET` `https://affiliate.tebex.io/api/referrals/:reference`

Retrieve an existing referral. This method is useful for checking if a customer has created their webstore and can also be used to retrieve the plugin urls and locations of the premade config files.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/affiliate-api/referrals#path-parameters)

Path Parameters

Name

Type

Description

reference

string

The reference provided when you created the referral.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/affiliate-api/referrals#headers-1)

Headers

Name

Type

Description

Authorization

string

Bearer <Your API Key>

200: OK Successfully retrieved an existing referral

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/affiliate-api/referrals#get-referral-config-file)

Get Referral Config File


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`GET` `https://affiliate.tebex.io/api/referrals/:reference/config/:platform`

Retrieve the premade config file for a specific platform (such as Minecraft Spigot or Forge). The config file will include the customer's secret key, removing any need of manual setup of the Tebex plugin on the server's behalf.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/affiliate-api/referrals#path-parameters-1)

Path Parameters

Name

Type

Description

platform

string

The plugin platform such as bukkit or forge.

reference

string

The reference provided when you created the referral.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/affiliate-api/referrals#headers-2)

Headers

Name

Type

Description

Authorization

string

Bearer <Your API Key>

200: OK The premade config file for the Tebex plugin

[PreviousOverviewchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/affiliate-api/overview)
[NextGame Typeschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/affiliate-api/game-types)

# Login Webhooks | Developers

Login verification allows you to integrate your own authentication layer into your webstore. Once you have set up player verification the webstore will ping an endpoint hosted on your own website with information about the player attempting to log in. Depending on your response you can deny/allow the customer from logging in.

The login verification system opens up a whole new world of opportunities for integrating with your own backend systems.

circle-info

**Please only use this feature if you know how to use it, incorrectly using this system (such as using a Discord webhook) will prevent customers from logging in to your store.**

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/webhooks/login-webhooks#how-to-setup-player-verification)

How To Setup Player Verification


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Go to **Webhooks**.
    
2.  Enter the full URL of your endpoint in the login webhooks config box, for example, [http://example.com/tebex/verification.phparrow-up-right](http://example.com/tebex/verification.php)
    . You can use any programming language to create your endpoint as long as it returns the response as listed below.
    

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/webhooks/login-webhooks#accepting-notifications-and-returning-a-response)

Accepting Notifications And Returning A Response


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/webhooks/login-webhooks#example-request)

Example Request

When a customer attempts to log in to your webstore we will send a GET request to the URL you have previously set as outlined above. An example request URL would look like the following: ​

Copy

    http://example.com/tebex/verification.php?ign=Notch&ip=127.0.0.1&country=US

**Request Query Parameters**

1.  **ign** - The username of the customer attempting to log in.
    
2.  **ip** - The IP address of the customer attempting to log in.
    
3.  **country** - The country code of the customer (Based on GEO locating their IP address).
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/webhooks/login-webhooks#example-response)

Example Response

To allow the customer to log in based on the provided query parameters you need to return a JSON response such as the following example: ​

​ If you don't want to allow the customer to login you can return a JSON response such as: ​

[PreviousOverviewchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/webhooks/overview)
[NextOverviewchevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/game-server-api/overview)

Last updated 2 years ago

*   [How To Setup Player Verification](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/webhooks/login-webhooks#how-to-setup-player-verification)
    
*   [Accepting Notifications And Returning A Response](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/webhooks/login-webhooks#accepting-notifications-and-returning-a-response)
    
*   [Example Request](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/webhooks/login-webhooks#example-request)
    
*   [Example Response](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/webhooks/login-webhooks#example-response)
    

Copy

    {  
        "verified":true,
        "message":"An optional message to send to the customer upon login. This field is optional."
    }
    ​

Copy

    {
        "verified":false,
        "error":"You are not allowed to access our webstore."
    }
    ​

# Tiers | Developers

This guide will detail the expected flows and endpoints for implementing tiers using Headless API.

See our Creator docs for [Tiered Packagesarrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/tiered-packages)
 to learn how to set up tiers.

circle-exclamation

If you are using an older or custom store template, you may need to modify your template to support tiers. A tiered category view is different from a non-tiered category.

See [Supporting Tiers on Custom Store Templates](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/guides/supporting-tiers-on-custom-store-templates)
 to learn how to set up the necessary pages.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/tiers#checkout-flow)

Checkout Flow


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Tiers require an authenticated user. After you create the basket, you must log the user in using the relevant basket auth links.

See [Creating A Basket](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/creating-a-basket)
 for further information.

The expected flow for checking out with a Tier is identical to any other package:

1.  Create the basket
    
2.  Authenticate the user via the basket's auth links
    
3.  Add the tiered package to the basket
    
4.  Direct the user to checkout
    

On successful checkout, the user will now have an `active_tier` when retrieving their tiered categories against their `usernameId`.

If the `active_tier` property is not present, the user does not have an active package in that tier.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/tiers#api-endpoints)

API Endpoints


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Tiered categories use our existing `/categories` endpoint.

Unlike other Headless API endpoints, you must use HTTP Basic authentication with the **Username** set to your project ID and **Password** as your secret key.

Provide a `usernameId` as a query parameter to check for an `active_tier`

All tiered categories will have the property `tiered: true`

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/tiers#get-accounts-token-categories)

Gets all categories available in the webstore.

get

https://headless.tebex.io/api/accounts/{token}/categories

Gets all categories from a webstore. This does not include package information. To include package information, add `?includePackages=1` to the URL.

Path parameters

tokenstringRequired

The webstore identifier.

Example: `t66x-7cd928b1e9312709e6810edac6dc1fd1eefc57cb`

Responses

chevron-right

200

patch

Updates a tier to a new package. A recurring payment updated webhook is sent when an update is successful.

# Integration | Developers

Tebex.js enables you to integrate a seamless checkout experience for customers without them leaving your website or game.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/integration#installation)

Installation


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/integration#from-npm)

From NPM

Tebex.js is available as an NPM package, which you can install using your preferred JS package manager:

Copy

    npm install @tebexio/tebex.js

The `Tebex` object can then be imported into your code like so:

Copy

    import Tebex from "@tebexio/tebex.js";

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/integration#from-our-cdn)

From Our CDN

Alternatively, we also provide Tebex.js via our own CDN, which you can add as a script within the `<head>` tag of your website:

Copy

    <script defer src="https://js.tebex.io/v/1.js"></script>

circle-info

We will automatically update `v/1.js` with new minor and patch releases of Tebex.js. This shouldn't present any breaking changes, but if you would prefer to stay on a fixed version, you can specify the full version number in the URL, for example `https://js.tebex.io/v/1.1.1.js`. Our version history can be found on our [GitHubarrow-up-right](https://github.com/tebexio/Tebex.js/releases)
 releases page.

When installing Tebex.js this way, the `Tebex` object will become available globally on the `window` object.

We recommend using `defer` on the script to prevent it from blocking your website's initial page render, but when doing do, it's important to **wait for the page** `**load**` **event** before you begin configuring the checkout:

Copy

    <script>
        addEventListener("load", function() {
            // Configure Tebex.js here
        });
    </script>

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/integration#config)

Config


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Before your checkout can be launched, it must first be configured by calling the `Tebex.checkout.init()` method. This method takes an object containing config options:

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/integration#options)

Options

Option

Details

Default

ident

**Required.** This should be the checkout request ident received via the [Webstore Builder](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/pages/checkout.html)
, [Headless API](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/overview)
 or [Checkout API](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview)
.

locale

Default language for checkout text. Specified as an ISO locale code, e.g. `"en_US"` for American English, `"de_DE"` for German, etc. Users can change the language from within the checkout panel UI.

English

theme

Checkout color theme. Must be one of the following options:

*   `"light"`
    
*   `"dark"`
    
*   `"auto"` - applies the theme based on the user's light/dark mode system preference.
    
*   `"default"` - applies the theme option you have selected in your store's settings.
    

`"default"`

colors

Checkout [brand colors](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/integration#brand-color-config)
.

`[]`

defaultPaymentMethod

The default payment method ID to be selected when the user loads the checkout. You can get the list of available methods from the [creator panelarrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/payment-methods)
. To get the ID of the method, hover over the name in the table.

closeOnPaymentComplete

If enabled, the checkout popup will automatically close as soon as the payment has completed. Otherwise, the user will see a "Payment Complete" screen with a button that will close the popup when clicked.

`false`

circle-exclamation

In some cases, pages with heavy ad content can trigger browser pop-up blocking when loading Tebex.js. Ensuring the page has minimal ads, or redirecting users to the checkout flow in a new tab, will avoid this behaviour.

circle-info

You're able to retrieve the checkout request ident by using the `{{ basket.ident }}` global Twig variable if you are using a Tebex hosted webstore.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/integration#brand-color-config)

Brand Color Config

Brand colors can be specified as an array of objects with `name` and `color` keys. `name` must be either `"primary"` or `"secondary"`, while `color` must be a valid CSS color:

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/integration#launch)

Launch


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you are ready to show the Tebex.js checkout to your user, you can call the `Tebex.checkout.launch()` method. On desktop devices this will open the checkout as a popup, while on mobile devices it will open as a new tab.

If you are only calling the `Tebex.checkout.launch()` inside a click event, you might prefer to also call `Tebex.checkout.init()`inside your click handler.

This way, you don't need to wait for the page `load` event to fire to configure your checkout:

[PreviousOverviewchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/overview)
[NextEventschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/events)

Last updated 19 days ago

*   [Installation](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/integration#installation)
    
*   [From NPM](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/integration#from-npm)
    
*   [From Our CDN](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/integration#from-our-cdn)
    
*   [Config](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/integration#config)
    
*   [Options](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/integration#options)
    
*   [Brand Color Config](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/integration#brand-color-config)
    
*   [Launch](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/integration#launch)
    

Copy

    Tebex.checkout.init({
        ident: "checkout request ident"
    });

Copy

    
    Tebex.checkout.init({
        //..
        colors: [\
            {\
                name: "primary",\
                color: "#910f0f",\
            },\
            {\
                name: "secondary",\
                color: "#25c235"\
            }\
        ]
    });

Copy

    <!-- Include the Tebex.js script here -->
    <script>
      function checkout() {
        Tebex.checkout.init({
          ident: "your checkout request ident goes here"
        };
        Tebex.checkout.launch();
      }
    </script>
    <!-- ... -->
    <button onclick="checkout()">Checkout</button>

---

# Getting Your Listings | Developers

You can retrieve your packages & category listings in JSON format and display them however you wish.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/getting-your-listings#get-accounts-token-categories)

Gets all categories available in the webstore.

get

https://headless.tebex.io/api/accounts/{token}/categories

Gets all categories from a webstore. This does not include package information. To include package information, add `?includePackages=1` to the URL.

Path parameters

tokenstringRequired

The webstore identifier.

Example: `t66x-7cd928b1e9312709e6810edac6dc1fd1eefc57cb`

Responses

chevron-right

200

Successful response returns a list of category information.

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

get

/accounts/{token}/categories

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

Test it

200

Successful response returns a list of category information.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/getting-your-listings#get-accounts-token-categories-includepackages-1)

Gets a store's categories including all package information with them.

get

https://headless.tebex.io/api/accounts/{token}/categories?includePackages=1

Gets all categories from a webstore including packages.

Path parameters

tokenstringRequired

The webstore identifier.

Example: `t66x-7cd928b1e9312709e6810edac6dc1fd1eefc57cb`

Responses

chevron-right

200

Successful response returns a list of category information.

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

get

/accounts/{token}/categories?includePackages=1

HTTPchevron-down

Test it

200

Successful response returns a list of category information.
