[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/getting-your-listings#get-accounts-token-categories-categoryid)

Gets information about a specific category

get

https://headless.tebex.io/api/accounts/{token}/categories/{categoryId}

Gets information about a category and returns the packages in that category.

Path parameters

tokenstringRequired

The webstore identifier.

Example: `t66x-7cd928b1e9312709e6810edac6dc1fd1eefc57cb`

categoryIdstringRequired

The ID of the category to fetch.

Example: `127244343`

Responses

chevron-right

200

Successful response returns the category without package information.

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

/accounts/{token}/categories/{categoryId}

          "order": 1,\
          "display_type": "list"\
        }\
      ]
    }

# Applying Discounts / Creator Codes | Developers

If offered by your store, you can apply coupons, gift cards, and creator codes via Headless API once a basket has been created and the user's desired packages have been added.

circle-exclamation

Depending on the store's configuration, multiple gift cards or coupons may be applied. To remove a gift card or coupon, use the relevant **/remove** endpoint.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/applying-discounts-creator-codes#post-accounts-token-baskets-basketident-creator-codes)

Apply a creator code to a basket.

post

https://headless.tebex.io/api/accounts/{token}/baskets/{basketIdent}/creator-codes

Applies a creator code to a basket.

Path parameters

tokenstringRequired

The webstore identifier.

Example: `t66x-7cd928b1e9312709e6810edac6dc1fd1eefc57cb`

basketIdentstringRequired

The basket identifier.

Example: `c00244-d2ac2e77418a55b25292a6bc7a719ad9c529ba2c`

Body

application/jsonchevron-down

application/json

creator\_codestringOptionalExample: `Academy10`

Responses

chevron-right

200

Successful response returns the basket.

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

chevron-right

422

The provided request is invalid. The error response will include detail as to which parameter failed validation.

post

/accounts/{token}/baskets/{basketIdent}/creator-codes

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

Test it

200

Successful response returns the basket.

chevron-down

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/applying-discounts-creator-codes#post-accounts-token-baskets-basketident-creator-codes-remove)

Remove a creator code from the basket.

post

https://headless.tebex.io/api/accounts/{token}/baskets/{basketIdent}/creator-codes/remove

Applies a creator code to a basket.

Path parameters

tokenstringRequired

The webstore identifier.

Example: `t66x-7cd928b1e9312709e6810edac6dc1fd1eefc57cb`

basketIdentstringRequired

The basket identifier.

Example: `c00244-d2ac2e77418a55b25292a6bc7a719ad9c529ba2c`

Responses

chevron-right

200

Creator code removed successfully.

No content

chevron-right

422

The provided request is invalid. The error response will include detail as to which parameter failed validation.

post

/accounts/{token}/baskets/{basketIdent}/creator-codes/remove

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

Test it

200

Creator code removed successfully.

chevron-down

No content

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/applying-discounts-creator-codes#post-accounts-token-baskets-basketident-giftcards)

# Growth and Success | Creators

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success#best-practices)

Best Practices


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

Whether you’re a creator using Tebex or any game monetization platform, you should strive to maximize every opportunity from every buyer that enters your store.

This section will highlight some essential must-haves to help steer your store toward success.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success#product-images)

Product Images

Store Images display the product you’re selling - and you want them to look good and represent clearly what you are selling. The images are the first things buyers notice when they browse your store. High-resolution and clear images are strongly recommended to improve conversion rates.

![](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1152203580-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LuI8PwvsHA79mTA-7bh%252Fuploads%252F17RbOoZ1G0XcaqW80sTe%252FScreenshot%25202024-01-23%2520092628.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc83d26d5-4047-47fa-bd4f-fdab3e0badd4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=efec729c&sv=2)

Visual representation of the amount of coins a package contains

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success#product-description)

Product Description

A product description is the text that explains what a product is and why it's worth purchasing. The purpose of a product description is to supply customers with important information and get them excited about purchasing as well as the features and key benefits of the product so they're about to buy.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success#subscription-products)

Subscription Products

Subscription revenue is more predictable than non-subscription revenue because it is based on recurring payments from customers. This helps businesses plan their future, forecasts and budgets more effectively. Your store's analytics will show you the most popular products, which will give you a clearer picture of what people consider most important in your store and server.

circle-info

[Maximizing Your Tebex Store Potential: The Benefits and Strategies of Subscription Revenue Modelarrow-up-right](https://blog.tebex.io/maximizing-your-business-potential-the-benefits-and-strategies-of-subscription-revenue-models/)

![](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1152203580-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LuI8PwvsHA79mTA-7bh%252Fuploads%252F5K2NzGSn0yoDdWmQvDeU%252FScreenshot%25202024-01-23%2520094718.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da4f4c40b-8adf-429e-9769-7b4d88f8e018&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1f60ca0e&sv=2)

Ranks being used as a subscription model

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success#abandoned-basket-recovery)

Abandoned Basket Recovery

Abandoned basket recovery sends customers a follow-up email or an in-game message if they have added items to their basket but have not yet completed the checkout. This is a great way to give your customer another chance to buy their product.

Options you can modify:

*   **Email Delay** - The number of minutes to wait before sending an email to the customer. We recommend a few hours.
    
*   **Recovery Discount** - Enter the percentage discount the customer should receive to entice them back to complete their purchase.
    
*   **Categories** - Select a list of categories to which the recovery discount should apply. Leave this blank if you want the discount to apply to all categories on your webstore.
    
*   **In-Game Messages** - If this feature is enabled, you can also configure messages to be sent to the customer in-game to ensure they are notified about the discount offered.
    

circle-info

[https://docs.tebex.io/store/key-features/abandoned-basket-recoveryarrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/store/key-features/abandoned-basket-recovery)
 [arrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/store/key-features/abandoned-basket-recovery)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success#purchase-follow-ups)

Purchase Follow-ups

Sending an email to a customer after their purchase helps them stay connected to your project and can help them return to support you again. For more info about using coupons in your store, you may find this [postarrow-up-right](https://blog.tebex.io/coupons/)
 helpful.

Options you can modify:

*   **Coupon Discount** - Enter the percentage discount the customer should receive to entice them back to complete their purchase.
    
*   **Coupon Duration -** Enter the amount of time (hours, days) for the coupon duration.
    
*   **Email Delay -** How long should the delay be until the email is sent to the customer after purchasing? You can also choose the value to be in hours, days, or weeks.
    
*   **Email Subject** - The subject of the email sent to your customer. This should be worded to entice your customers to open the email, such as "Hey! Thanks for your purchase - here's a coupon code as a thank you for your support".
    

circle-info

[https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/post-purchase-follow-upsarrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/post-purchase-follow-ups)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success#creator-codes)

Creator Codes

Creator codes allow your customers to support your streamers, YouTubers, and other creators while removing all the headaches around handling payouts. You're able to create a code that will automatically send a predefined percentage of the payment to your creator's wallet.

Options you can modify:

*   **Code** \- Unique code that names the creator code the buyer will use.
    
*   **Revenue share** - the % of revenue that will go to the creator.
    
*   **Customer discount** - the % discount received by customers.
    

circle-info

[https://docs.tebex.io/store/key-features/creator-codesarrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/store/key-features/creator-codes)
 [arrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/store/key-features/creator-codes)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success#gift-cards)

Gift Cards

Gift Cards allow you to sell unique codes on your store which contain a balance of real currency. Customers purchase Gift Cards from your webstore and then receive an email containing a code, which they can use themselves or pass on to friends or family as a gift.

![](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1152203580-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LuI8PwvsHA79mTA-7bh%252Fuploads%252FUddRTJDiowj6qACewJBj%252FScreenshot%25202024-01-23%2520094646.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db9d04e69-ef6c-478b-ad69-52099eef7801&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fc1bdaec&sv=2)

Gift Cards

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success#bundles)

Bundles

Product bundling is a technique in which several products are grouped together and sold as a single unit for one price. This strategy is used to encourage customers to buy more products. Product bundling can increase the profits and sales of individual items over time. By grouping your items together, you can make your customers buy more than one product during a single purchase, which increases your average transaction value.

![](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1152203580-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LuI8PwvsHA79mTA-7bh%252Fuploads%252FmGF6mvfaIXXHqnF2tHOh%252FScreenshot%25202024-01-23%2520094559.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2e4de1d3-03f5-4e8f-91be-dd639e44b363&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e1e92a17&sv=2)

Bundling examples

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success#customer-support-channels)

Customer Support Channels

Customer support should be a critical part of the buyer experience. Be responsive to customer inquiries and provide clear and helpful responses. Consider offering support via Discord or a ticketing system to make it easy for customers to get in touch.

# Pages | Developers

Pages represent different landing points of your customers on your Tebex store. For example, when customers visit a category on your store, the category.html page will be rendered. For this reason, pages must be implemented in your templates and cannot be deleted (unlike [Assets](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/assets)
).

If you'd like access to a variable that is not currently available, [please let us know.arrow-up-right](https://forms.monday.com/forms/8cbacdac7c30b725cd4617cbba0e5eeb?r=use1)

The only pages that are not accessible to the public are the following:

Page

layout.html

This is the global layout of your store that all pages extend from. You are able to create multiple layouts if you wish via creating an [Asset](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/assets)
.

module.\*

These pages are used to build the Sidebar modules of your store, and you can view more information within the [Sidebar Modules](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/sidebar-modules)
 section.

[Previouspagechevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/global-variables/page)
[Nextindex.htmlchevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/pages/index.html)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Overview | Developers

Webhooks enable you to receive notifications upon certain webstore events, for example when a new payment is made. We will send a HTTP request containing a JSON object to any configured endpoints that are subscribing to the respective event. Webhooks are a great way to integrate Tebex with your own website, forum or internal database.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/webhooks/overview#how-to-setup-webhooks-endpoints)

How To Setup Webhooks Endpoints


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Go to **Developers** > **Webhooks** > **Endpoints**.
    
2.  Click **Add Endpoint**.
    
3.  Enter the URL of your webhook endpoint.
    
4.  Select the types of webhooks that you'd like to subscribe to.
    
5.  Click **Add**.
    

After adding your endpoint, you will receive a warning to inform you that we haven't been able to validate endpoint. Please see the section below for further information about handling validation webhooks.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/webhooks/overview#handling-validation-webhooks)

Handling Validation Webhooks


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Webhooks will not be sent to an endpoint unless it has been validated first. This is to ensure we are not sending HTTP requests to URLs that are not expecting our webhooks.

The validation webhook that we send will look similar to the example below. To identify a validation webhook you can check the `type` property in the JSON body.

Copy

    {
      "id": "2c116b11-1110-91e0-b266-b792c8da5f11",
      "type": "validation.webhook",
      "date": "2021-08-24T12:21:47+00:00",
      "subject": {}
    }

Upon receiving a validation webhook you must respond with a **200 OK** response containing a JSON object that has an `id` property representing the validation webhook's ID, please see the example response below.

Once your endpoint is setup to successfully handle validation webhooks, please visit **Developers** > **Webhooks** \> **Endpoints** and click the **Validate** button next to the endpoint to re-send the validation webhook.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/webhooks/overview#verifying-webhook-authenticity)

Verifying Webhook Authenticity


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/webhooks/overview#ip-address)

IP Address

Webhooks from Tebex will only ever be sent from the two IP addresses listed below.

**18.209.80.3 54.87.231.232**

When building your webhook endpoint, we suggest that you check the IP address of the sender and throw a 404 Not Found error if the IP address isn't in the above list.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/webhooks/overview#signature)

Signature

In addition to checking the IP address, we strongly advise that you verify the **X-Signature** header that we send with all requests.

The signature is generated by SHA256 hashing the JSON body and then building a SHA256 HMAC with the body hash as the data/content and your webhook secret as the key.

Your webhook secret is displayed on the **Developers** > **Webhooks** > **Endpoints** page. Please see our example code snippets below of how to generate the signature.

PHP

Node.js (Express)

If the signature that you generate doesn't match the **X-Signature** header, please disregard the webhook because it is not from Tebex.

circle-info

Some frameworks such as Express (Node.js) automatically parse JSON request bodies which can result in a signature mismatch. Please ensure the signature is calculated using the raw request body and not a parsed version of the body.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/webhooks/overview#handling-webhooks)

Handling Webhooks


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

All of our webhooks are sent using the standardised format with the following properties:

**id**: This property represents the unique ID of the webhook. [**type**](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/webhooks/overview#webhook-types)
: The type of webhook we are sending, for example _payment.completed_. **date**: This is the date that the webhook was generated. [**subject**](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/webhooks/overview#webhook-subjects)
: The data within this property will differ depending on the _type_ of webhook. To view the different subject formats please see the subject types below.

When handling a webhook, please ensure you respond with a 2XX status code (anywhere between 200-299). If your endpoint responds with any other status code we will automatically try to resend the webhook later-on.

After several attempts of retrying we will mark the webhook as failed and your endpoint may require validating again.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/webhooks/overview#webhook-types)

Webhook Types

*   **payment.completed** Sent when a payment is completed.
    
*   **payment.declined** Sent when a payment is declined.
    
*   **payment.refunded** Sent when a payment is refunded.
    
*   **payment.dispute.opened** Sent when a dispute is opened against a payment.
    
*   **payment.dispute.won** Sent when a dispute against a payment is won.
    
*   **payment.dispute.lost** Sent when a dispute against a payment is lost.
    
*   **payment.dispute.closed** Sent when a dispute against a payment is closed.
    
*   **recurring-payment.started** Sent when a recurring payment starts.
    
*   **recurring-payment.renewed** Sent when a recurring payment renews.
    
*   **recurring-payment.ended** Sent when a recurring payment ends and the purchased products should be revoked from the customer.
    
*   **recurring-payment.cancellation.requested** Sent when a customer requests to cancel a recurring payment. The cancellation will take place at the end of the current billing period (i.e. when renewal would typically occur) and a _recurring-payment.ended_ webhook will be sent.
    
*   **recurring-payment.cancellation.aborted** Sent when a customer aborts the outstanding cancellation request. The recurring payment will renew as normal.
    
*   **validation.webhook** Sent when initially adding a new webhook endpoint.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/webhooks/overview#webhook-subjects)

Webhook Subjects

Payment

Recurring Payment

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/webhooks/overview#useful-status-ids)

**Useful Status IDs**

ID

Status

`1`

Complete

`2`

Refund

`3`

Chargeback

`18`

Declined

`19`

Pending Checkout

`21`

Refund Pending

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/webhooks/overview#decline-reasons)

**Decline Reasons**

Code

Message

`rejected`

The payment method was declined by the customers payment method provider. We recommend asking the customer to contact their bank/provider to have this issue resolved.

`fraud_card_issuer`

The payment method was declined by the customers card issuer or their bank due to suspected fraud. We recommend asking the customer to contact their bank to have this issue resolved.

`fraud_tebex`

Tebex implements artificial intelligence to determine if a transaction is fraudulent. Based on the data we have collected, we have decided this transaction to be too risky to accept. Do not tell the customer that they have been blocked due to fraud.

`incorrect_card_information`

The customer has entered incorrect card details during the checkout process. Please advise the customer to try again with the correct details.

`network_failure`

There was a failure in the payment network. Please advise the customer to try again later.

`insufficient_funds`

The payment method was declined due to the customer having insufficient funds.

`fraud_history`

Tebex reviews the fraud history of customers as part of our fraud assessment. Based on the data we have collected, the fraud history of this customer makes this transaction too risky to accept. Do not tell the customer that they have been blocked due to fraud.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/webhooks/overview#useful-status-ids-1)

**Useful Status IDs**

ID

Status

Description

Active

`2`

Active

The recurring payment is active.

check

`3`

Overdue

We couldn't charge the customer for the renewal, but we will automatically retry tomorrow.

check

`4`

Expired

After multiple attempts, we couldn't renew the recurring payment.

`5`

Cancelled

The recurring payment has been cancelled as requested by the creator/customer.

`7`

Pending Downgrade

Only applies to recurring payments for packages in Tiered Categories:

The customer has requested to downgrade their recurring payment to a lower priced package.

check

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/webhooks/overview#testing-webhooks)

Testing Webhooks


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Our webhook testing feature allows you to manually trigger webhooks from your control panel. Please follow the steps below to send a test webhook.

1.  Navigate to **Developers** > **Webhooks** in your control panel.
    
2.  Click the **Send Test** button.
    
3.  Choose the type of webhook you'd like to send.
    
4.  Provide a valid transaction ID if you've selected a payment webhook type, or enter a recurring payment reference if you've chosen a recurring payment webhook type.
    
5.  Click the **Send Test** button.

    var bodyParser = require('body-parser');
    
    var app = express();
    
    app.use(bodyParser.json({
      verify: (req, res, buf) => {
        req.rawBody = buf
      }
    }));
    
    router.post('/webhook', function(req, res, next) {
      const secret = 'xxxxxxxxxxx';
    
      const bodyHash = crypto
          .createHash('sha256')
          .update(req.rawBody.toString(), 'utf-8')
          .digest('hex');
      const finalHash = crypto.createHmac('sha256', secret)
          .update(bodyHash)
          .digest('hex');
      console.log('finalHash', finalHash)
    
      // Compare hash...
    });

# Sidebar Modules | Developers

Modules allow you to add dynamic modules on your store, which you can configure from within your creator panel on the [sidebararrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/sidebar)
 section.

Each modules HTML is configurable in their associated `module.*.html` page (documented onwards).

You can display the modules on your store by printing the modules variable, as seen below:

Copy

    {{ modules|raw }}

circle-info

Please ensure to use the `raw` [filter](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/twig/filters)
, as the `modules` variable contains HTML that will be escaped automatically by TWIG if this filter is not used.

[Previouslayout.htmlchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/pages/layout.html)
[Nextmodule.communitygoal.htmlchevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/sidebar-modules/module.communitygoal.html)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Endpoints | Developers

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/endpoints#get-accounts-token)

Fetch a webstore by its identifier

get

https://headless.tebex.io/api/accounts/{token}

Gets the webstore associated with the provided identifier.

Path parameters

tokenstringRequired

The webstore identifier.

Example: `some-uuid`

Responses

chevron-right

200

Successful response returns the webstore's information.

application/json

Responseobject

Wrapped webstore information in a "data" object.

get

The webstore identifier.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/endpoints#post-accounts-token-baskets)

Create a new basket

post

https://headless.tebex.io/api/accounts/{token}/baskets

Creates a new basket for use during checkout.

Path parameters

tokenstringRequired

The webstore identifier.

Example: `t66x-7cd928b1e9312709e6810edac6dc1fd1eefc57cb`

Body

application/jsonchevron-down

application/json

complete\_urlstringOptional

A URL the user can return to when checkout is completed.

Example: `https://example.tebex.io/thank-you`

cancel\_urlstringOptional

A URL the user can return to when cancelling checkout.

Example: `https://tebex.io/`

customobjectOptional

Custom data you wish to associate with the basket. This data will be included with webhook responses and GET requests associated with the Basket.

Example: `{"foo":"bar"}`

complete\_auto\_redirectbooleanOptional

True if the user should automatically be redirected to the relevant complete/cancel URL

Example: `true`

Responses

chevron-right

200

Successful response returns the basket information.

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

chevron-right

422

The provided webstore ID is invalid.

post

/accounts/{token}/baskets

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

200

Successful response returns the basket information.

chevron-down

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/endpoints#get-accounts-token-baskets-basketident-auth-returnurl-returnurl)

Get authentication links for a basket.

get

https://headless.tebex.io/api/accounts/{token}/baskets/{basketIdent}/auth?returnUrl={returnUrl}

Fetches a basket's auth URL.

Path parameters

tokenstringRequired

The webstore identifier.

Example: `t66x-7cd928b1e9312709e6810edac6dc1fd1eefc57cb`

basketIdentstringRequired

The basket identifier.

Example: `c00244-d2ac2e77418a55b25292a6bc7a719ad9c529ba2c`

returnUrlstringRequired

The URL you would like to redirect the user to after successful basket authentication.

Example: `https://example.tebex.io/`

Responses

chevron-right

200

Successful response returns the basket auth information.

application/json

Responseobject\[\]

Show propertiesplus

chevron-right

422

The provided webstore ID or basket ID is invalid.

get

/accounts/{token}/baskets/{basketIdent}/auth?returnUrl={returnUrl}

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

Test it

200

Successful response returns the basket auth information.

chevron-down

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/endpoints#category-and-package-retrieval)

Category and Package Retrieval

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/endpoints#get-accounts-token-categories)

Gets all categories available in the webstore.

get

https://headless.tebex.io/api/accounts/{token}/categories

Gets all categories from a webstore. This does not include package information. To include package information, add `?includePackages=1` to the URL.

Path parameters

tokenstringRequired

The webstore identifier.

Example: `t66x-7cd928b1e9312709e6810edac6dc1fd1eefc57cb`

Responses

chevron-right

200

Successful response returns a list of category information.

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

get

/accounts/{token}/categories

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

Test it

200

Successful response returns a list of category information.

*   [POSTAdd a package to a basket](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/endpoints#post-baskets-basketident-packages)
    
*   [POSTRemove a package from a basket](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/endpoints#post-baskets-basketident-packages-remove)
    
*   [PUTUpdates the quantity of the given package in the basket. The user must be logged in before the quantity can be changed.](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/endpoints#put-baskets-basketident-packages-packageid)
    
*   [PATCHUpdates the given tier to the provided package.](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/endpoints#patch-accounts-token-tiers-tierid)
    
*   [Sidebar](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/endpoints#sidebar)
    
*   [GETRetrieves the available sidebar modules.](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/endpoints#get-accounts-token-sidebar)

---

# Overview | Developers

The Checkout API is designed to allow creators to use Tebex's Merchant of Record platform without the need to use a Tebex-powered webstore.

If you haven't already done so, we recommend having a read of our [quick start guide](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/getting-started)
 before beginning integration.

This means creators can create baskets with **custom products** (as opposed to **pre-created** products on our webstore platform), and send customers directly to the checkout flow to proceed with payment.

The Checkout API can be used with [Tebex.js](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/overview)
 for a fully embedded checkout experience without the user ever leaving your own website.

**Using the Checkout API requires prior approval from our compliance teams. Please note that the Checkout API is not available to some UGC creators, such as those on FiveM or RedM.**

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#terminology)

Terminology


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Term

Description

Basket

To start a transaction, a basket must be created. The basket, similar to a standard eCommerce basket will contain the items that the customer is purchasing

Ident

A string identifier representing the basket

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#checkout-api-flow)

Checkout API Flow


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Below is the expected flow your application should follow when implementing the Checkout API. This should be considered a general guideline. For a full list of endpoints available, see the [Endpoints](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/endpoints)
 page.

You have two options for implementing Checkout API. We include a **Checkout** request where all data about the customer and their desired packages can be provided in one request.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#option-1.-using-the-checkout-request)

Option 1. Using the Checkout Request

If your app has existing basket functionality, we recommend using a **Checkout** request. You can send the details of your customer, basket, and sale information all in one request:

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#post-checkout)

Create a checkout request

post

https://checkout.tebex.io/api/checkout

This API call allows the complete checkout flow (create basket, add items, add sale) to be made in a single API call, for when the Seller is managing the basket locally. **This endpoint requires prior approval - please contact your account manager.**

Authorizations

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basicchevron-down

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basic

AuthorizationstringRequired

Body

application/jsonchevron-down

application/json

basketobjectRequired

An object containing the customer's information, relevant links, and any custom tracking data.

Example: `{"first_name":"Neil","last_name":"McNeil","email":"[[email protected]](https://docs.tebex.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection) ","return_url":"https://tebex.io","complete_url":"https://tebex.io","custom":{"foo":"bar","trackingId":127,"list":["1","2","3"]}}`

Show propertiesplus

itemsobject\[\]Required

An array of `Packages` in the basket.

Show propertiesplus

saleobjectOptional

Show propertiesplus

Responses

chevron-right

200

Successfully created basket. The basket will be returned with `links` containing the URLs you should direct the customer to in order to complete payment.

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

chevron-right

400

Bad Request. See ErrorResponse.

post

/checkout

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

Test it

200

Successfully created basket. The basket will be returned with `links` containing the URLs you should direct the customer to in order to complete payment.

chevron-down

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#option-2.-using-the-tebex-basket)

Option 2. Using the Tebex Basket

If you do not have existing basket functionality in your app, you can use the Checkout API to fully manage the customer's basket on Tebex:

1.  Create a basket for the customer.
    
    *   Your app should save the `ident` value for reference later, as this is the identifier for this customer's basket.
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#post-baskets)

Create a basket that can be used to pay for items

post

https://checkout.tebex.io/api/baskets

This will create and return a `Basket` that can be paid for by redirecting the user to `links.checkout`

Authorizations

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basicchevron-down

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basic

AuthorizationstringRequired

Body

application/jsonchevron-down

application/json

return\_urlstringOptional

The URL a customer can return to without completing checkout

Example: `https://example.tebex.io/`

complete\_urlstringOptional

URL the customer can return to after completing payment

Example: `https://example.tebex.io/complete`

customobjectOptional

Any custom data to be passed through the request. This will be returned in a post-completion webhook.

Example: `{"foo":"bar"}`

first\_namestringOptional

The first name of the customer

Example: `Neil`

last\_namestringOptional

The last name of the customer

Example: `McNeil`

emailstringOptional

The email address of the customer

Example: `[[email protected]](https://docs.tebex.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection) `

expires\_atstringOptional

An ISO8601 formatted date. After this date the basket cannot be used to checkout.

Example: `2025-01-27T18:09:51Z`

complete\_auto\_redirectbooleanOptional

Automatically redirect to the complete\_url provided

Example: `true`

countrystringOptional

An ISO 3166-1 alpha-2 character code representing the customer's country.

Example: `US`

creator\_codestringOptional

The creator code is used to share a percentage of the payment with another party. See more about creator codes at [https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/creator-codes](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/creator-codes)

ipstringOptional

The IP address of the customer using this basket. Provide the IP if creating a basket on your server backend.

Example: `1.2.3.4`

Responses

chevron-right

200

Basket created successfully

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

post

/baskets

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

Test it

200

Basket created successfully

1.  Add or remove packages from the customer's basket as desired.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#post-baskets-ident-packages)

Add a package to the basket

post

https://checkout.tebex.io/api/baskets/{ident}/packages

This adds a package (an object describing the product) to the basket `{ident}`. For subscriptions, **only one subscription item may be in a basket at a time**, and it cannot be included with one-time payment items. **This endpoint requires prior approval. Please contact your account manager.**

Authorizations

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basicchevron-down

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basic

AuthorizationstringRequired

Path parameters

identstringRequired

The basket identifier.

Example: `1a-55fff4107740a1f40d844ff89607557f45bfafb3`

Body

application/jsonchevron-down

application/json

packageobjectOptional

Show propertiesplus

qtyintegerOptional

The quantity of `package` in this basket. This is not the total quantity of overall items in the basket.

Example: `2`

typestring · enumOptional

The type of payment, either `single` for one-time payments or `subscription`.

Example: `single`Possible values: `single``subscription`

revenue\_shareobject\[\]Optional

An array of payment destination objects describing how the purchase should be split between multiple wallets. **Only available with pre-agreement from Tebex.**

Show propertiesplus

Responses

chevron-right

200

Package is successfully added to the basket, and basket is returned.

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

chevron-right

400

Improperly formatted package. See ErrorResponse.

chevron-right

404

Basket not found.

post

/baskets/{ident}/packages

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

Test it

200

Package is successfully added to the basket, and basket is returned.

chevron-down

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#delete-baskets-ident-packages-rows.id)

Remove a row from the basket

delete

https://checkout.tebex.io/api/baskets/{ident}/packages/{rows.id}

This will remove the given `{rows.id}` from the basket `{ident}`. The basket must be re-fetched after running to receive updated totals.

Authorizations

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basicchevron-down

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basic

AuthorizationstringRequired

Path parameters

identstringRequired

The basket identifier.

Example: `1a-55fff4107740a1f40d844ff89607557f45bfafb3`

rows.idintegerRequired

The `id` of the `basket.rows` row to remove.

Example: `1`

Responses

chevron-right

204

Successfully deleted a row from the basket.

chevron-right

404

Row or basket not found.

delete

/baskets/{ident}/packages/{rows.id}

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

Test it

204

Successfully deleted a row from the basket.

chevron-down

No content

1.  Add any desired sales / discounts to the basket
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#post-baskets-ident-sales)

Add a sale to the basket

post

https://checkout.tebex.io/api/baskets/{ident}/sales

Adds a `Sale` to the basket with `{ident}`. **Sales cannot be applied to baskets with `revenue_share` set.**

Authorizations

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basicchevron-down

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basic

AuthorizationstringRequired

Path parameters

identstringRequired

The basket identifier.

Example: `1a-55fff4107740a1f40d844ff89607557f45bfafb3`

Body

application/jsonchevron-down

application/json

namestringOptional

The name of the sale (displayed to the customer)

Example: `Test Sale`

discount\_typestring · enumOptional

The type of discount, either `percentage` for deducting a percentage of each item, or `amount` to deduct a fixed amount from each item.

Example: `amount`Possible values: `percentage``amount`

amountnumberOptional

The amount or percentage to deduct

Example: `4.99`

Responses

chevron-right

200

Successfully adds sale to basket.

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

chevron-right

400

Bad request. Improperly formatted Sale or this basket cannot accept sales. See ErrorResponse.

chevron-right

404

Basket not found.

post

/baskets/{ident}/sales

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

Test it

200

Successfully adds sale to basket.

chevron-down

1.  Direct the user to the basket's `links.checkout` URL in order to complete payment.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#get-baskets-ident)

Fetch a basket by its identifier

get

https://checkout.tebex.io/api/baskets/{ident}

Gets the basket associated with the provided identifier.

Authorizations

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basicchevron-down

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basic

AuthorizationstringRequired

Path parameters

identstringRequired

The basket identifier.

Example: `1a-55fff4107740a1f40d844ff89607557f45bfafb3`

Responses

chevron-right

200

Successful response returns the basket.

The `links.payment` property is only returned if the basket has been paid for, and a payment exist with the **complete**/**refund**/**chargeback** status.

The `links.checkout` property is only returned if the basket has not been paid, and is the URL to send the customer to in order to complete payment.

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

chevron-right

404

Basket not found.

get

/baskets/{ident}

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

Test it

200

Successful response returns the basket.

The `links.payment` property is only returned if the basket has been paid for, and a payment exist with the **complete**/**refund**/**chargeback** status.

The `links.checkout` property is only returned if the basket has not been paid, and is the URL to send the customer to in order to complete payment.

chevron-down

1.  After payment is complete, you may verify payment if you wish by checking the `links.payment` URL associated with the customer's basket.
    

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#recurring-payments)

Recurring Payments


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Tebex Checkout supports recurring payments in addition to single, one-time payments. Below are the endpoints you can use for managing a customer's recurring payments.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#get-recurring-payments-reference)

Fetch a recurring payment (subscription) by its reference

get

https://checkout.tebex.io/api/recurring-payments/{reference}

Authorizations

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basicchevron-down

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basic

AuthorizationstringRequired

Path parameters

referencestringRequired

The recurring payment reference to fetch.

Example: `tbx-r-55fff4107740a1f40d844ff89607557f45bfafb3`

Responses

chevron-right

200

Successfully fetched recurring payment.

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

chevron-right

404

Recurring payment not found.

get

/recurring-payments/{reference}

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

Test it

200

Successfully fetched recurring payment.

chevron-down

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#put-recurring-payments-reference)

Update a subscription with a new product / amount to pay - replacing the existing product

put

https://checkout.tebex.io/api/recurring-payments/{reference}

If the new subscription amount is higher than the existing amount, a pro-rata charge will be made to cover the cost of the new price up until the next billing date.

**This endpoint requires prior approval - please contact your account manager.**

Authorizations

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basicchevron-down

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basic

AuthorizationstringRequired

Path parameters

referencestringRequired

The recurring payment reference to fetch.

Example: `tbx-r-55fff4107740a1f40d844ff89607557f45bfafb3`

Body

application/jsonchevron-down

application/json

itemsobject\[\]Optional

An array containing the items to be added to the recurring payment. **Only 1 item is supported at this time.**

Show propertiesplus

Responses

chevron-right

200

Successfully updated subscription. The updated `RecurringPayment` is returned.

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

chevron-right

400

Bad Request.

chevron-right

404

Recurring payment not found.

put

/recurring-payments/{reference}

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

Test it

200

Successfully updated subscription. The updated `RecurringPayment` is returned.

chevron-down

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#delete-recurring-payments-reference)

Cancel a recurring payment

delete

https://checkout.tebex.io/api/recurring-payments/{reference}

This cancels the recurring payment for the reference provided. Recurring payment references start with `tbx-r-`

Authorizations

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basicchevron-down

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basic

AuthorizationstringRequired

Path parameters

referencestringRequired

The recurring payment reference to cancel.

Example: `tbx-r-55fff4107740a1f40d844ff89607557f45bfafb3`

Responses

chevron-right

200

Recurring payment cancelled successfully.

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

chevron-right

404

Recurring payment not found.

delete

/recurring-payments/{reference}

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

Test it

200

Recurring payment cancelled successfully.

chevron-down

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#put-recurring-payments-reference-status)

Pause or reactivate a recurring payment

put

https://checkout.tebex.io/api/recurring-payments/{reference}/status

Authorizations

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basicchevron-down

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basic

AuthorizationstringRequired

Path parameters

referencestringRequired

The recurring payment reference to update.

Example: `tbx-r-55fff4107740a1f40d844ff89607557f45bfafb3`

Body

application/jsonchevron-down

application/json

statusstring · enumRequired

Your desired state of the recurring payment. Provide `Paused` with `paused_until` to pause a recurring payment. Otherwise, provide `Active` to resume a recurring payment.

Example: `Paused`Possible values: `Paused``Active`

paused\_untilstringOptional

To pause a payment, provide a ISO8601 formatted date on which the payment should be reactivated.

Example: `2025-01-27T16:43:53.000000Z`

Responses

chevron-right

200

Successfully paused or reactivated a payment. The `RecurringPayment` is returned.

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

chevron-right

404

Recurring payment not found.

chevron-right

422

Unprocessible Entity. An invalid status was provided or the recurring payment cannot be processed. See ErrorResponse.

put

/recurring-payments/{reference}/status

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

Test it

200

Successfully paused or reactivated a payment. The `RecurringPayment` is returned.

chevron-down

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#openapi-schema-and-sdks)

OpenAPI Schema and SDKs


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Tebex Checkout is documented with OpenAPI. To view the schema and available SDKs, see our [releasesarrow-up-right](https://github.com/tebexio/TebexCheckout-OpenAPI/releases)
 on GitHub.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#postman-schema)

Postman Schema


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

An importable Postman collection can always be downloaded from [Tebex Checkout's repositoryarrow-up-right](https://github.com/tebexio/TebexCheckout-OpenAPI/releases)
 on GitHub.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#examples)

*   [Terminology](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#terminology)
    
*   [Checkout API Flow](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#checkout-api-flow)
    
*   [Option 1. Using the Checkout Request](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#option-1.-using-the-checkout-request)
    
*   [POSTCreate a checkout request](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#post-checkout)
    
*   [Option 2. Using the Tebex Basket](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#option-2.-using-the-tebex-basket)
    
*   [POSTCreate a basket that can be used to pay for items](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#post-baskets)
    
*   [POSTAdd a package to the basket](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#post-baskets-ident-packages)
    
*   [DELETERemove a row from the basket](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#delete-baskets-ident-packages-rows.id)
    
*   [POSTAdd a sale to the basket](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#post-baskets-ident-sales)
    
*   [GETFetch a basket by its identifier](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#get-baskets-ident)
    
*   [Recurring Payments](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#recurring-payments)
    
*   [GETFetch a recurring payment (subscription) by its reference](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#get-recurring-payments-reference)
    
*   [PUTUpdate a subscription with a new product / amount to pay - replacing the existing product](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#put-recurring-payments-reference)
    
*   [DELETECancel a recurring payment](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#delete-recurring-payments-reference)
    
*   [PUTPause or reactivate a recurring payment](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#put-recurring-payments-reference-status)
    
*   [OpenAPI Schema and SDKs](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#openapi-schema-and-sdks)
    
*   [Postman Schema](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#postman-schema)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/overview#examples)

    Content-Type: application/json
    Accept: */*
    Content-Length: 330

      "basket": {
        "first_name": "Neil",
        "last_name": "McNeil",

            "revenue_share": [],\
            "image": null,\
            "realprice": 1.27\
          },\
          "custom": null,\
          "image_url": null,\
          "recurring_price": null\
        }\
      ],
      "fingerprint": "",
      "creator_code": "text",
      "roundup": false,
      "cancel_url": "https://tebex.io",
      "complete_url": null,
      "complete_auto_redirect": false,
      "custom": {
        "foo": "bar",
        "ref": 1234
      },

        "payment": "https://checkout.tebex.io/api/payments/tbx-12345",
        "checkout": "https://checkout.tebex.io/checkout/1a-55fff4107740a1f40d844ff89607557f45bfafb3"
      }
    }

# Endpoints | Developers

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/endpoints#get-baskets-ident)

Fetch a basket by its identifier

get

https://checkout.tebex.io/api/baskets/{ident}

Gets the basket associated with the provided identifier.

Authorizations

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basicchevron-down

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basic

AuthorizationstringRequired

Path parameters

identstringRequired

The basket identifier.

Example: `1a-55fff4107740a1f40d844ff89607557f45bfafb3`

Responses

chevron-right

200

Successful response returns the basket.

The `links.payment` property is only returned if the basket has been paid for, and a payment exist with the **complete**/**refund**/**chargeback** status.

The `links.checkout` property is only returned if the basket has not been paid, and is the URL to send the customer to in order to complete payment.

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

chevron-right

404

Basket not found.

get

/baskets/{ident}

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

Test it

200

Successful response returns the basket.

The `links.payment` property is only returned if the basket has been paid for, and a payment exist with the **complete**/**refund**/**chargeback** status.

The `links.checkout` property is only returned if the basket has not been paid, and is the URL to send the customer to in order to complete payment.

chevron-down

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/endpoints#post-baskets)

Create a basket that can be used to pay for items

post

https://checkout.tebex.io/api/baskets

This will create and return a `Basket` that can be paid for by redirecting the user to `links.checkout`

Authorizations

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basicchevron-down

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basic

AuthorizationstringRequired

Body

application/jsonchevron-down

application/json

return\_urlstringOptional

The URL a customer can return to without completing checkout

Example: `https://example.tebex.io/`

complete\_urlstringOptional

URL the customer can return to after completing payment

Example: `https://example.tebex.io/complete`

customobjectOptional

Any custom data to be passed through the request. This will be returned in a post-completion webhook.

Example: `{"foo":"bar"}`

first\_namestringOptional

The first name of the customer

Example: `Neil`

last\_namestringOptional

The last name of the customer

Example: `McNeil`

emailstringOptional

The email address of the customer

Example: `[[email protected]](https://docs.tebex.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection) `

complete\_auto\_redirectbooleanOptional

Automatically redirect to the complete\_url provided

Example: `true`

countrystringOptional

An ISO 3166-1 alpha-2 character code representing the customer's country.

Example: `US`

creator\_codestringOptional

The creator code is used to share a percentage of the payment with another party. See more about creator codes at [https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/creator-codes](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/creator-codes)

ipstringOptional

The IP address of the customer using this basket. Provide the IP if creating a basket on your server backend.

Example: `1.2.3.4`

Responses

chevron-right

200

Basket created successfully

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

post

/baskets

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

Test it

200

Basket created successfully

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/endpoints#post-baskets-ident-packages)

Add a package to the basket

post

https://checkout.tebex.io/api/baskets/{ident}/packages

This adds a package (an object describing the product) to the basket `{ident}`. For subscriptions, **only one subscription item may be in a basket at a time**, and it cannot be included with one-time payment items. **This endpoint requires prior approval. Please contact your account manager.**

Authorizations

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basicchevron-down

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basic

AuthorizationstringRequired

Path parameters

identstringRequired

The basket identifier.

Example: `1a-55fff4107740a1f40d844ff89607557f45bfafb3`

Body

application/jsonchevron-down

application/json

packageobjectOptional

Show propertiesplus

qtyintegerOptional

The quantity of `package` in this basket. This is not the total quantity of overall items in the basket.

Example: `2`

typestring · enumOptional

The type of payment, either `single` for one-time payments or `subscription`.

Example: `single`Possible values: `single``subscription`

revenue\_shareobject\[\]Optional

An array of payment destination objects describing how the purchase should be split between multiple wallets. **Only available with pre-agreement from Tebex.**

Show propertiesplus

Responses

chevron-right

200

Package is successfully added to the basket, and basket is returned.

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

chevron-right

400

Improperly formatted package. See ErrorResponse.

chevron-right

404

Basket not found.

post

/baskets/{ident}/packages

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

Test it

200

Package is successfully added to the basket, and basket is returned.

chevron-down

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/endpoints#delete-baskets-ident-packages-rows.id)

Remove a row from the basket

delete

https://checkout.tebex.io/api/baskets/{ident}/packages/{rows.id}

This will remove the given `{rows.id}` from the basket `{ident}`. The basket must be re-fetched after running to receive updated totals.

Authorizations

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basicchevron-down

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basic

AuthorizationstringRequired

Path parameters

identstringRequired

The basket identifier.

Example: `1a-55fff4107740a1f40d844ff89607557f45bfafb3`

rows.idintegerRequired

The `id` of the `basket.rows` row to remove.

Example: `1`

Responses

chevron-right

204

Successfully deleted a row from the basket.

chevron-right

404

Row or basket not found.

delete

/baskets/{ident}/packages/{rows.id}

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

Test it

204

Successfully deleted a row from the basket.

chevron-down

No content

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/endpoints#post-baskets-ident-sales)

Add a sale to the basket

post

https://checkout.tebex.io/api/baskets/{ident}/sales

Adds a `Sale` to the basket with `{ident}`. **Sales cannot be applied to baskets with** `**revenue_share**` **set.**

Authorizations

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basicchevron-down

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basic

AuthorizationstringRequired

Path parameters

identstringRequired

The basket identifier.

Example: `1a-55fff4107740a1f40d844ff89607557f45bfafb3`

Body

application/jsonchevron-down

application/json

namestringOptional

The name of the sale (displayed to the customer)

Example: `Test Sale`

discount\_typestring · enumOptional

The type of discount, either `percentage` for deducting a percentage of each item, or `amount` to deduct a fixed amount from each item.

Example: `amount`Possible values: `percentage``amount`

amountnumberOptional

The amount or percentage to deduct

Example: `4.99`

Responses

chevron-right

200

Successfully adds sale to basket.

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

chevron-right

400

Bad request. Improperly formatted Sale or this basket cannot accept sales. See ErrorResponse.

chevron-right

404

Basket not found.

post

/baskets/{ident}/sales

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/endpoints#post-checkout)

Create a checkout request

post

https://checkout.tebex.io/api/checkout

This API call allows the complete checkout flow (create basket, add items, add sale) to be made in a single API call, for when the Seller is managing the basket locally. **This endpoint requires prior approval - please contact your account manager.**

Authorizations

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basicchevron-down

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basic

AuthorizationstringRequired

Body

application/jsonchevron-down

application/json

basketobjectRequired

An object containing the customer's information, relevant links, and any custom tracking data.

Example: `{"first_name":"Neil","last_name":"McNeil","email":"[[email protected]](https://docs.tebex.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection) ","return_url":"https://tebex.io","complete_url":"https://tebex.io","custom":{"foo":"bar","trackingId":127,"list":["1","2","3"]}}`

Show propertiesplus

itemsobject\[\]Required

An array of `Packages` in the basket.

Show propertiesplus

saleobjectOptional

Show propertiesplus

Responses

chevron-right

200

Successfully created basket. The basket will be returned with `links` containing the URLs you should direct the customer to in order to complete payment.

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

chevron-right

400

Bad Request. See ErrorResponse.

post

/checkout

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

Test it

Payment refunded successfully. The payment details are returned.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/endpoints#put-recurring-payments-reference)

Update a subscription with a new product / amount to pay - replacing the existing product

put

https://checkout.tebex.io/api/recurring-payments/{reference}

If the new subscription amount is higher than the existing amount, a pro-rata charge will be made to cover the cost of the new price up until the next billing date.

**This endpoint requires prior approval - please contact your account manager.**

Authorizations

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basicchevron-down

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basic

AuthorizationstringRequired

Path parameters

referencestringRequired

The recurring payment reference to fetch.

Example: `tbx-r-55fff4107740a1f40d844ff89607557f45bfafb3`

Body

application/jsonchevron-down

application/json

itemsobject\[\]Optional

An array containing the items to be added to the recurring payment. **Only 1 item is supported at this time.**

Show propertiesplus

Responses

chevron-right

200

Successfully updated subscription. The updated `RecurringPayment` is returned.

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

chevron-right

400

Bad Request.

chevron-right

404

Recurring payment not found.

put

/recurring-payments/{reference}

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

Test it

200

Successfully updated subscription. The updated `RecurringPayment` is returned.

chevron-down

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/endpoints#put-recurring-payments-reference-status)

Pause or reactivate a recurring payment

put

https://checkout.tebex.io/api/recurring-payments/{reference}/status

Authorizations

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basicchevron-down

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basic

AuthorizationstringRequired

Path parameters

referencestringRequired

The recurring payment reference to update.

Example: `tbx-r-55fff4107740a1f40d844ff89607557f45bfafb3`

Body

application/jsonchevron-down

application/json

statusstring · enumRequired

Your desired state of the recurring payment. Provide `Paused` with `paused_until` to pause a recurring payment. Otherwise, provide `Active` to resume a recurring payment.

Example: `Paused`Possible values: `Paused``Active`

paused\_untilstringOptional

To pause a payment, provide a ISO8601 formatted date on which the payment should be reactivated.

Example: `2025-01-27T16:43:53.000000Z`

Responses

chevron-right

200

Successfully paused or reactivated a payment. The `RecurringPayment` is returned.

application/json

Responseobject

Show propertiesplus

chevron-right

404

Recurring payment not found.

chevron-right

422

Unprocessible Entity. An invalid status was provided or the recurring payment cannot be processed. See ErrorResponse.

put

/recurring-payments/{reference}/status

HTTPchevron-down

HTTPcURLJavaScriptPython

Test it

200

Successfully paused or reactivated a payment. The `RecurringPayment` is returned.

chevron-down

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/endpoints#put-baskets-ident)

Update a basket's details, including expiry date.

put

https://checkout.tebex.io/api/baskets/{ident}

This will update the customer's details on the basket. If the customer is already logged in and a new email is provided, they will be logged out.

Authorizations

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basicchevron-down

tebex\_checkout\_auth\_basic

AuthorizationstringRequired

Path parameters

identstringRequired

The basket identifier.

Example: `1a-55fff4107740a1f40d844ff89607557f45bfafb3`

Body

application/jsonchevron-down

application/json

countrystring · nullableOptional

namestring · nullableOptional

state\_idstring · nullableOptional

first\_namestring · nullableOptional

last\_namestring · nullableOptional

postal\_codestring · nullableOptional

creator\_codestring · nullableOptional

complete\_auto\_redirectboolean · nullableOptional

expires\_atstring · date-time · nullableOptional

An ISO8601 formatted date. After this date the basket cannot be used to checkout.

Example: `2025-01-27T18:09:51Z`

Responses

chevron-right

200

Basket updated successfully

No content

chevron-right

404

Basket not found.

/baskets/{ident}

*   [DELETERemove a row from the basket](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/endpoints#delete-baskets-ident-packages-rows.id)
    
*   [POSTAdd a sale to the basket](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/endpoints#post-baskets-ident-sales)
    
*   [POSTCreate a checkout request](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/endpoints#post-checkout)
    
*   [GETFetch a payment by its transaction ID](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/endpoints#get-payments-txnid-type-txn_id)
    
*   [POSTRefund a payment by its transaction ID](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/endpoints#post-payments-txnid-refund-type-txn_id)
    
*   [GETFetch a recurring payment (subscription) by its reference](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/endpoints#get-recurring-payments-reference)
    
*   [PUTUpdate a subscription with a new product / amount to pay - replacing the existing product](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/endpoints#put-recurring-payments-reference)
    
*   [DELETECancel a recurring payment](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/endpoints#delete-recurring-payments-reference)
    
*   [PUTPause or reactivate a recurring payment](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/endpoints#put-recurring-payments-reference-status)
    
*   [PUTUpdate a basket's details, including expiry date.](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/checkout-api/endpoints#put-baskets-ident)

    GET /api/baskets/{ident} HTTP/1.1
    Host: checkout.tebex.io
    Authorization: Basic username:password
    Accept: */*

# Tebex Control Panel | Creators

The **Tebex Control Panel** provides a user-friendly interface and a comprehensive set of tools allowing **creators and game studios** to efficiently manage and grow their online businesses.

Use this guide to explore each key section of the platform.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel#dashboard-and-payments)

*   [Dashboardarrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/dashboard)
    
*   [Paymentsarrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/payments)
    
*   [Manual Paymentsarrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/payments/manual-payments)
    
*   [Recurring Paymentsarrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/payments/recurring-payments)
    
*   [Payment Methodsarrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/payments/payment-methods)
    
*   [Fraud Analysisarrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/payments/fraud-analysis)
    
*   [Tebex Walletsarrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/payments/wallet)
    
*   [Payment Exportsarrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/payments/payment-exports)

# Supporting Package Media on Custom Store Templates | Developers

If you’re using a custom or legacy store template, you may not see all package images (when multiple images are uploaded) or the package video.

If you are using the Exo template, this guide does not apply.

Older templates relied on the `package.image` property to display a package’s image URL. To support package media properly, you now need to use the new `package.media` array instead. See the example code snippet below demonstrating how to use the new media array.

Copy

    {% for media in package.media %}
      <div class="slide">
        {% if media.type == 'image' %}
          <img
            class="slide-image"
            src="{{ media.url }}"
            alt="{{ package.name }}"
          />
        {% elseif media.type == 'video' %}
          <iframe
            class="slide-frame"
            src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/{{ media.url }}?color=white&amp;rel=0"
            title="YouTube video player"
            frameborder="0"
            allow="accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture; web-share"
            referrerpolicy="strict-origin-when-cross-origin"
            allowfullscreen
          ></iframe>
        {% endif %}
      </div>
    {% endfor %}

[PreviousSupporting Tiers on Custom Store Templateschevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/guides/supporting-tiers-on-custom-store-templates)
[NextOverviewchevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/headless-api/overview)

Last updated 4 months ago

# How Payments Work | Creators

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/how-payments-work#stage-1-customer-makes-a-purchase)

Stage 1: Customer Makes a Purchase

When a customer completes a payment:

*   Any **automatic delivery actions** are triggered immediately (e.g., game server commands, webhooks, RCON commands—based on your setup).
    
*   You’ll receive an **email notification** confirming the purchase.
    
*   **Gateway fees** and **platform fees** are deducted automatically.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/how-payments-work#fee-details)

Fee Details

*   **Gateway Fees**: Charged by the payment provider. Varies by method (e.g., PayPal, iDEAL, card). ➤ [View gateway fees by payment methodarrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/payment-methods)
    
*   **Platform Fees**: Charged by Tebex to support development, platform maintenance, and fraud protection. ➤ [View platform fees by game/store typearrow-up-right](https://www.tebex.io/pricing-for-game-servers)
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/how-payments-work#stage-2-funds-settle-in-your-tebex-wallet)

Stage 2: Funds Settle in Your Tebex Wallet

After the purchase, funds enter a **settlement period** before becoming available for withdrawal.

*   **Average settlement time**: 14 days (can vary by payment method) ➤ [See settlement timesarrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/payment-methods)
    
*   During settlement, your funds remain in your **Tebex Wallet**.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/how-payments-work#wallet-setup)

Wallet Setup

*   Ensure your **withdrawal methods** (PayPal, bank account, wire transfer) are correctly added.
    
*   Updating withdrawal info may require additional verification. ➤ [How to manage your wallet and withdrawal methodsarrow-up-right](https://app.gitbook.com/s/k6TR7SuepunW7QJVY0dc)
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/how-payments-work#stage-3-requesting-a-payout)

🧾 Stage 3: Requesting a Payout

Once funds appear in your **settled balance**, you can request a withdrawal:

*   **Minimum payout**: Starts at USD $5 (varies by method)
    
*   **Withdrawal fees**: Start from approximately USD $0.50 ➤ [View withdrawal fees by methodarrow-up-right](https://wallet.tebex.io/withdraw)
    

> **Tip**: PayPal is usually the cheapest withdrawal option.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/how-payments-work#stage-4-money-received)

Stage 4: Money Received

After your payout is approved:

*   Funds are transferred to your **PayPal or bank account**
    
*   Transfer times depend on method, ranging from **instant to 7 working days**
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/how-payments-work#summary)

Summary

Stage

Description

1\. Customer Purchase

Payment is received; fees deducted; items delivered

2\. Wallet Settlement

Funds settle in your Tebex Wallet

3\. Withdrawal Request

You request a payout after settlement

4\. Money Received

Funds arrive in your PayPal or bank account

[PreviousTebex Checkoutchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout)
[NextSeller Protection and Chargebackschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/seller-protection-and-chargebacks)

Last updated 6 months ago

*   [Stage 2: Funds Settle in Your Tebex Wallet](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/how-payments-work#stage-2-funds-settle-in-your-tebex-wallet)
    
*   [🧾 Stage 3: Requesting a Payout](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/how-payments-work#stage-3-requesting-a-payout)
    
*   [Stage 4: Money Received](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/how-payments-work#stage-4-money-received)

# Starter & Plus Plans | Creators

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/pricing-overview/starter-and-plus-plans#free-90-day-trial-of-tebex-plus)

**Free 90-Day Trial of Tebex Plus**

All new Tebex Stores come with a **free 90-day trial** of our **Plus Plan**, giving you full access to all premium features — no payment details required.

If your trial has ended and you’d like to continue with Tebex Plus, you can subscribe on the [Plans page.arrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/billing/plans)

*   **Starter Plan (Free):** Everything you need to launch your store and start selling.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/pricing-overview/starter-and-plus-plans#accepted-payment-methods-for-tebex-plus)

**Accepted Payment Methods for Tebex Plus**

You can pay for Tebex Plus using **credit or debit cards** and **PayPal**. However, please note:

*   **PayPal balances** cannot be used for monthly recurring subscriptions due to limitations with PayPal's recurring billing system.
    
*   If you wish to pay **exclusively using PayPal balance**, you can do so by choosing a **prepaid plan** instead of a monthly subscription.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/pricing-overview/starter-and-plus-plans#billing-and-subscription-details)

**Billing & Subscription Details**

*   Subscriptions are billed **monthly** starting from your initial upgrade date. _Example:_ If you upgrade on **June 7**, your next payment will be due on **July 7**.
    
*   You can manage or update your billing method via the Plans page.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/pricing-overview/starter-and-plus-plans#prepaid-plans-save-with-upfront-payments)

**Prepaid Plans: Save with Upfront Payments**

Prepaid plans offer discounted rates for Tebex Plus when you pay for multiple months in advance — ideal for creators and studios planning for the long term.

Plan Length

Price

Savings vs Monthly

3 Months

£33.72

Save 10%

6 Months

£63.70

12 Months

£119.90

Save 20%

You can subscribe as a **new user**, or extend your current plan if you're already using Tebex Plus. Visit the Plans page to subscribe or contact **Creator Support** to switch from monthly to prepaid.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/pricing-overview/starter-and-plus-plans#cancelling-or-downgrading-your-tebex-plus-plan)

**Cancelling or Downgrading Your Tebex Plus Plan**

If you're on a **trial** or currently subscribed to Tebex Plus and decide not to renew, here’s what happens when you downgrade:

*   No data is deleted — your store remains intact.
    
*   Certain features become **read-only**, **inactive**, or **restricted** after downgrade.
    

**Feature**

**Effect After Downgrade**

**Custom Templates**

Read-only; active ones remain functional, but not editable.

**Sales & Coupons**

Read-only; current promotions run until expiry.

**Gift Cards**

Read-only; existing cards work, no new ones can be created.

**Abandoned Basket Recovery**

Access revoked; already sent links still work.

**Purchase Follow-ups**

Access revoked; previously sent discounts still apply.

**Team Accounts**

Deactivated; collaborators lose access.

**Custom Domain**

Reverts to tebex.io subdomain.

**Referral Links**

Stats inaccessible; links continue to function.

> To cancel, visit the [Plans pagearrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/billing/plans)
> , select the **Starter Plan**, and click **"Downgrade"**. Follow the on-screen instructions to complete the process.
