# Tebex Fees & Billing Overview | Creators

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/pricing-overview/tebex-fees-and-billing-overview#table-of-contents)

Table of Contents

1.  Platform Fee
    
2.  Gateway Fees
    
3.  Chargebacks & Disputes
    
4.  Refunds
    
5.  Creator Codes
    
6.  Withdrawals
    
    *   PayPal Withdrawal Fees
        
    *   Local Bank Transfers
        
    *   Wire Transfers
        
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/pricing-overview/tebex-fees-and-billing-overview#id-1.-platform-fee)

1\. Platform Fee

Tebex applies a platform fee on each transaction:

*   **Standard Rate**: 5% of the transaction amount
    
*   **FiveM-Specific Rate**: 15% of the transaction amount
    

This fee is deducted from the transaction before the funds are deposited into your Tebex Wallet. The Platform Fee supports ongoing platform development, customer support, expanded payment infrastructure, and Seller Protection services.

[Learn why we charge a Platform Fee →](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/pricing-overview/tebex-fees-and-billing-overview/tebex-platform-fee-explained)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/pricing-overview/tebex-fees-and-billing-overview#id-2.-gateway-fees)

2\. Gateway Fees

Gateway Fees are charged by third-party payment providers such as PayPal, iDeal, and Klarna. These fees vary based on the payment method selected by the customer.

*   The fee is deducted **before funds reach your Tebex Wallet**.
    
*   Tebex **does not profit** from these fees.
    
*   In some cases (e.g. PayPal), Tebex negotiates **preferential rates**:
    
    *   **PayPal via Tebex**: 2.49% + $0.40 (vs 3.49% + $0.49 standard rate)
        
    

You can choose which payment methods to accept via [**Payments > Payment Methods** arrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/payment-methods)
in your dashboard.

[See full gateway fee list here →arrow-up-right](https://www.tebex.io/payment-methods)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/pricing-overview/tebex-fees-and-billing-overview#id-3.-chargebacks-and-payment-disputes)

3\. Chargebacks & Payment Disputes

Most creators are covered under **Tebex Seller Protection**, meaning:

*   **No chargeback fees**
    
*   **You keep the revenue**, even if the dispute is lost
    
*   **Tebex handles dispute management**
    

If a transaction is not eligible for Seller Protection, you will be notified by email. In such cases:

*   A **$20 chargeback fee** and the transaction amount are withheld during dispute resolution.
    
*   If the dispute is lost, those funds are not returned.
    

[See Section 7 of the Creator Agreement for eligibility →arrow-up-right](https://www.tebex.io/terms-creator-agreement)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/pricing-overview/tebex-fees-and-billing-overview#id-4.-refunds)

4\. Refunds

When a refund is issued:

*   The **original transaction amount** and the **Gateway Fee** are charged from your Tebex Wallet.
    

**Example:**

*   Original payment: $5.00
    
*   Gateway Fee: $0.20
    
*   Total cost on refund: $5.00 + $0.20 (original) + $0.20 (refund fee) = $5.40
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/pricing-overview/tebex-fees-and-billing-overview#id-5.-creator-codes)

5\. Creator Codes

When using Creator Codes to pay influencers:

*   An **additional 1% fee** of the total payment is applied.
    
*   This covers the payout distribution and processing to influencers.
    

This fee is deducted **before payout** to either the creator or influencer.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/pricing-overview/tebex-fees-and-billing-overview#id-6.-withdrawals)

6\. Withdrawals

Withdrawal fees depend on your chosen method, currency, and destination country.

A **2.00% foreign exchange fee** applies if you withdraw in a different currency than your Wallet’s currency.

Rejected/returned withdrawals will **still incur the withdrawal fee**, so double-check your details before requesting.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/pricing-overview/tebex-fees-and-billing-overview#id-6.1-paypal-withdrawal-fees)

6.1 PayPal Withdrawal Fees

Currency

Fee

CAD (Canadian Dollar)

0.50 CAD

USD (US Dollar)

0.50 USD

GBP (British Pound)

0.25 GBP

EUR (Euro)

0.25 EUR

HKD (Hong Kong Dollar)

0.25 HKD

AUD (Australian Dollar)

0.50 AUD

NZD (New Zealand Dollar)

0.50 NZD

SGD (Singapore Dollar)

0.50 SGD

JPY (Japanese Yen)

28.00 JPY

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/pricing-overview/tebex-fees-and-billing-overview#id-6.2-local-bank-account)

6.2 Local Bank Account

Region/Countries

Fee

UK, US, SEPA, Gibraltar, Guernsey, Jersey

£1.50

Australia, Canada, EU countries, Singapore, others

£3.00

Brazil, China, South Africa, Vietnam, etc.

£4.50

India, Japan, Nigeria, UAE, etc.

£5.00

Bulgaria, Jamaica

£12.00

> Some countries only support select currencies for local transfers.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/pricing-overview/tebex-fees-and-billing-overview#id-6.3-wire-transfers)

6.3 Wire Transfers

*   **Flat fee**: £12 per wire transfer
    
*   **Available in 150+ countries**
    
*   Wire transfers are more expensive than local or PayPal options and should be used only when necessary.
    

[Full list of supported wire transfer countries →arrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/pricing-overview/tebex-fees-and-billing-overview/supported-countries-for-wire-transfers)

# Seller Protection and Chargebacks | Creators

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/seller-protection-and-chargebacks#what-is-seller-protection)

What Is Seller Protection?

Seller Protection ensures that if a customer initiates a chargeback or payment dispute, **Tebex will defend it on your behalf**. If the dispute is lost, **you won’t lose the funds**, as long as the transaction is covered under our Seller Protection policy.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/seller-protection-and-chargebacks#key-benefits)

Key Benefits:

*   Chargeback defense handled by Tebex
    
*   No loss of funds on protected transactions
    
*   Peace of mind with fewer manual escalations
    

> ⚠️ Note: Not all payments are eligible. See Eligibility Requirements.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/seller-protection-and-chargebacks#what-is-a-chargeback)

What Is a Chargeback?

A **chargeback** (or dispute) occurs when a customer asks their payment provider to reverse a transaction.

*   The bank investigates the request
    
*   If approved, the payment is returned to the customer
    
*   The merchant (you) may be charged a **dispute fee**
    

Tebex handles this process for eligible transactions and will notify you of any action required.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/seller-protection-and-chargebacks#why-are-chargebacks-a-problem)

Why Are Chargebacks a Problem?

While Tebex shields you financially (if covered), excessive chargebacks may still result in:

*   Store **suspension** or **wallet lock** (typically for 30 days)
    
*   **Fund access restriction** while disputes are active
    
*   Potential **loss of Seller Protection** for repeat violations
    

> Review the [Creator Agreementarrow-up-right](https://www.tebex.io/terms-creator-agreement)
>  and [Acceptable Use Policyarrow-up-right](https://www.tebex.io/terms-acceptable-use-policy)
>  for details.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/seller-protection-and-chargebacks#common-chargeback-reasons)

Common Chargeback Reasons

Reason

Description

**Fraud**

Cardholder claims unauthorized use

**Item not received**

Customer says they didn’t get the item

**Item not as described**

Product doesn’t match its description

**Subscription issues**

Forgotten renewals or unwanted recurring charges

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/seller-protection-and-chargebacks#how-to-reduce-chargebacks)

How to Reduce Chargebacks

Follow these best practices to minimize chargeback risk:

*   **Write clear product descriptions** Avoid “coming soon” features unless clearly labeled.
    
*   **Offer responsive customer support** Use a support email, web form, or Discord community channel.
    
*   **Foster a positive community** Toxic environments may prompt emotional chargebacks.
    
*   **Escalate unresolved billing issues** Refer customers to [Buyer Supportarrow-up-right](https://www.tebex.io/support-customer-form)
     if needed.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/seller-protection-and-chargebacks#what-happens-if-i-get-a-chargeback)

What Happens If I Get a Chargeback?

1.  **Tebex investigates** and responds to the chargeback
    
2.  **You may be contacted** for transaction details (via your support email)
    
3.  **If covered**, you keep your earnings—even if Tebex loses the dispute
    

> ❗Some stores or specific packages may not be covered. Tebex will notify you if Seller Protection does not apply.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/seller-protection-and-chargebacks#eligibility-requirements)

Eligibility Requirements

*   Most standard digital goods are covered
    
*   Packages must have verifiable delivery methods (e.g., server commands, keys)
    
*   Transactions over **$1000 USD** are **excluded**
    
*   Coverage may be revoked for excessive disputes
    

Check eligibility for any transaction in your **Payments tab**, or contact the **Payments & Compliance Team**.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/seller-protection-and-chargebacks#faqs)

FAQs

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/seller-protection-and-chargebacks#how-do-i-know-if-my-product-is-covered-by-seller-protection)

How do I know if my product is covered by Seller Protection?

Check the **Payments** section in your control panel or contact the [Payments & Compliance Teamarrow-up-right](https://www.tebex.io/support-creator-form)
. We’ll also notify you if protection is removed.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/seller-protection-and-chargebacks#can-my-store-be-disabled-for-too-many-chargebacks)

Can my store be disabled for too many chargebacks?

Yes. In extreme cases, we may **temporarily disable your store** or restrict withdrawals. Please contact us if you’re concerned.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/seller-protection-and-chargebacks#why-were-funds-deducted-from-my-wallet)

Why were funds deducted from my wallet?

This may be due to clause [6.7 of the Creator Agreementarrow-up-right](https://www.tebex.io/terms-creator-agreement)
. You’ll be notified if this occurs.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/seller-protection-and-chargebacks#how-long-do-chargebacks-take-to-resolve)

How long do chargebacks take to resolve?

Each case varies. The timeline depends on the payment provider's review process, which Tebex does not control.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/seller-protection-and-chargebacks#need-help)

Need Help?

If you’ve received a chargeback or have questions about your eligibility, contact: [Payments & Compliance Teamarrow-up-right](https://www.tebex.io/support-creator-form)
.

# Tebex Accounts vs. Projects | Creators

Tebex provides a robust monetization platform for game creators and studios, allowing you to manage multiple storefronts under a single identity. This guide explains the difference between **Tebex Accounts** and **Tebex Projects**, and how to structure your setup for maximum flexibility and compliance.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/tebex-accounts-vs.-projects#what-is-a-tebex-account)

What is a Tebex Account?

Your **Tebex Account** is your master login — a personal or business-level profile used to access all projects, manage your identity, and maintain platform credentials.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/tebex-accounts-vs.-projects#key-characteristics)

Key Characteristics

*   **One Account per Creator**: Each user or entity may only maintain one active Tebex Account.
    
*   **Identity Verification**: Only one identity verification is required. Additional accounts will be declined.
    
*   **Personal or Business Representation**: This account represents you (as an individual or organization) across all monetization activities.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/tebex-accounts-vs.-projects#use-your-tebex-account-to)

Use Your Tebex Account To:

*   Access the **Tebex Creator Dashboard**
    
*   Manage your identity and billing information
    
*   Control global credentials and security settings
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/tebex-accounts-vs.-projects#what-is-a-tebex-project)

What is a Tebex Project?

A **Tebex Project** is an individual storefront or monetization instance under your account. Each project operates independently, with its own branding, configuration, and product catalog.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/tebex-accounts-vs.-projects#key-characteristics-1)

Key Characteristics

*   **Unlimited Projects**: Create as many projects as you need under one verified account.
    
*   **Scoped Configuration**: Each project supports its own payment settings, custom domain, branding, and server integration.
    
*   **Reuse of Verification**: Once your account is verified, all associated projects are covered — no need to repeat the process.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/tebex-accounts-vs.-projects#use-projects-to)

Use Projects To:

*   Run separate storefronts for multiple game servers, mods, or titles
    
*   Manage distinct monetization strategies across communities or regions
    
*   Maintain brand-specific themes, integrations, and customer experiences
    

[Create a New Project →arrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/projects)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/tebex-accounts-vs.-projects#best-practices)

Best Practices

*   Always maintain **a single Tebex Account** to ensure account integrity, simplified onboarding, and policy compliance.
    
*   Use **separate Projects** to scale across games, servers, or business units while retaining centralized control.
    
*   Avoid creating multiple accounts to circumvent limits — this can delay approval or cause verification issues.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/tebex-accounts-vs.-projects#need-help)

Need Help?

If you’re unsure how to structure your setup or need help creating new projects, visit the [Tebex Knowledgebasearrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators)
 or [reach out to supportarrow-up-right](https://www.tebex.io/support-creator-form)
.

[PreviousInitial Setup Guidechevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide)
[NextTebex Project Launch Checklist: From Account to Activationchevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/tebex-project-launch-checklist-from-account-to-activation)

# Where and Why We Charge Sales Tax/VAT | Creators

circle-info

This page is about how and when we (Tebex) charge Sales Taxes to players. To find out how Sales Taxes/VAT impact you as a creator, see [Information for Accountants](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/vat/information-for-accountants)

When you use Checkout, you are selling digital goods to Tebex. We then resell this content in our own right directly to consumers. Because Tebex are selling the goods directly, we are responsible for the collection and remittance of sales taxes such as GST, VAT, TVA, IVA etc.

As Tebex is the seller of these goods, and as a VAT-registered company, we are required to charge VAT to players based in the European Union and in other jurisdictions where local laws require. As time passes and regulations change we may also have to charge sales taxes in other regions.

We collect and pay all sales tax on your behalf to the relevant tax authorities. For example, if we collect VAT for a player based in France, we will pay that sales tax to the French tax authorities for you without any input needed from yourself. Because you are not selling any goods to customers directly, you do not need to account for, or remit any VAT or sales tax for goods sold via Tebex Checkout. By default, we charge this **in addition** to your RRP - this means that the Sales Tax/VAT does **not** come out of the money you receive - please see 'Tax Modes' below.

This is a **legal requirement** for any business selling virtual goods online, and this same process happens with platforms such as Patreon, the Apple App Store and the Google Play Store.

Points to note:

*   You cannot disable or turn off sales tax/VAT - Please do not request this from the support team.
    
*   You do not need to add your own VAT number - As Tebex is the MoR, your VAT number is not required.
    
*   Do not advise your customers to avoid paying sales tax/VAT - Stores advising this risk permanent closure and removal from the Tebex platform.
    

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/vat#where-we-collect-vat-gst-or-sales-tax)

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/vat#tax-modes)

Tax Modes


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Tebex support two different 'Tax Modes' for Tebex Checkout users - allowing you to specify if the product prices you provide should be considered to be inclusive or exclusive of VAT.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/vat#vat-exclusive-pricing)

VAT Exclusive Pricing

By default, Tebex assumes prices provided are exclusive of VAT. In this mode, we will calculate and add on tax _in addition to_ the payment price. The benefit to this is that the brand owner will receive the same amount from each payment, regardless of where a customer comes from, however it means that different customers will see different prices for your products, depending on their country of residence.

Example 1: UK based customer

Example 2: Italy based customer

In the UK, the VAT rate is 20%. If a product is priced at $10 with the VAT exclusive pricing mode, then the price a UK-based customer would be charged is $12. When a purchase was made, the $2 VAT would be deducted, meaning $10 was available to the brand holder, before processing and platform fees.

In Italy, the VAT rate is 22%. If a product is priced at $10 with the VAT exclusive pricing mode, then the price a UK-based customer would see would be $12.20. When a purchase was made, the $2.20 VAT would be deducted, meaning $10 was available to the brand holder, before processing and platform fees.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/vat#vat-inclusive-pricing)

VAT Inclusive Pricing

If the brand owner opts to enable 'VAT Inclusive' pricing, then we will charge customers the same amount every time, and calculate the VAT as part of that price. Unlike VAT exclusive pricing, this means that every customer will see exactly the same price for your products, regardless of their country, but it does mean you'll receive a different amount depending on the amount of VAT charged.

Example 1: UK based customer

Example 2: Italy based customer

In the UK, the VAT rate is 20%. If a product is priced at $10 with the VAT inclusive pricing mode, then regardless of country the customer would be charged $10. From this, $1.67 would be deducted as VAT, meaning $8.33 was available to the brand holder, before processing and platform fees.

In Italy, the VAT rate is 22%. If a product is priced at $10 with the VAT inclusive pricing mode, then regardless of country the customer would be charged $10. From this, $1.80 would be deducted as VAT, meaning $8.20 was available to the brand holder, before processing and platform fees.

[NextInformation for Accountantschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/vat/information-for-accountants)

# Tebex Project Launch Checklist: From Account to Activation | Creators

This checklist provides a step-by-step overview of the essential actions required to launch a fully functional Tebex store. Whether you're a new creator or a game studio integrating Tebex into your ecosystem, following these steps ensures your store is secure, optimized, and ready for transactions.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/tebex-project-launch-checklist-from-account-to-activation#id-1.-account-setup)

1\. Account Setup

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/tebex-project-launch-checklist-from-account-to-activation#create-a-tebex-account)

Create a Tebex Account

Start by creating your Tebex Creator Account at [creator.tebex.ioarrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/)
. This account serves as your master login.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/tebex-project-launch-checklist-from-account-to-activation#confirm-your-email-address)

Confirm Your Email Address

Verify your email address to unlock dashboard functionality and receive important account notifications.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/tebex-project-launch-checklist-from-account-to-activation#activate-your-plus-plan-trial)

Activate Your Plus Plan Trial

All new stores begin with a **90-day trial** of Tebex Plus — no payment details required. This unlocks premium features during onboarding.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/tebex-project-launch-checklist-from-account-to-activation#id-2.-store-setup)

2\. Store Setup

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/tebex-project-launch-checklist-from-account-to-activation#configure-your-store-details)

Configure Your Store Details

Set your store name, currency, and primary branding preferences.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/tebex-project-launch-checklist-from-account-to-activation#set-up-your-tebex-wallet)

Set Up Your Tebex Wallet

Your wallet is where you’ll receive earnings. Configure withdrawal methods and verify your payout details.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/tebex-project-launch-checklist-from-account-to-activation#add-packages)

Add Packages

Create your digital products using the **Package Management** system. Add pricing, descriptions, and delivery configurations.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/tebex-project-launch-checklist-from-account-to-activation#id-3.-domain-and-team-setup)

3\. Domain & Team Setup

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/tebex-project-launch-checklist-from-account-to-activation#connect-your-domain)

Connect Your Domain

Use either a free `tebex.io` subdomain or configure your own custom domain.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/tebex-project-launch-checklist-from-account-to-activation#invite-team-members)

Invite Team Members

Add collaborators with role-based permissions to help manage your store.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/tebex-project-launch-checklist-from-account-to-activation#id-4.-webstore-appearance)

4\. Webstore Appearance

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/tebex-project-launch-checklist-from-account-to-activation#choose-a-theme)

Choose a Theme

Select and customize your webstore appearance. We recommend the **'Exo' template** for its modern design and flexibility.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/tebex-project-launch-checklist-from-account-to-activation#id-5.-platform-integrations)

5\. Platform Integrations

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/tebex-project-launch-checklist-from-account-to-activation#connect-your-game-server)

Connect Your Game Server

Use Tebex’s integrations to link supported platforms like Minecraft, Rust, or FiveM to automate in-game product delivery.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/tebex-project-launch-checklist-from-account-to-activation#connect-your-discord-server)

Connect Your Discord Server

Link your Discord community for role-based rewards, notifications, and buyer engagement.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/tebex-project-launch-checklist-from-account-to-activation#id-6.-testing-and-promotion)

6\. Testing & Promotion

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/tebex-project-launch-checklist-from-account-to-activation#enable-test-mode)

Enable Test Mode

Simulate real purchases in **Test Mode** to ensure your checkout and package delivery are configured correctly.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/tebex-project-launch-checklist-from-account-to-activation#use-manual-payments-for-package-testing)

Use Manual Payments for Package Testing

Use the **manual payment** option to validate package triggers without incurring charges.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/tebex-project-launch-checklist-from-account-to-activation#promote-your-store)

Promote Your Store

Announce your store to your community through Discord, social media, or server broadcasts. Use banners, Creator Codes, and promotions to drive engagement.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/tebex-project-launch-checklist-from-account-to-activation#next-steps)

Next Steps

Once your store is live and tested, explore advanced features such as:

*   Abandoned cart recovery
    
*   Subscription packages
    
*   Gift cards and coupon codes
    
*   Analytics and revenue reports

# Checkout Process | Creators

When using Tebex Checkout, your customers will use a streamlined, centralised checkout flow.

If you are creating a custom template for your Tebex Store, you must ensure the following HTML is placed on the checkout page to enable your customers to proceed to the Checkout flow.

circle-info

We recommend taking a backup of your template before making any changes. If you're unsure on what to do, contact an experienced web developer or Tebex support.

Copy

    <div class="card py-5 px-4 rounded-0 border-top text-center">
        <h2 class="mb-3">{{ __("Proceed to checkout") }}</h2>
        <div class="row justify-content-center">
            <div class="col-12 col-lg-8">
                <form method="post" action="/checkout/pay" class="gateway">
                    <button type="submit" class="btn btn-primary btn-lg btn-block" id="purchase-button" data-loading-text="{{ __("Loading, please wait...") }}">
                        {{ __("Proceed to checkout") }}
                    </button>
                    <p class="mb-0 text-center mt-3"><small>{{ __("You will be redirected to our payment gateway to complete your purchase") }}</small></p>
                </form>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

# Preparing Your Project for Review | Creators

Creating a compelling and professional storefront is essential to launching a successful monetized project on Tebex. This guide outlines best practices for customizing your homepage and writing effective product descriptions that align with Tebex policies and improve your store’s approval chances.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/preparing-your-project-for-review#customize-your-storefront-homepage)

Customize Your Storefront Homepage

Your homepage is the face of your game, server, or community. It’s the first impression buyers see—and the first thing our review team evaluates.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/preparing-your-project-for-review#why-it-matters)

Why It Matters

*   Clearly communicates who you are and what you sell
    
*   Builds trust with customers and increases conversions
    
*   Helps Tebex assess project legitimacy for approval
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/preparing-your-project-for-review#include-the-following)

Include the Following

*   Store or community name
    
*   Date established or brief origin story
    
*   Mission statement or store intro
    
*   Links to Discord, Twitter, or social platforms
    
*   Upcoming updates or featured content
    

> ⚠️ Stores with default homepage content cannot be approved. Customize yours at [creator.tebex.io/pagesarrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/pages)
> .

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/preparing-your-project-for-review#write-clear-product-descriptions)

Write Clear Product Descriptions

Product descriptions are one of the most common reasons store applications are rejected.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/preparing-your-project-for-review#why-they-matter)

Why They Matter

*   Required for project approval and Seller Protection
    
*   Clarify what buyers are purchasing
    
*   Ensure compliance with payment processors
    

As the Merchant of Record, Tebex must understand your offerings in detail to support disputes and process payments on your behalf.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/preparing-your-project-for-review#include-in-each-description)

Include in Each Description

*   What’s included (items, commands, features)
    
*   How it affects gameplay (benefits or abilities unlocked)
    
*   Delivery method (automated, license key, Discord role, etc.)
    
*   Redemption steps (if manual fulfillment is required)
    
*   Platform or version compatibility
    
*   Images or links to showcase videos
    

> ✅ **Tip:** Write as if the buyer has never joined your community before.

**Example: Minecraft Rank Description**

**Example: Crate Key Bundle**

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/preparing-your-project-for-review#deliverables-and-automation)

Deliverables and Automation

To ensure a seamless customer experience:

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/preparing-your-project-for-review#use-tebex-integrations)

Use Tebex Integrations

*   Automate delivery with supported plugins (e.g. LuckPerms for Minecraft, Oxide for Rust)
    
*   Contact Technical Support for help with integration
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/preparing-your-project-for-review#if-manual-fulfillment-is-required)

If Manual Fulfillment is Required

Include:

*   Redemption instructions (e.g., open a ticket on Discord)
    
*   Required links and estimated timeframes
    
*   A valid deliverable (e.g., Discord role or access key)
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/preparing-your-project-for-review#final-checklist-for-approval)

Final Checklist for Approval

✅ Homepage is customized and informative ✅ Each product description is complete and clear ✅ Delivery method (automated or manual) is defined ✅ All links, media, and instructions are working

[PreviousTebex Project Launch Checklist: From Account to Activationchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/tebex-project-launch-checklist-from-account-to-activation)
[NextProject Review Processchevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/project-review-process)

Last updated 6 months ago

*   [Write Clear Product Descriptions](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/preparing-your-project-for-review#write-clear-product-descriptions)
    
*   [Deliverables and Automation](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/preparing-your-project-for-review#deliverables-and-automation)
    
*   [Final Checklist for Approval](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/preparing-your-project-for-review#final-checklist-for-approval)
    

Copy

    Diamond Rank – 1 Month Access
    - /fly command
    - Diamond tag
    - Light blue particle trail
    - DIAMOND prefix
    - 1x Diamond Kit

Copy

    This crate includes potential rewards:
    - Diamond Sword
    - Diamond Pickaxe
    - Diamond Helmet
    - Diamond Chestplate
    ...and more.

# Paysafecard | Creators

To accept payments via **paysafecard**, creators must first apply and meet specific compliance requirements set by **Paysafe Group**.

> ❗Important: Your store **must be fully compliant** before we can submit your application for review.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/requirements-for-paysafecard#paysafecard-application-requirements)

Paysafecard Application Requirements

Your webstore must meet **all** of the following criteria:

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/requirements-for-paysafecard#store-setup)

Store Setup

*   The store is **fully functional**—no “under construction” or “coming soon” content.
    
*   You have at least **5 active packages** with complete and descriptive details.
    
*   Each package must clearly explain what it provides—avoid internal slang or shorthand (e.g., explain what an “airdrop” is).
    
*   **“**[**Allow Guests to View Packages**arrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/appearance)
    **”** must be enabled in your store settings.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/requirements-for-paysafecard#package-content)

Package Content

*   **Donation-only packages** with **no in-game benefits** are not allowed.
    
*   Every package must provide a **tangible in-game benefit**, such as:
    
    *   Custom skins
        
    *   Colored name tags
        
    *   Special items or perks
        
    
*   **Lootboxes** or any **chance-based mechanics** are prohibited.
    
*   **Gift cards** must state a clear expiration or validity period.
    
*   Ranks or roles offered must be **time-limited**—**permanent/lifetime options are not allowed**.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/requirements-for-paysafecard#store-behavior)

Store Behavior

*   Do **not link to external terms of service** (including your server’s TOS).
    
*   Do **not link to other websites or platforms** offering alternative payment methods (e.g., crypto).
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/requirements-for-paysafecard#transaction-history)

Transaction History

*   Your store must have an **established payment history** on other payment methods:
    
    *   At least **10 successful purchases** over **14 days**
        
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/requirements-for-paysafecard#how-to-apply)

How to Apply

Once your store meets all of the above requirements:

1.  Go to **Control Panel → Payment Methods**
    
2.  Select **Paysafecard**
    
3.  Submit your application
    

> Most applications are reviewed within **5 business days**. In some cases, delays may occur depending on queue volume or review findings.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/requirements-for-paysafecard#summary-of-required-criteria)

✅ Summary of Required Criteria

Requirement

Mandatory

Store has ≥ 5 detailed packages

✅

In-game benefit per package

✅

No donation-only or lootbox items

✅

No permanent/lifetime ranks

✅

Guest view enabled

✅

10+ purchases in past 14 days

✅

No links to external TOS or crypto

✅

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/requirements-for-paysafecard#faqs)

FAQs

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/requirements-for-paysafecard#what-if-im-selling-ranks-or-roles)

What if I’m selling ranks or roles?

If you sell server ranks, you **must** ensure they are **not permanent**. All roles must include a time limit (e.g., 30 days). Paysafe will **decline** any applications that include lifetime or indefinite access.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/requirements-for-paysafecard#can-i-ask-support-to-bypass-these-requirements)

Can I ask support to bypass these requirements?

No. These requirements are **non-negotiable**, as they are set by Paysafe, not Tebex.

[PreviousCheckout Processchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/custom-template-change)
[NextWalletchevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/wallet)

Last updated 6 months ago

*   [Paysafecard Application Requirements](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/requirements-for-paysafecard#paysafecard-application-requirements)
    
*   [How to Apply](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/requirements-for-paysafecard#how-to-apply)
    
*   [✅ Summary of Required Criteria](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/requirements-for-paysafecard#summary-of-required-criteria)
    
*   [FAQs](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/requirements-for-paysafecard#faqs)

# Project Review Process | Creators

Every new project on Tebex must complete a **Store Review** before it can go live and begin accepting payments. This process ensures that all projects comply with legal requirements, intellectual property guidelines, and our platform standards.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/project-review-process#why-project-reviews-are-required)

Why project Reviews Are Required

The review process helps us ensure:

*   No copyrighted or infringing content is being sold
    
*   Packages are configured correctly and deliver content as described
    
*   The project complies with all Tebex policies, terms, and legal obligations
    

This review protects both creators and buyers and upholds the integrity of the Tebex platform.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/project-review-process#what-happens-before-approval)

What Happens Before Approval?

Until your project is approved:

*   Payments cannot be accepted
    
*   The project is not publicly visible
    
*   You can still use **Test Mode** to simulate purchases and validate package delivery
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/project-review-process#how-to-submit-for-review)

How to Submit for Review

1.  Complete all tasks in the project Setup Checklist
    
2.  Once setup is complete, a **Submit for Review** button will appear in the **top-right** of your Creator Dashboard
    
3.  Click the button to begin the review process
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/project-review-process#tips-for-a-successful-review)

Tips for a Successful Review

*   Ensure all packages are complete, functional, and accurately described
    
*   Remove any test or placeholder content
    
*   Avoid uploading content that violates Intellectual Property Guidelines
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/project-review-process#review-outcomes)

Review Outcomes

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/project-review-process#permanently-rejected)

Permanently Rejected

This means your project was created using the wrong project type, or violates platform requirements. Please click **Read Report** on the Getting Started page for specific feedback and next steps.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/project-review-process#temporarily-rejected)

Temporarily Rejected

Rejection may occur due to issues like:

*   Package misconfiguration
    
*   Unapproved or incomplete content
    

Review the **Read Report** for actionable feedback. You can fix issues and **resubmit**. A short cooldown timer may apply before resubmission.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/project-review-process#approved)

Approved

Your project has been approved — you may now:

*   Accept live payments
    
*   Publish your project for public access
    
*   Begin monetizing your community
    

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/project-review-process#video-guide)

Video Guide:

# Dashboard Overview | Creators

The Dashboard is your central view for understanding the performance of your Tebex project. It provides real-time insights into sales, transaction trends, and buyer behavior—all designed to help creators and studios manage and optimize monetization efforts effectively.

![](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1152203580-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LuI8PwvsHA79mTA-7bh%252Fuploads%252F1438izUMZAPiI42RhhpZ%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-13%2520at%252011.47.28.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1d160463-e3cb-446f-9d5a-712731c8ff45&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b39aaea&sv=2)

An Example Tebex Project Dashboard

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/dashboard-overview#key-metrics-at-a-glance)

Key Metrics at a Glance

At the top of the Dashboard, you’ll find summary statistics covering key performance indicators:

*   **Today's Sales** – Your revenue for the current calendar day.
    
*   **Month-to-Date Sales** – Total income generated during the current month.
    
*   **Year-to-Date Sales** – Cumulative sales revenue since the start of the calendar year.
    
*   **Average Payment Value** – The average transaction amount from your customers.
    
*   **Transaction Volume** – The number of transactions processed during each period.
    

These metrics offer immediate insight into your financial performance and are especially useful for identifying sales patterns and seasonal trends.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/dashboard-overview#interactive-sales-graph)

Interactive Sales Graph

Beneath the summary, a visual sales graph shows transaction activity over time.

**Tip:** To analyze a specific timeframe, click and drag over the graph (e.g., from the 21st to the 24th of the month). The view will zoom into that range, allowing for detailed inspection of spikes, dips, or campaign performance.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/dashboard-overview#revenue-report)

Revenue Report

The Revenue Report section provides deeper insight into purchasing behavior. By default, it displays data from the last 30 days.

Included metrics:

*   **Total Sales**
    
*   **Average Payment Value**
    
*   **Upsell Revenue**
    
*   **Number of Transactions**
    
*   **Repeat Purchase Rate** – The percentage of returning customers.
    
*   **Tebex Offers Revenue** – Earnings generated from applied offers and promotions.
    

**Tip:** Use the dropdown in the top-right corner of the Revenue Report to switch between timeframes (e.g., last 30 days, previous month, or custom ranges).

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/dashboard-overview#recent-activity-overview)

Recent Activity Overview

At the bottom of the Dashboard, you’ll find real-time updates on:

*   **Recent Transactions** – The latest payments made by customers.
    
*   **Top Packages** – Your most popular items based on purchase volume.
    

These insights allow you to monitor the latest project activity and identify which packages are performing best.

* * *

circle-info

You can exclude 'free' payments from your Dashboard Statistics [from the Project Pagearrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/project)
 - see the '**Dashboard Preferences**' section.

[PreviousTebex Control Panelchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel)
[NextPayments Overviewchevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/payments-overview)

Last updated 13 days ago

# Wallet | Creators

Your **Tebex Wallet** allows you to receive and withdraw payments from your store. This guide covers how to:

*   Create your wallet
    
*   Add and update payout methods
    
*   Link stores to an existing wallet
    
*   Understand security rules and withdrawal timelines
    

> **Important:** You’ll need to verify your identity before requesting withdrawals. ➤ [Start identity verificationarrow-up-right](https://accounts.tebex.io/profile)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/wallet#academy-video)

Academy Video

📺 **Watch the Tebex Wallet Setup Guide**

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/wallet#creating-your-wallet)

Creating Your Wallet

1.  Go to **Payments → Wallet** in your Tebex Control Panel
    
2.  Click **Setup My Wallet**
    
3.  Choose a wallet email address (can differ from your store email)
    

![](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1152203580-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LuI8PwvsHA79mTA-7bh%252Fuploads%252FsRD931coA5rFgb2vTdMd%252FScreenshot%25202024-07-31%2520at%252016.33.19.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc100ab24-27b7-46cb-bfe3-fd64df2e3430&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6515af58&sv=2)

Wallet page when account does not have a wallet created.

You’ll be prompted to enter your personal information:

*   Use your **legal name and address**
    
*   Do **not** use autofill—enter data manually to avoid errors
    

![](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1152203580-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LuI8PwvsHA79mTA-7bh%252Fuploads%252FApyPpOVGIszzcBblNcqI%252FScreenshot%25202024-07-31%2520at%252016.35.46.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dee324fcf-fafa-4f5a-b5e4-80bdc40b58c7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=434e3fa3&sv=2)

Wallet personal information page

> This information is used for ID verification and account recovery.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/wallet#adding-a-payout-method)

Adding a Payout Method

After setting up your wallet:

1.  Select your **region**, **currency**, and **payout method**
    
2.  Available payout options vary by region
    
3.  PayPal accounts can only be used with **one Tebex Wallet**
    

![](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1152203580-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LuI8PwvsHA79mTA-7bh%252Fuploads%252F6vrXVayLmXXEueIIFkBs%252FScreenshot%25202024-07-31%2520at%252016.37.45.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc3a4131c-2543-4aa0-bbe9-25b7682ade9c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e552187f&sv=2)

Selecting region, currency and method.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/wallet#payout-timelines-and-recommendations)

Payout Timelines & Recommendations

Method

Estimated Time

Notes

**PayPal**

0–2 days (fastest)

Lowest fees

**Bank Transfer**

2–10 business days

Speed depends on region

**Wire Transfer**

5–10 business days

High fees; not recommended unless necessary

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/wallet#updating-your-payout-method)

Updating Your Payout Method

To change your payout method:

1.  Click **Update** in the Wallet section
    
2.  Input new payout details
    

![](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1152203580-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LuI8PwvsHA79mTA-7bh%252Fuploads%252FPrWeJVHyItgl1leclOcU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0699c20b-e529-43e3-94b3-891c0d806cc6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=79f2ca99&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/wallet#important-rules)

Important Rules:

*   Your **current method is replaced** immediately
    
*   You can update the payout method **once every 30 days per currency**
    
*   Adding a new payout method **starts a 5-day security hold**
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/wallet#key-wallet-rules)

Key Wallet Rules

Rule

Description

**One payout method per currency**

Adding a new method (e.g., PayPal USD) replaces the old one (e.g., Bank USD)

**First withdrawal limit**

Max $1,000 for the first withdrawal

**Security holds**

5-day hold after new method added

**One withdrawal per 24 hours**

No same-day double withdrawals allowed

**Withdrawal reviews**

Some payouts may be reviewed for compliance (processed in ~1 business day)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/wallet#linking-an-existing-wallet-to-a-store)

Linking an Existing Wallet to a Store

Already have a wallet? Here’s how to link it:

1.  Log in to your wallet at [accounts.tebex.ioarrow-up-right](https://accounts.tebex.io/)
    
2.  Visit [https://creator.tebex.io/walletarrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/wallet)
    
3.  Select the store you wish to link
    

> If prompted to create a new wallet, try using an **Incognito/Private tab**—you may be logged into the wrong account.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/wallet#troubleshooting-and-faqs)

Troubleshooting & FAQs

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/wallet#im-being-asked-to-create-a-wallet-but-i-already-have-one)

I’m being asked to create a wallet but I already have one.

Try:

*   Logging out of all Tebex tabs
    
*   Re-opening the Wallet page in a **private/incognito window**
    
*   Ensuring you're logged into the correct account
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/wallet#my-withdrawal-is-under-review-what-now)

My withdrawal is under review - what now?

Some transactions are reviewed for compliance. These are usually processed within 1 working day. Contact Tebex Support if delayed.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/wallet#i-use-regional-pricing-what-currency-currencies-do-i-receive-my-funds-in)

I use Regional Pricing, what currency/currencies do I receive my funds in?

Check the [How Does Settlement Work section on our Regional Pricing article.arrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/checkout/regional-pricing#how-does-settlement-work)

* * *

# What is Intellectual Property? | Creators

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/what-is-intellectual-property#understanding-intellectual-property-ip)

Understanding Intellectual Property (IP)


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Intellectual Property (IP)** refers to original creations—such as names, designs, and content—that are legally owned by individuals or organizations. These creations are typically protected under **copyrights**, **trademarks**, or **patents**, which prevent others from using, selling, or distributing them without permission.

Tebex enforces IP protections in accordance with [Clause 1.4 of our Acceptable Use Policyarrow-up-right](https://www.tebex.io/terms-creator-agreement/acceptable-use-policy)
 and aligns with [CFX's Terms of Service for FiveMarrow-up-right](https://runtime.fivem.net/platform-license-agreement-12-sept-2023.pdf)
, which prohibit unlicensed IP usage in-game.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/what-is-intellectual-property#what-is-considered-ip)

What Is Considered IP?

Examples of commonly protected IP include:

*   **Brand identifiers** – Unique company or product names
    
*   **Logos and design elements** – Emblems, stylized fonts, or distinctive symbols
    
*   **Character designs** – Recognizable figures from games, comics, or animations
    
*   **Product silhouettes** – Iconic item shapes (e.g., cars, weapons, gadgets) associated with real brands
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/what-is-intellectual-property#what-you-cannot-sell)

What You Cannot Sell

You may **not list or distribute content** that includes:

*   **Direct brand references** – Real-world names, logos, slogans, or imagery
    
*   **Altered brand names** – Misspellings or phonetic imitations (e.g., “Gucci” → “Gucchi”)
    
*   **Cloned character models** – Replicas or imports from commercial games
    
*   **Lookalike products** – Vehicles, weapons, or items that resemble real-world models, even without logos
    

> **Note:** Intent matters. Minor changes to copyrighted content **do not make it compliant**.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/what-is-intellectual-property#what-you-can-sell)

What You Can Sell

You are allowed to list and sell:

*   **Original content** – Fully custom models, textures, names, or styles
    
*   **Lore-friendly designs** – Fictional creations that suit your game’s universe
    
*   **Stylized assets** – Generic items or vehicles inspired by broader categories, not directly replicating real brands
    

> **Creativity is encouraged—as long as it respects legal boundaries.**

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/what-is-intellectual-property#vehicle-designs-a-common-ip-risk)

Vehicle Designs: A Common IP Risk

Vehicle models are one of the most common sources of unintentional IP infringement. To stay compliant:

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/what-is-intellectual-property#design-guidelines)

✔ Design Guidelines

*   Remove **badges, emblems, and logos**
    
*   Avoid copying recognizable **shapes or silhouettes**
    
*   Prioritize **fictional or modified** vehicles
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/what-is-intellectual-property#how-to-test-for-ip-infringement)

How to Test for IP Infringement

Use tools like **Google Lens** or reverse image search. If your model closely matches a real-world brand or product, it’s likely not compliant.

> [Explore CFX’s Lore-Friendly Vehicle List for pre-approved models.arrow-up-right](https://docs.fivem.net/docs/game-references/vehicle-references/vehicle-models/)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/what-is-intellectual-property#disclosure-requirements)

Disclosure Requirements

If you’re selling packages that include **user-selectable or customizable content**, you must clearly disclose that content on your store page.

Ensure that customers can:

*   View **item names, previews, or thumbnails**
    
*   Access **images, videos, or links** showing the item
    
*   Understand what they’re purchasing **before joining a server or completing checkout**
    

Transparency builds trust and protects both you and your customers.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/what-is-intellectual-property#ip-compliance-checklist)

IP Compliance Checklist

Before listing content for sale, confirm the following:

Compliance Item

Confirmed?

Content is **original** or clearly **fictional/lore-friendly**

\[ \]

No use of **real-world brands, logos, or names**

\[ \]

No **altered brand spellings** (e.g., “Porsh” for Porsche)

\[ \]

Vehicles/models do not **resemble real products**

\[ \]

All **logos and brand badges removed** from assets

\[ \]

A **reverse image search** confirms no likeness to real items

\[ \]

Customizable items are **clearly disclosed** on the store page

\[ \]

Buyers can **preview items** without joining the server

\[ \]

[PreviousProject Review Processchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/project-review-process)
[NextAdult Content Guidelineschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/adult-content-guidelines)

Last updated 6 months ago

# Payments Overview | Creators

The **Payments** section of your Control Panel provides a comprehensive view of all customer transactions across your Tebex store. This includes both automatically recorded purchases and manually issued payments.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/payments-overview#transaction-details-at-a-glance)

Transaction Details at a Glance

Each payment entry includes:

*   Customer name and email address
    
*   Purchased package details
    
*   Payment amount and currency
    
*   Purchase timestamp and transaction status
    

This information helps you track buyer activity, manage support queries, and maintain transparency across your store operations.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/payments-overview#manual-payments)

Manual Payments

Tebex also allows you to manually generate payments directly from the Control Panel. This feature is useful for:

*   **Testing** your packages before launch
    
*   **Issuing free items** to team members, influencers, or giveaway winners
    
*   **Granting access** to specific packages as part of a promotional or loyalty campaign
    

> **Tip:** Manual payments are fully logged alongside standard transactions to preserve a complete purchase history.

circle-info

This section covers the **Payments** functionality available in your Tebex Control Panel, including how to manage transactions, test purchases, and understand associated fees.

**How Payments Work** Learn how customer transactions are processed and recorded on Tebex.? [Check out this article.](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/how-payments-work)

**Creating a Test Payment** Need to simulate a purchase before going live? [This guide](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-test-a-package)
 walks you through test mode.?

**Fees and Sales Tax** Understand platform fees, gateway charges, and how taxes are handled across regions.? [See the Fees Overview.](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/pricing-overview/tebex-fees-and-billing-overview)

[PreviousDashboard Overviewchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/dashboard-overview)
[NextManual Paymentschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/payments-overview/manual-payments)

# Cfx Marketplace | Creators

circle-info

Tebex Partners can now apply to have their packages distributed via the Cfx Marketplace.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/cfx-marketplace#overview)

Overview

The Cfx Marketplace is a curated platform where high-quality scripts, maps, vehicles, and other assets can be purchased by the FiveM community. Partners can list their assets directly from their Tebex Store, increasing visibility and sales while maintaining full control over their products.

This guide explains how the Marketplace works, who can participate, and how to submit packages and bundles for review and listing.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/cfx-marketplace#quick-summary)

Quick Summary

*   Only approved Partners can list assets in the Marketplace.
    
*   Marketplace assets must pass a review by the Cfx Team.
    
*   Listing is free; no additional fees or commission are charged.
    
*   Some package settings (limits, variables, regional pricing) do not apply to Marketplace listings.
    
*   Packages and bundles must include proper categorisation (Collection, Subtitle, Tags).
    

Sales on Marketplace items can only be global, percentage-based discounts.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/cfx-marketplace#what-is-the-cfx-marketplace)

What Is the Cfx Marketplace?

The Cfx Marketplace showcases popular, high-quality FiveM assets selected by the Cfx Team.

**Benefits for Customers**

*   Discover top-rated scripts, maps, and vehicles.
    
*   View trending products and new releases.
    
*   Review detailed Creator profiles.
    

**Benefits for Partners**

*   Increased visibility for your products.
    
*   Access to a broader FiveM audience.
    
*   Potential for higher sales.
    

Listing your assets on the Marketplace is free. Neither Tebex nor Cfx takes extra commission.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/cfx-marketplace#eligibility)

Eligibility

All Tebex Partners that create FiveM Assets can apply to list packages on the Marketplace.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/cfx-marketplace#preparing-your-marketplace-profile)

Preparing Your Marketplace Profile

Before submitting a package, you should complete your Marketplace Profile Information.

You can complete this information here: **Project Settings → Marketplace Profile**

![](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1152203580-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LuI8PwvsHA79mTA-7bh%252Fuploads%252F1QE0LZ6xMaQyiUeGyoec%252Funknown.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0c403a48-86da-4673-af64-49450d5cadb4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=266299ba&sv=2)

Field

Description

Recommended Content

**Profile Image**

Displayed on your public Creator profile

320 × 320 px Minimum Size

**Profile Banner**

Wide header shown on your profile

2560 × 400 px Recommended

**Follow URL**

Link to your related Discord server, website, or YouTube

Any public URL you'd like interested customers to follow

**Customer Support URL**

Where customers go for help

Support form, Discord invite link, etc.

It is recommended that any inbound communication via your support URL is regularly monitored.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/cfx-marketplace#submitting-a-package-to-the-marketplace)

Submitting a Package to the Marketplace

You may submit existing packages or create new ones.

1.  **Open Package Settings**
    

Navigate to: **Packages → Create/Edit**

1.  **Enable Marketplace Listing**
    

Enable the option labelled Cfx.re Marketplace Enabled.

![](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1152203580-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LuI8PwvsHA79mTA-7bh%252Fuploads%252FanMPcLIyHx95GvoFhPc8%252Funknown.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd017885d-b0ec-4d5d-8024-180cbd4b5a04&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bb5bcf85&sv=2)

**What Enabling Marketplace Listing Changes:**

*   Limits, Restrictions & Custom Variables settings are removed.
    
*   Regional Pricing and Upsells will not apply on the Marketplace (only on your own Tebex Store).
    

1.  **Add Marketplace Categorization**
    

You must define:

*   Collection (example: Vehicles → Sports Cars)
    
*   Subtitle (a one-line summary under your package title)
    
*   Tags (recommended: 2–3 relevant tags; maximum 5)
    

1.  **Complete the Package Content**
    

Add your:

*   Title and description
    
*   Media (images and videos)
    
*   Deliverables
    
*   Price
    
*   Marketplace Price (Always in USD)
    
*   Tebex category
    

1.  **Submit for Review**
    

Saving your package automatically sends it to the Cfx Team for review.

*   **If approved**, it will be published on the Marketplace.
    
*   **If changes are needed**, you will receive instructions via email.
    

Editing an existing Marketplace package in a material way may require re-review.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/cfx-marketplace#submitting-a-bundle-to-the-marketplace)

Submitting a Bundle to the Marketplace

A bundle may be listed on the Marketplace if each included package has already been approved individually.

1.  **Create or edit** a bundle.
    
2.  **Enable** Cfx.re Marketplace Enabled.
    
3.  Select **Collection, Subtitle, and Tags.**
    
4.  **Save** to submit for review.
    

Bundle behaviour follows the same restrictions as individual packages:

*   Limits, Restrictions & Custom Variables settings are removed.
    
*   Regional Pricing and Upsells will not apply on the Marketplace (only on your own Tebex Store).
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/cfx-marketplace#how-sales-work-on-the-marketplace)

How Sales Work on the Marketplace

Marketplace listings support only global, percentage-based discount sales.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/cfx-marketplace#allowed)

Allowed

*   Percentage discounts (e.g., 20% off)
    
*   Sales are applicable to all customers
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/cfx-marketplace#not-allowed)

Not Allowed

*   Fixed-amount discounts (e.g., $5 off)
    
*   Regional pricing discounts
    
*   Customer-specific requirements on sales
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/cfx-marketplace#creating-a-sale)

Creating a Sale

1.  Navigate to **Engagement → Sales.**
    
2.  Select **Create Sale**. Configure the sale’s name, applied items, discount type, and schedule.
    
3.  Save your sale.
    

If a sale’s start date is in the past, it activates immediately.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/cfx-marketplace#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting

**My package/bundle is not appearing on the Marketplace**

*   Ensure the Marketplace toggle is enabled.
    
*   Check for review feedback.
    
*   Confirm deliverables and descriptions meet guidelines.
    

**The Marketplace Enabled toggle is missing**

*   You may not have been approved to submit packages to the Marketplace yet.
    

**My bundle submission was rejected**

*   Verify that all included packages are already live on the Marketplace.
    

**A sale I enabled is not applying correctly**

Ensure you are using a percentage-based discount; fixed-amount discounts do not apply to Marketplace listings.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/cfx-marketplace#faqs)

FAQs

**Can I edit a Marketplace-listed package?**

Yes, but significant changes may require re-review.

**Do Marketplace purchases appear in my Tebex statistics?**

Yes, they appear as standard purchases.

**Are there extra fees for Marketplace sales?**

No.

**Are settlement times different for Marketplace sales?**

No. Your usual settlement times apply.

# Wallet Restrictions - Deposits & Locks | Creators

Your **Tebex Wallet** may be temporarily restricted by a **deposit hold** or a **wallet lock** in cases of high financial risk, chargebacks, or compliance violations. These measures protect you, Tebex, and the platform from fraud or financial loss.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/wallet-restrictions-deposits-and-locks#what-is-a-wallet-deposit)

What Is a Wallet Deposit?

A **deposit** is a portion of your wallet balance that is **temporarily withheld** and cannot be withdrawn.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/wallet-restrictions-deposits-and-locks#example)

🔍 Example:

If your wallet balance is **$200** and a **$50 deposit** is applied, you may withdraw up to **$150**.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/wallet-restrictions-deposits-and-locks#when-are-deposits-used)

When Are Deposits Used?

Deposits are applied to offset the risk of chargebacks, fraud, or non-compliance. Common reasons include:

*   ❌ Packages with no deliverables
    
*   ❌ Vague or missing package descriptions
    
*   ❌ Unsupported or misleading products
    
*   ⚠️ Sudden spike in chargebacks
    
*   ⚠️ Violation of the Acceptable Use Policy or Creator Agreement
    

> Deposits are **recalculated monthly** (on the 1st) and usually removed after **~60 days**, depending on risk. Tebex may extend deposit periods at its discretion.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/wallet-restrictions-deposits-and-locks#why-use-deposits)

Why Use Deposits?

Deposits ensure funds remain available to cover potential chargebacks. Without this measure, your wallet could reach a **negative balance**, which may result in:

*   Permanent wallet lock
    
*   Store suspension
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/wallet-restrictions-deposits-and-locks#what-is-a-wallet-lock)

What Is a Wallet Lock?

A **wallet lock** temporarily prevents withdrawals. Locks are typically applied for **30 days** in the following cases:

*   Store was **suspended or disabled**
    
*   Suspected **fraud or chargeback abuse**
    
*   **Policy violations** (e.g., content, refund fraud, Terms breach)
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/wallet-restrictions-deposits-and-locks#unlock-process)

Unlock Process

*   You’ll receive an **email notification** when the wallet is locked
    
*   The **Payments & Compliance Team** will review your account within **5 business days** of your lock’s end date
    
*   Wallets may be **permanently locked** in cases of severe breaches or negative balances
    

> Wallet locks are **non-negotiable** and may be extended at our discretion.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/wallet-restrictions-deposits-and-locks#summary-of-key-rules)

Summary of Key Rules

Rule

Details

**Deposits**

Recalculated monthly; removed after ~60 days if risk lowers

**Wallet Locks**

Typically last 30 days; may be extended

**Negative Balance**

May result in permanent account lock

**Acceptable Use Policy Violation**

Can trigger both locks and deposits

**No advance notice required**

Tebex may take immediate action

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/wallet-restrictions-deposits-and-locks#best-practices-to-avoid-restrictions)

Best Practices to Avoid Restrictions

*   Ensure all packages have **clear, descriptive content**
    
*   Never sell **chance-based, misleading, or illegal** content
    
*   Keep chargeback rates **below industry norms**
    
*   Stay compliant with the Acceptable Use Policy and Creator Agreement

# Adult Content Guidelines | Creators

Tebex is committed to maintaining a safe, inclusive, and professional environment for all users and creators—including both individual creators and game studios. As the **Merchant of Record**, we are legally responsible for the content sold through our platform and must ensure that it complies with global standards, industry regulations, and our Acceptable Use Policy (specifically Section 1.3).

To maintain platform integrity, **adult content is strictly prohibited on Tebex**. This guide outlines what is considered adult or inappropriate content, why these rules matter, and how to stay compliant when building your monetized projects.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/adult-content-guidelines#why-these-guidelines-exist)

Why These Guidelines Exist

These rules are in place to:

*   Protect all users—especially minors—from explicit or inappropriate content
    
*   Ensure compliance with payment processors and international laws
    
*   Preserve a professional platform experience for creators, studios, and buyers alike
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/adult-content-guidelines#what-counts-as-adult-content)

What Counts as Adult Content?

Adult content refers to any material that is **Not Safe For Work (NSFW)** or unsuitable for minors or general audiences. This includes, but is not limited to:

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/adult-content-guidelines#extreme-violence-or-gore)

Extreme Violence or Gore

*   Graphic depictions of dismemberment, torture, or excessive blood
    
*   Realistic visual portrayals that glorify violence
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/adult-content-guidelines#nudity)

Nudity

*   Exposed sensitive areas (regardless of character species or realism)
    
*   Pixelated or censored nudity
    
*   Transparent or sheer clothing that reveals sensitive areas
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/adult-content-guidelines#sexualized-content)

Sexualized Content

*   Sexual acts or suggestive poses
    
*   Items associated with fetish or sexual behavior (e.g., sex toys, bondage outfits)
    
*   Descriptions, names, or visuals implying sexual activity
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/adult-content-guidelines#profanity)

Profanity

*   Excessive swearing or vulgarity in product names, descriptions, or images
    
*   Slurs or offensive language targeting protected groups
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/adult-content-guidelines#a-visual-guide-to-nudity-restrictions)

A Visual Guide to Nudity Restrictions

![](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1152203580-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LuI8PwvsHA79mTA-7bh%252Fuploads%252F1y1oCLTJyDTN8yGmZije%252Fimage%2520%2813%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3b0980eb-83dc-414d-802c-c98fb8e57403&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=36d0574a&sv=2)

Tebex evaluates images holistically. Content is considered **inappropriate** if it:

*   Features characters (human or non-human) wearing **insufficient clothing**
    
*   Uses **semi-transparent outfits** that draw attention to sensitive areas
    
*   Depicts avatars in suggestive or compromising positions
    

> ⚠️ If you're unsure, err on the side of caution or contact our Content & Safety team.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/adult-content-guidelines#whats-allowed)

What's Allowed?

We encourage creative freedom—but within safe, professional boundaries. Here are some examples of what’s **acceptable**:

*   Lore-friendly cosmetics, costumes, or custom skins that are fully clothed
    
*   Horror or action themes that avoid realistic gore or dismemberment
    
*   Language that reflects your community’s tone, as long as it doesn’t violate our profanity or harassment rules
    

> Studios working on mature themes must ensure **storefront content (descriptions, visuals, etc.)** is always suitable for general audiences, even if in-game content includes mature ratings.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/adult-content-guidelines#responsibilities-for-creators-and-studios)

Responsibilities for Creators and Studios

As a Tebex Creator, you are responsible for:

*   Verifying all content you upload is compliant with these guidelines
    
*   Removing or editing any flagged content when notified
    
*   Moderating user-submitted material (e.g. uploads, screenshots) if applicable
    

Failure to comply may result in:

*   Removal of individual items or packages
    
*   Temporary or permanent suspension of your store or account
    
*   Delays in project approval or payment processing
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/adult-content-guidelines#how-to-stay-compliant)

How to Stay Compliant

*   Avoid using **real-world adult brands**, adult toys, or real adult references
    
*   When showcasing character models or avatars, ensure appropriate attire
    
*   Double-check your **storefront banners**, **product thumbnails**, and **video previews**
    
*   Use tools like **Google SafeSearch** or content filters to verify image safety
    

* * *

If you're ever unsure whether your content is compliant:

*   Refer to the [Acceptable Use Policyarrow-up-right](https://www.tebex.io/acceptable-use-policy)
    
*   Reach out via the [Creator Support Portalarrow-up-right](https://support.tebex.io/)

# Packages | Creators

The **Packages** page in your **Control Panel** is where you configure all the digital products and content available to your customers.

A **package** defines what the customer receives when they make a purchase. You can create packages that deliver:

*   **Game server commands**
    
*   **Discord roles**
    
*   **FiveM assets** and downloadable files
    
*   **License keys**
    
*   And other digital entitlements
    

You can customize how packages are delivered, grouped, and displayed across your storefront.

* * *
