# Identity Verification with Tebex | Creators

To maintain platform integrity and comply with global payment and identity standards, Tebex uses **Onfido**, a leading identity verification provider. This process is required for all store creators before a Tebex Store can be reviewed and approved.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/identity-verification-with-tebex#why-identity-verification-is-required)

Why Identity Verification Is Required

Tebex acts as the **Merchant of Record**, which means we are responsible for handling payments, fraud prevention, tax compliance, and dispute resolution. Verifying the identity of store creators ensures:

*   Fraud prevention
    
*   Platform compliance with international regulations
    
*   Safer experiences for buyers and creators
    
*   Trust and accountability across the Tebex ecosystem
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/identity-verification-with-tebex#age-requirement)

Age Requirement

To complete identity verification, **you must be 18 or older**.

*   If you are under 18, a parent or guardian must:
    
    *   Create the Tebex Account and Wallet
        
    *   Complete identity verification on your behalf
        
    
*   Once you turn 18, contact Tebex to transfer the account to your name and complete verification with your own ID.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/identity-verification-with-tebex#step-by-step-onfido-verification-process)

Step-by-Step: Onfido Verification Process

1.  **Start the Verification** During onboarding, you’ll be prompted to begin verification using Onfido.
    
2.  **Accept Terms & Scan QR Code** Accept the terms and scan the QR code with your phone to launch the mobile verification interface.
    
3.  **Submit a Valid ID** Upload a valid, non-expired government-issued ID:
    
    *   Passport
        
    *   Driver’s license
        
    *   National ID card
        
    
4.  **Submit a Live Selfie** Use your device camera to capture a live selfie, which will be matched with your ID.
    
5.  **AI & Human Review** Onfido uses AI to detect inconsistencies, fraud attempts, and tampered documents. In some cases, a manual review may follow.
    
6.  **Tebex Store Review** Once identity verification is complete, the Tebex team will continue processing your store application.
    

> ⚠️ **Verification must be completed before your store can be reviewed or approved.**

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/identity-verification-with-tebex#accepted-documents)

Accepted Documents

Onfido accepts the following forms of government-issued ID:

*   Passport
    
*   Driver’s License
    
*   National Identity Card
    

Ensure your document is **valid** and **not expired**. Expired documents will be rejected.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/identity-verification-with-tebex#is-my-personal-data-secure)

Is My Personal Data Secure?

Yes. Onfido is compliant with global data protection regulations (e.g. GDPR, CCPA) and handles identity data securely. Your personal information is used **solely for the purpose of verification** and is not stored by Tebex beyond what is required for compliance.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/identity-verification-with-tebex#frequently-asked-questions)

Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/identity-verification-with-tebex#im-under-18.-can-i-create-a-tebex-store)

"I'm under 18. Can I create a Tebex Store?"

No. You must be 18+ to complete identity verification. A parent or guardian can create the account and verify their ID until you reach legal age. When you turn 18, contact Tebex to transfer ownership.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/identity-verification-with-tebex#how-long-does-the-verification-take)

"How long does the verification take?"

Most verifications are completed within a few minutes. In some cases, Onfido may take longer to manually review your submission.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/initial-setup-guide/identity-verification-with-tebex#can-i-verify-my-identity-on-more-than-one-account)

"Can I verify my identity on more than one account?"

No. You may only have one active Tebex Account. Attempting to verify multiple accounts with the same identity will result in rejection. To manage multiple stores, use **Projects** under your single verified account.

[NextTebex Control Panelchevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel)

# Entry level subscription | Creators

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/entry-level-subscription#tl-dr)

TL;DR:


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Start small: Subscriptions that are 10/15% cheaper than your average order value.
    
*   More purchases → more upgrades → more revenue.
    
*   Strike a balance between perks and listening to feedback to keep subscribers happy.
    

![entry level subscription ideas](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1152203580-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LuI8PwvsHA79mTA-7bh%252Fuploads%252FGNjV5Jnnx3zk8hhYTNAy%252FScreenshot%25202025-08-04%2520105808.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D32a26a8f-ea0d-4592-bffe-bf30f2c707f6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=33a5226f&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/entry-level-subscription#introduction)

Introduction


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Subscriptions are one of the most powerful tools in a creator's monetisation toolkit. While one-time purchases generate revenue only once, subscriptions create recurring income, increasing predictability and stability for both creators and their communities.

An entry-level subscription (a lower-priced tier, often in the $5–$15/month range) is especially effective because it:

*   Reduces friction to entry – users who may be hesitant to commit to a higher cost are more willing to start small.
    
*   Increases conversion rates – more people are likely to subscribe when the barrier is low.
    
*   Boosts retention – once subscribed, players are more likely to stick around and may upgrade later.
    
*   Builds community loyalty – even small contributions give players a sense of belonging and investment in the server.
    

By offering a welcoming and affordable tier, creators can expand their subscriber base, resulting in higher overall revenue and long-term sustainability.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/entry-level-subscription#calculations-and-pricing)

Calculations and Pricing


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Pricing an entry-level subscription should feel natural to your existing store economy. The goal is to make the subscription affordable and convenient—not necessarily your biggest earner at first, but your most accessible entry point.

1\. Identify Existing Packages to Convert

Start by reviewing your top-selling one-time products. Often, your entry-level subscription should be based on what players already buy most frequently.

*   Hero Value A – Convenience: Offer a monthly subscription instead of one-time purchases (e.g., “VIP Access” → “Monthly VIP”).
    
*   Hero Value B – Popularity: Base your pricing around your most purchased low-tier item—what players already find worth paying for.
    

Example:

*   Your “VIP Access” sells for $6.99 one-time.
    
*   The average player buys it every 2–3 months.
    
*   Converting it to a $4.99/month subscription gives convenience to the player and predictable recurring revenue to you.
    

2\. Identify the Average Basket Size (AOV)

Using the Tebex dashboard, find the average basket value (AOV) of your buyers. ([https://creator.tebex.io/statisticsarrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/statistics)
 > Payments)

Example:

*   Average Basket Size for casual buyers: $7.50
    
*   You can safely introduce a $5–$7 subscription tier as your entry point — this aligns with what players already spend in one visit, but now on a recurring basis.
    

Formula:

![](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1152203580-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LuI8PwvsHA79mTA-7bh%252Fuploads%252FcRg7D28GzssZdAV8I5e7%252FChatGPT%2520Image%2520Dec%25201%252C%25202025%252C%252011_33_53%2520AM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8954f09f-987c-49b6-b4c5-d57746da4014&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8c042df8&sv=2)

**Entry-Level Sub Price ≈ 60–80% of AOV** This ensures the price feels affordable while converting impulse buyers into subscribers.

3\. Divide by Category

🎮 Game Servers

*   Target user: Casual players, newcomers, and community supporters.
    
*   Typical basket value: $6–$10 Suggested Subscription Range: $4.99–$7.99
    
*   Hero Value: Convenience — players get recurring access without needing to repurchase.
    
*   Example: If your “Supporter Rank” sells 80 times per month at $7.50, totalling $600, switching to a $5/month subscription and converting 60 of those users would yield $300/month recurring, with retention and future upgrades improving total revenue over time.
    

🧩 Scripts / Mods

*   Target user: Developers, server owners.
    
*   Typical AOV: $30–$60
    
*   Suggested Subscription Range: $10–$20
    
*   Hero Value: Popularity — give access to updates, Discord support, or early versions.
    
*   Example: If your average buyer spends $15 per purchase every three months, offering a $ 6 monthly subscription creates a steady income and increases perceived value through consistent updates.
    

4\. Test and Iterate

Start with your calculated range, then use your dashboard data to adjust:

*   If churn is high → lower the price or improve value.
    
*   If conversion is strong → test higher pricing or an upgrade path to premium tiers.
    

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/entry-level-subscription#receiving-feedback)

Receiving Feedback


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1152203580-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LuI8PwvsHA79mTA-7bh%252Fuploads%252FPIEMG4NdAaii6sGXJ3X9%252FMegaphone.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc04f3a62-c61a-414b-a231-ca1a32471713&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8a11db47&sv=2)

When rolling out entry-level subscriptions, listening to the community is essential.

*   Who is the customer?
    
    *   Casual players or those new to the server. They may not want to spend $10–$20 right away, but want to support and feel included.
        
    
*   Why listen to feedback?
    
    *   Players might feel a $1–$2 subscription is “too low value” if it doesn’t offer anything tangible.
        
    *   Understanding these perspectives helps you tweak perks—e.g., keeping low-tier rewards cosmetic or symbolic (such as a title, Discord role, or supporter badge), while reserving exclusive perks for higher tiers.
        
    

By gathering and prioritising feedback, creators ensure subscription tiers enhance both the player experience and store performance.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/entry-level-subscription#summary)

Summary


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

An entry-level subscription is a proven strategy for increasing conversions, revenue, and retention in Tebex stores. Priced affordably, it encourages more players to become paying supporters, creates recurring income for creators, and fosters community loyalty.

[PreviousCfx Marketplacechevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/cfx-marketplace)
[NextTebex Store Best Practiceschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/tebex-store-best-practices)

Last updated 1 month ago

# Fund Withdrawals and Transfers | Creators

This guide outlines how fund withdrawals work with **Tebex Checkout**, including payout timelines, supported methods, minimum thresholds, and restrictions.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/fund-withdrawals-and-transfers#settlement-and-withdrawal-timeline)

Settlement & Withdrawal Timeline

Before you can withdraw funds, payments must first **settle**. Settlement times vary by payment method.

Payment Method

Typical Settlement Time

PayPal

7 days (minimum)

Credit Cards

Up to 14 days

Other Methods

[View settlement chartarrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/payment-methods)

> ⏳ **Note**: Stores created **after Jan 1, 2024** have longer settlement times due to enhanced chargeback protection.

➤ Check your store’s [settlement timesarrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/payment-methods)
 in your Control Panel

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/fund-withdrawals-and-transfers#payout-methods-and-timelines)

Payout Methods & Timelines

Method

Minimum Amount

Processing Time

Fees

**PayPal**

$5 USD

1–2 working days

[Fixed low feearrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/fund-withdrawals-and-transfers/paypal-withdrawal-fees)

**Bank Transfer**

~$20 USD

Up to 7 days

[View regional fees](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/fund-withdrawals-and-transfers/bank-account-withdrawal-fees)

**Wire Transfer**

~$50 USD

5–10 working days

£12.00 per transfer

> 💡 **Recommendation**: Use **PayPal** for faster, lower-cost withdrawals when available in your region.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/fund-withdrawals-and-transfers#withdrawal-restrictions)

Withdrawal Restrictions

Tebex uses **security delays and rules** to protect your wallet:

Restriction Type

Description

**New payout method**

5-day hold before withdrawals are allowed

**Updated method**

Only one update per 30 days per currency

**Daily limit**

One withdrawal allowed every 24 hours

**First withdrawal cap**

$1,000 max (limit is removed afterward)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/fund-withdrawals-and-transfers#adding-or-updating-payout-methods)

Adding or Updating Payout Methods

1.  Go to **Control Panel → Payments → Wallet**
    
2.  Select your payout method (PayPal, Bank, or Wire)
    
3.  Enter the required region, currency, and account info
    

> ⚠️ You can only register **one payout method per currency**. Adding a new one will replace the existing method.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/fund-withdrawals-and-transfers#withdrawal-reviews)

Withdrawal Reviews

Withdrawals may be reviewed by Tebex or our partner, **HyperWallet**.

*   This is a standard part of compliance
    
*   No action is needed unless you are contacted
    
*   Reviews usually add **1–2 working days** of delay
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/fund-withdrawals-and-transfers#wire-transfer-availability)

Wire Transfer Availability

Wire transfers are supported in over 200 countries. ➤ [View full country list herearrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/fund-withdrawals-and-transfers/wire-transfer-list-of-countries-and-fees)

> 💸 Fees for wire transfers are higher than other methods. We recommend using **bank transfer** where possible.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/fund-withdrawals-and-transfers#faqs)

FAQs

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/fund-withdrawals-and-transfers#why-cant-i-withdraw-funds-right-away)

Why can't I withdraw funds right away?

Funds must settle before being released. Also, new payout methods trigger a 5-day delay.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/fund-withdrawals-and-transfers#how-do-i-know-what-fees-apply-to-me)

How do I know what fees apply to me?

Check the **Wallet section** of your Control Panel for your store's withdrawal and currency settings.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/fund-withdrawals-and-transfers#my-withdrawal-is-still-under-review.-what-should-i-do)

My withdrawal is still under review. What should I do?

Nothing—this is part of our regular security process. If action is needed, we will contact you.

[PreviousWallet Restrictions - Deposits & Lockschevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/wallet-restrictions-deposits-and-locks)
[NextPayPal Withdrawal Feeschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/fund-withdrawals-and-transfers/paypal-withdrawal-fees)

# Statistics | Creators

The **Statistics** section of your **Tebex Control Panel** provides a comprehensive view of your store’s performance, including sales trends, customer behaviour, coupon performance, and more.

To get started, go to **Statistics** in the left-hand sidebar.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/statistics#available-statistics-views)

Available Statistics Views

You can switch between views using the dropdown at the top-right of the **Statistics** page. Below is a breakdown of each available view:

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/statistics#id-1.-overview)

**1\. Overview**

Includes high-level metrics such as:

*   Most popular packages
    
*   Top purchasing customers
    
*   Revenue by game server (if multiple servers exist)
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/statistics#id-2.-monthly-report)

**2\. Monthly Report**

Displays **daily metrics** for the selected month:

*   Number of payments
    
*   Chargebacks and refunds
    
*   Revenue breakdown per day
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/statistics#id-3.-payments)

**3\. Payments**

Provides transaction-level data for a custom date range:

*   Total revenue and average payment value
    
*   Repeat purchase rate
    
*   Purchase activity by hour
    
*   Purchase location heatmap
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/statistics#id-4.-sales)

**4\. Sales**

Shows data for a selected **sale** and date range:

*   Total revenue generated
    
*   Number of purchases
    
*   Total customer savings (discounts applied)
    
*   Graphical revenue trend
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/statistics#id-5.-coupons)

**5\. Coupons**

Data for individual coupon codes:

*   Total revenue generated
    
*   Number of uses
    
*   Revenue over time graph
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/statistics#id-6.-creator-codes)

**6\. Creator Codes**

Insights for selected **creator codes**:

*   Revenue generated via the code
    
*   Commission paid to the creator
    
*   Number of uses
    
*   Graph of revenue performance
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/statistics#id-7.-categories)

**7\. Categories**

Displays performance per **category**:

*   Total revenue
    
*   Purchase volume
    
*   Revenue trend graph
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/statistics#id-8.-servers)

**8\. Servers**

If your store supports multiple game servers:

*   View revenue and purchase data per server
    
*   Graphical revenue timeline
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/statistics#id-9.-referrals)

**9\. Referrals**

For referral-based tracking:

*   Referrer names
    
*   Clicks, purchases, and conversion rate
    
*   Total revenue generated
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/statistics#id-10.-gift-cards)

**10\. Gift Cards**

Tracks how gift cards are used:

*   Gift card-spent revenue
    
*   Number of purchases involving gift cards
    
*   Revenue graph
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/statistics#id-11.-abandoned-baskets)

**11\. Abandoned Baskets**

Tracks recovery effectiveness:

*   Emails sent to customers
    
*   Click-backs to your store
    
*   Sales recovered from abandonment
    
*   Conversion and revenue graph
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/statistics#id-12.-purchase-follow-ups)

**12\. Purchase Follow-Ups**

Shows follow-up email performance:

*   Emails sent post-purchase
    
*   Follow-up sales generated
    
*   Revenue from follow-ups
    
*   Visual data chart
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/statistics#id-13.-upselling)

**13\. Upselling**

Monitors upsell success:

*   Revenue from upsold packages
    
*   Number of purchases with upsells
    
*   Sales graph for performance tracking
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/statistics#id-14.-offers)

**14\. Offers**

For **Tebex Offers**:

*   Ad impressions
    
*   Total revenue generated
    
*   Visual revenue timeline
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/statistics#id-15.-recurring-payments)

**15\. Recurring Payments**

Tracks subscriptions:

*   Active subscriptions
    
*   Estimated revenue for the upcoming month
    
*   Historical subscription data graph
    

> _Note_: Subscription data is refreshed every 24 hours (UTC). Check back in the afternoon for the latest update.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/statistics#vat-inclusion)

VAT Inclusion

Each statistics view clearly indicates whether VAT is included. Hover over the **"i" info icon** beside the view title to confirm.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/statistics#time-zone-discrepancies)

Time Zone Discrepancies

**Payment exports are in UTC**, while the dashboard uses your local time zone by default. This may cause discrepancies in daily totals.

To align both:

*   Go to **Account Settings**
    
*   Change your statistics timezone to **UTC**
    

> Note: This will also affect any **Team Accounts** linked to your store.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/statistics#academy-guide)

**Academy Guide**

Check out our video tutorial on Statistics.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/statistics#need-help)

Need Help?

If your data appears incorrect or isn't updating, try the following:

*   **Payment totals misaligned?** Check your **timezone settings**
    
*   **Subscription data missing?** Wait 24 hours for it to refresh
    

[PreviousTiered Categorieschevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/tiered-categories)
[NextCustomerschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/customers)

Last updated 5 months ago

*   [Available Statistics Views](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/statistics#available-statistics-views)
    
*   [VAT Inclusion](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/statistics#vat-inclusion)

# Tebex Checkout for WHMCS | Creators

Tebex offers an official Payment Gateway for WHMCS that implements **Tebex Checkout**.

You can use this gateway to accept payments and setup subscriptions backed by Tebex. You'll also be able to use our powerful web panel to manage your store.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/tebex-checkout-for-whmcs#downloads)

Downloads

You can get the latest version of our WHMCS Payment Gateway here:

*   **WHMCS Marketplace:** [https://marketplace.whmcs.com/product/7200-tebex-checkoutarrow-up-right](https://marketplace.whmcs.com/product/7200-tebex-checkout)
    
*   **GitHub Repository:** [https://github.com/tebexio/TebexCheckout-WHMCSarrow-up-right](https://github.com/tebexio/TebexCheckout-WHMCS)
    
    *   See **Releases** tab
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/tebex-checkout-for-whmcs#installation-and-setup)

Installation and Setup

1.  Create your account at [https://tebex.io/arrow-up-right](https://tebex.io/)
    
2.  Download the latest version of Tebex Checkout from one of the resources above.
    
3.  Place the `.zip` archive in \[`whmcs]/modules/gateways` where `[whmcs]` is your WHMCS root directory.
    
4.  Unzip the `.zip` archive.
    
5.  Enable Tebex Checkout as a Payment Gateway in WHMCS.
    
6.  Add a [webhook endpointarrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/webhooks/endpoints)
     to your Tebex Store panel that points to: `https://[your WHMCS domain]/modules/gateways/callback/tebexcheckout.php`
    
7.  Add your store's API keys and webhook secret keys to Tebex Checkout's configuration.
    

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/tebex-checkout-for-whmcs#additional-resources)

Additional Resources


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here are some resources to help you integrate with Tebex.

[Submit Feedbackarrow-up-right](https://wkf.ms/45PQwfE)
 - Help us build a better product by sharing your feedback

[Source Codearrow-up-right](https://github.com/tebexio)
 - All of our plugins’ source code are available on GitHub.

[PreviousCheckout Seller Actionschevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/checkout-seller-actions)
[NextFAQschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/faq)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [Downloads](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/tebex-checkout-for-whmcs#downloads)
    
*   [Installation and Setup](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/tebex-checkout-for-whmcs#installation-and-setup)

# checkout.html | Developers

There is no specific variables for checkout.html. All checkout functionality is handled via opening a new [Tebex.js](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/overview)
 session. To start a new Checkout session, you should do the following:

1.  [Add Tebex.js to your store](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/overview)
    
2.  [Receive the current baskets ident](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/pages/checkout.html#receive-an-ident-for-tebex.js)
    
3.  [Launch the Tebex.js modal](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/pages/checkout.html#using-tebex.js)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/pages/checkout.html#receive-an-ident-for-tebex.js)

Receive an ident for Tebex.js

`GET` `/checkout/ident`

This endpoint will return an ident for the current basket, which is required by [Tebex.js](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/overview)
 when launching a checkout modal.

**Response**

200

Copy

    {
        "ident":"null if customer is not logged in"
    }

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/pages/checkout.html#using-tebex.js)

Using Tebex.js

 or view the demo over at [https://js.tebex.ioarrow-up-right](https://js.tebex.io/)

# basket | Developers

The global basket object contains all information relevant to the customers basket, such as price & packages.

Variables

Type

Description

`id`

string

Internal ID of the basket.

`ident`

string

The identifier that can be passed to [Tebex.js](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/tebex.js/overview)

`ign`

string

The username of the customer.

`uuid`

string

The UUID of the customer.

`currency`

string

The 3 digit currency code of the basket.

`price`

string

The current price of the basket.

`packages`

array\[package\]

An array of packages in the customers basket.

`coupons`

array\[coupon\]

An array of coupons in the customers basket.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/templates/global-variables/basket#request-variable)

Request Variable

If you'd like access to a variable that is not currently available, [please let us know.arrow-up-right](https://forms.monday.com/forms/8cbacdac7c30b725cd4617cbba0e5eeb?r=use1)

# Tebex Store Best Practices | Creators

Selling digital goods successfully on Tebex takes more than just listing items. This guide distills key insights from top-performing stores into actionable best practices. Whether optimizing an existing storefront or building one from scratch, these tips will help you present your products, run more innovative promotions, and create a seamless customer checkout experience.

![](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1152203580-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LuI8PwvsHA79mTA-7bh%252Fuploads%252FDwY3x3Rp4lfSf7EDka4T%252F1%2520v1.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbcc7a08c-e21b-4175-88cf-a9544c40dab2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=92b90353&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/tebex-store-best-practices#store-design-and-landing-page)

Store Design and Landing Page

**1\. Prioritize the Visibility of Offers and Sales**

*   Avoid leaving the landing page empty—use it to showcase popular products, sales, or recently added items.
    
*   Reduce hero section space if it's not contributing directly to conversions or sales.
    
*   Ensure that the store's purpose and what's for sale are immediately clear. This will help people understand why they're in your store.
    

**2\. Create a "Store-Like" Feel**

*   Ensure the design feels like a real online store, with product visibility and clear and compelling categorization.
    
*   Utilize visual hierarchy to highlight key offers.
    

![](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1152203580-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LuI8PwvsHA79mTA-7bh%252Fuploads%252Frs5LYBSOX5neHz0TwMHZ%252F2%2520v2.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1edf6b8a-9ba4-4b6e-9214-3cfaf1dfd908&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=eb8c253e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/tebex-store-best-practices#layout-and-offer-presentation)

Layout and Offer Presentation

**3\. Use Tile-Based Layouts**

*   Display product offers in tiles rather than lists to make them easier to compare.
    
*   Tile layouts effectively showcase bundles, discounts, and bonus content.
    

**4\. Differentiate "Core" vs "Bonus" Benefits**

*   Make a clear visual distinction between the main item and any additional benefits.
    
*   Avoid duplicated information across offers to reduce confusion and buyer fatigue.
    

**5\. Price Placement Matters**

*   Show prices prominently within the call-to-action (CTA) to simplify the purchase process.
    

![](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1152203580-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LuI8PwvsHA79mTA-7bh%252Fuploads%252FuVfnHB1aJr4KmCy0H0b1%252F3%2520v1.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D42bd26d7-fb74-445f-944e-35b5b45ad5fa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=683db648&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/tebex-store-best-practices#sales-strategy)

Sales Strategy

**6\. Be Strategic with Discounts**

*   Avoid putting all items on sale simultaneously, as this diminishes the perceived value of discounts. **Remember, if everything is on sale, nothing is on sale.**
    
*   Stagger sales or use targeted discounts to maintain promotional impact.
    

**7\. Use Time-Limited Promotions**

*   Incorporate countdowns for time-sensitive deals to create urgency (FOMO) and encourage conversions.
    

**8\. Incorporate Nudging Techniques**

*   Use labels like "Best Value" or "Most Popular" thoughtfully—they should be meaningful, not just assigned to the highest-priced option.
    

![](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1152203580-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LuI8PwvsHA79mTA-7bh%252Fuploads%252FL2PY88dQcagEtkgbnuto%252F4%2520v1.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D02479f94-299f-4a45-9f5e-d68f0e2896cb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=48fb1004&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/tebex-store-best-practices#localization-and-currency)

Localization and Currency

**9\. Localize Currency Effectively**

*   Ensure that currency conversion works and that localized prices are displayed accurately. Use [Regional Pricingarrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/currency/regional-pricing)
     if your player and market demographics allow it.
    
*   Round prices down when converting to maintain psychological pricing advantages.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/tebex-store-best-practices#checkout-and-post-purchase)

Checkout and Post-Purchase

**10\. Streamline the Checkout Process**

*   Use [purchase follow-up campaignsarrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/post-purchase-follow-ups)
     to encourage repeat purchases.
    

![](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1152203580-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LuI8PwvsHA79mTA-7bh%252Fuploads%252F8N7ztkgG4HLYfXRgF3CU%252F5%2520v1.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1ebf7846-4665-4c5e-9ec6-c58abe841357&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8aca615b&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/tebex-store-best-practices#bundling-and-offer-structuring)

Bundling and Offer Structuring

**11\. Offer Compelling Bundles**

*   Create product bundles that combine different offers or currencies to maximize perceived value.
    
*   Consider cross-category, cross-currency bundles, or Starter Packs.
    

**12\. Use Visual Cues to Promote Offers**

*   To draw attention, highlight bundles, discounts, and featured products with ribbons, badges, or increased tile size.
    

[PreviousEntry level subscriptionchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/entry-level-subscription)
[NextSales Calendar - 2026chevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/sales-calendar-2026)

Last updated 8 months ago

# Checkout FAQ | Creators

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/faqs#table-of-contents)

Table of Contents

*   Getting Started
    
*   Wallet & Withdrawals
    
*   Refunds & Chargebacks
    
*   Payment Methods & Fees
    
*   Identity Verification
    
*   Legal, Age, and Compliance
    
*   Technical & Miscellaneous
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/faqs#getting-started)

Getting Started

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/faqs#what-is-tebex-checkout)

What is Tebex Checkout?

Tebex Checkout is a fully managed payment platform. You don’t need your own PayPal or Stripe account—Tebex handles all payments, chargebacks, and taxes as the **Merchant of Record**.

Watch the Tebex Checkout video guide

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/faqs#wallet-and-withdrawals)

Wallet & Withdrawals

Method

Min. Withdrawal

Avg. Time

**PayPal**

$5 USD

1–2 business days

**Bank Transfer**

~$20 USD

Up to 7 days

**Wire Transfer**

~$50 USD

5–10 days

*   Withdrawals may be **reviewed**, adding 1–2 business days
    
*   New payout methods have a **5-day lock**
    
*   Only one withdrawal per 24-hour period
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/faqs#why-cant-i-withdraw-funds-i-see-in-my-wallet)

Why can't I withdraw funds I see in my Wallet?

Payments must **fully settle** before they become available for withdrawal. ➤ See your [settlement timelinearrow-up-right](https://server.tebex.io/payment-methods)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/faqs#refunds-and-chargebacks)

Refunds & Chargebacks

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/faqs#how-do-i-issue-a-refund)

How do I issue a refund?

1.  Go to **Payments**
    
2.  Locate the transaction
    
3.  Click **Refund** (yellow button)
    

⏳ Refunds may take up to **14 business days** depending on method.

> ⚠️ PayPal payments **over 180 days** cannot be refunded.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/faqs#what-happens-if-i-receive-a-chargeback)

What happens if I receive a chargeback?

Tebex handles all chargebacks under Checkout. If one is lost, **you keep the funds** (under Seller Protection). No action is required unless we contact you.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/faqs#payment-methods-and-fees)

Payment Methods & Fees

*   **All payment processing is handled by Tebex**
    
*   Additional methods (e.g., Paysafecard) require approval
    
*   Tebex is regularly expanding payment method options
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/faqs#does-checkout-support-paysafecard)

Does Checkout support Paysafecard?

Yes, with prior approval. Read: [Paysafecard criteria & applicationarrow-up-right](https://app.gitbook.com/s/k6TR7SuepunW7QJVY0dc)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/faqs#identity-verification)

Identity Verification

Tebex only requests ID when needed for **KYC (Know Your Customer)** compliance.

Required Docs

Examples

**Government ID**

Passport, Driver’s License

**Proof of Address**

Utility bill, bank statement

Under 18? A parent or guardian must register the account. ➤ [Read our termsarrow-up-right](https://app.gitbook.com/s/k6TR7SuepunW7QJVY0dc)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/faqs#legal-age-and-compliance)

Legal, Age, and Compliance

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/faqs#can-i-pay-my-teammates-or-staff-from-my-wallet)

Can I pay my teammates or staff from my wallet?

**No.** Your payout method must be **owned by you**. Violating this will lead to **account lock** under Hyperwallet’s terms.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/faqs#should-i-charge-vat-to-tebex)

Should I charge VAT to Tebex?

No. Tebex purchases the right to sell your goods as a business-to-business transaction under **reverse charge VAT** rules.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/faqs#technical-and-miscellaneous)

Technical & Miscellaneous

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/faqs#why-are-customer-prices-different-by-region)

Why are customer prices different by region?

Tebex automatically adds VAT or local sales tax based on the customer’s location.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/faqs#why-did-my-withdrawal-fail)

Why did my withdrawal fail?

This typically occurs due to incorrect bank or PayPal details. Funds are returned automatically, or bounced by PayPal after 30 days if undeliverable.

> ⚠️ Tebex cannot retrieve funds sent to a **valid but incorrect PayPal email**.

**Why am I seeing a sponsored offer on my order confirmation page?**

This will be our [Tebex Offers feature](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/offers)
 - designed to give you the opportunity to unlock a new revenue stream.

**Customers can purchase multiple subscriptions on my monthly subscription package at the same time, why?**

Set a [User Limit of 1 purchase per Month](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-create-a-package#step-4-set-purchase-limits-optional)
 to stop this, otherwise customers can purchase a subscription as often as they like.

[PreviousWire Transfer List of Countries & Feeschevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/fund-withdrawals-and-transfers/wire-transfer-list-of-countries-and-fees)
[NextSeller Support Guidancechevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/seller-support-guidance)

Last updated 4 months ago

# How To Create A Category | Creators

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-create-a-category#what-are-categories)

What Are Categories?

Categories allow you to group related packages on your Tebex Store—for example, “Ranks,” “Cosmetics,” or “VIP Perks.” Categories also control visibility, upgrade behavior (cumulative pricing), and other advanced features.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-create-a-category#step-1-creating-a-category)

Step 1: Creating a Category

1.  Log in to your **Tebex Control Panel**.
    
2.  Click **Packages** from the left-hand sidebar.
    
3.  Click **Add New** → **Category**.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-create-a-category#step-2-fill-in-category-details)

Step 2: Fill in Category Details

Field

Description

**Name**

The title of the category as it appears on your storefront.

**Description**

A short explanation of what's inside. Displayed on the category page.

**Image**

Represents the category visually. Shown depending on your store template.

**Minecraft GUI Item** _(if applicable)_

Icon used in-game when using the Tebex Minecraft plugin.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-create-a-category#category-settings-overview)

Category Settings Overview

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-create-a-category#general)

**General**

*   **Parent Category**: Assign this category as a subcategory of another.
    
*   **Package Display Formation**: Toggle whether to show the category image on the storefront.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-create-a-category#visibility-options)

**Visibility Options**

Option

Description

**Only Show If Customer Has Purchased Package(s)**

Restrict visibility to customers who own specific package(s).

**Order Packages In This Category By**

Choose order: manual, price (low/high), or newest first.

**Hide From Subcategory Dropdown**

Prevent this subcategory from being listed under its parent.

**Disable This Category**

Hides category from storefront and disables all its packages (without deleting them).

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-create-a-category#cumulative-purchase-logic)

**Cumulative Purchase Logic**

Use **cumulative packages** to enable upgrade paths—for example, allowing a player to upgrade from Silver Rank to Gold Rank by only paying the price difference.

Setting

Description

**Enable Cumulative Pricing**

Charges customer only the difference between the packages they own and the one they want.

**Disable Lower-Priced Packages**

Prevents users from downgrading (useful in rank systems).

**Cumulative Discounts Are Permanent**

Discounts remain even if access expires (e.g., due to time-based removal).

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-create-a-category#advanced-options)

**Advanced Options**

Option

Description

**Category Slug**

Customize the end of the URL for SEO and clarity.

**Restrict to One Package**

Limit customers to purchasing only one package from this category.

**Delete Pending Expiry Commands of Other Packages**

Removes queued “on removal” commands from other packages when a new one is bought.

**Add Remaining Time from Previous Purchases**

Carries over unused time from old packages to new ones (if time-based).

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-create-a-category#final-step-save-your-category)

Final Step: Save Your Category

Once you've completed the fields and selected your options:

*   Click **Create** or **Update**.
    
*   Your category will now appear on your storefront and be available to assign packages to.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-create-a-category#prefer-a-video-guide)

Prefer a Video Guide?

Watch our Categories Overview Academy Video for a quick walkthrough.

[PreviousHow To Test A Packagechevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-test-a-package)
[NextTiered Categorieschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/tiered-categories)

Last updated 6 months ago

*   [What Are Categories?](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-create-a-category#what-are-categories)
    
*   [Step 1: Creating a Category](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-create-a-category#step-1-creating-a-category)

# How To Create A Package | Creators

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-create-a-package#what-is-a-package)

**What is a Package?**

A **package** in Tebex represents a digital product your customers can purchase. Each package includes:

*   A name and description
    
*   A price (one-time, recurring, or both)
    
*   Deliverables (e.g., game server commands, Discord roles, license keys)
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-create-a-package#step-1-create-a-new-package)

**Step 1: Create a New Package**

1.  Log in to your [**Tebex Control Panel**.arrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/dashboard)
    
2.  Navigate to **Packages** in the left sidebar.
    
3.  Click **Add New** → **Package**.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-create-a-package#step-2-fill-in-basic-package-info)

**Step 2: Fill in Basic Package Info**

circle-exclamation

You can attach videos to packages, in addition to images.

Field

Description

**Name**

The public name shown on your webstore.

**Description**

Clearly explain the product. List all included benefits if applicable.

**Category**

Assign to a store category. You can edit categories later if needed.

**Image and/or Video via YouTube**

Images are displayed on the store depending on your template. Use PNG ≤165px height. Videos (via YouTube) can be listed in addition to images; these are displayed alongside the images in a carousel.

**Price**

Set a one-time fee, subscription, or both.

circle-info

Clear, benefit-driven descriptions help increase conversions.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-create-a-package#step-3-configure-pricing-and-delivery-rules)

**Step 3: Configure Pricing & Delivery Rules**

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-create-a-package#payment-options)

**Payment Options**

*   **One-Time Payment**
    
*   **Recurring Subscription**
    
*   **Both** (same price for both)
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-create-a-package#delivery-scheduling)

**Delivery Scheduling**

*   **Remove After**: Automatically revoke access after X days.
    
*   **Charge Every**: Set subscription frequency (e.g., monthly).
    

triangle-exclamation

**'Remove After' does not work with FiveM/RedM Assets.**

Revoking an asset is only possible when issuing a refund for paid transactions or when a customer's subscription expires for recurring transactions. This is done to combat fraudulent use of the platform.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-create-a-package#step-4-set-purchase-limits-optional)

**Step 4: Set Purchase Limits (Optional)**

*   **Global Limit**: Limit total store-wide purchases.
    
*   **User Limit**: Limit per-customer purchases.
    
*   **Exclude Removed Packages** from limit tracking.
    

circle-info

**Setting up a subscription where you only want the customer to have one active subscription at a time?**

You'll need to set a User Limit of 1 per month to restrict purchases.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-create-a-package#step-5-apply-restrictions-optional)

**Step 5: Apply Restrictions (Optional)**

*   **Required Packages**: Gate access behind owning one or more packages.
    
*   **Quantity Lock**: Prevent customers from adjusting quantity.
    
*   **Visibility Options**:
    
    *   Publish date range
        
    *   Hide for anonymous users
        
    *   Fully disable package from store
        
    

circle-info

Disabling a package won’t affect any existing subscriptions, but it will prevent new ones from being created.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-create-a-package#step-6-add-deliverables)

**Step 6: Add Deliverables**

Each deliverable is triggered by specific events (purchase, refund, removal, etc.).

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-create-a-package#supported-deliverable-types)

Supported Deliverable Types

Type

Description

**Game Server Commands**

Send in-game commands on purchase (e.g., using [Tebex Pluginarrow-up-right](https://github.com/tebexio/Tebex-Minecraft/releases)
 or [RCONarrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/rcon-adapter)
).

**FiveM Assets**

Link assets from your CFX Account for automatic delivery.

**Discord Actions**

Assign/remove roles, send messages, or invite users to Discord.

**License Keys**

Upload a CSV (max 500 keys) for Tebex to distribute via email.

**File Downloads**

Provide digital downloads (max 300MB).

**Webhooks**

Send transaction info to your own server. [See Developer Docsarrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/webhooks/overview)
.

**Gift Cards**

Issue a [gift cardarrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/gift-cards)
 to the customer equal to the purchase amount.

circle-info

**Need help writing server commands?** [Check our Command Guide.](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/an-introduction-to-commands)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-create-a-package#step-7-advanced-options)

**Step 7: Advanced Options**

*   **Custom URL Slug**: Make package URLs more readable and SEO-friendly.
    
*   **Community Goal Tracking**: Add packages toward Community Goals.
    
*   **Upsell Configurations**: Promote additional products during checkout.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-create-a-package#final-step-save-the-package)

**Final Step: Save the Package**

Click **Create** or **Update** to finalize your package. Your new product will now appear on your webstore.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-create-a-package#prefer-a-video-walkthrough)

**Prefer a Video Walkthrough?**

Check out our Package Creation Overview Guide for a visual introduction.

# How To Test A Package | Creators

Testing your packages is an essential step before launching your Tebex Store. It ensures your customers reliably receive the content they purchase and allows you to verify that deliverables (e.g., commands, files, roles) are correctly configured.

There are **two primary methods** for testing packages:

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-test-a-package#method-1-store-test-mode)

Method 1: Store Test Mode

**Store Test Mode** allows you to simulate real transactions without charging your testers. It's ideal for pre-launch testing.

> ⚠️ **Important:** Only use Store Test Mode when your store is private. If your store is publicly accessible, enabling this feature may allow unintended users to complete purchases for free.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-test-a-package#how-to-enable-store-test-mode)

**How to Enable Store Test Mode:**

1.  Go to your **Tebex Control Panel**.
    
2.  Navigate to **Settings** → **Checkout**.
    
3.  Scroll down and toggle **Test Mode** to "On".
    

Once enabled:

*   Test purchases can be completed instantly with no real payment details.
    
*   Test transactions will appear in your Control Panel.
    
*   You can delete test transactions after testing (button available at the bottom of Checkout Settings).
    

> 🔍 **Note:** Test payments:
> 
> *   **Trigger webhooks**
>     
> *   **Appear in Sales statistics**
>     
> *   **Do NOT affect your Earnings statistics**
>     

**Don’t forget to disable Test Mode before going live.**

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-test-a-package#method-2-manual-payments)

Method 2: Manual Payments

**Manual Payments** allow you to simulate a package delivery without using the checkout process. This method is ideal for quick internal testing, giveaways, or delivering packages to individual users.

To initiate a manual payment:

*   Go to your Tebex Control Panel.
    
*   Navigate to the **Payments** section and select **Manual Payment**.
    
*   Enter the recipient’s information and select the package to issue.
    

> 🔍 **Note:** Manual payments:
> 
> *   **Do not trigger webhooks**
>     
> *   **Do not appear in Sales or Earnings statistics**
>     

Learn more about [Manual Paymentsarrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/payments-overview/manual-payments)
. Prefer a video guide? [Find one here.](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/payments-overview/manual-payments#prefer-a-video-walkthrough)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-test-a-package#special-consideration-testing-fivem-assets)

Special Consideration: Testing FiveM Assets

Assets delivered via **Manual or Test Payments** cannot be revoked. To safely test FiveM package delivery:

1.  Create a **subscription-based package**.
    
2.  Issue your tester a **gift card or coupon** to cover the first billing cycle.
    
    *   If the first payment is fully covered, it will not renew, and no billing info is required.
        
    
3.  The asset will be delivered as normal, and the subscription will not continue unless renewed manually.
    

* * *

[PreviousHow To Create A Packagechevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-create-a-package)
[NextHow To Create A Categorychevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-create-a-category)

Last updated 1 month ago

*   [Method 1: Store Test Mode](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/how-to-create-packages/how-to-test-a-package#method-1-store-test-mode)

# Creator Codes | Creators

Creator Codes enable your customers to support streamers, YouTubers, and other influencers directly at checkout. When a Creator Code is used, a portion of the payment is automatically allocated to the creator's Tebex Wallet—no manual payouts required.

You can optionally incentivize usage by applying a customer discount when a Creator Code is used.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/creator-codes#pricing-and-revenue-share)

Pricing & Revenue Share

*   **Tebex Fee**: An additional **1% fee** applies to payments made using a Creator Code.
    
*   **Revenue Share Cap**: The **maximum payout to a creator is capped at 20%** per transaction. This ensures that payment breakdowns across methods, taxes, and fees don't leave creators with negligible earnings.
    
*   **Gift Card Restrictions**: If you offer gift cards with an associated discount, the **discount will not apply** to purchases where a Creator Code is used.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/creator-codes#how-creators-get-a-wallet)

How Creators Get a Wallet

To receive payouts from Creator Codes, creators must register for a **Tebex Wallet**. Provide them with the following steps:

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/creator-codes#if-the-creator-does-not-have-a-wallet)

If the Creator Does Not Have a Wallet:

1.  Visit [https://wallet.tebex.io/registerarrow-up-right](https://wallet.tebex.io/register)
    .
    
2.  Create a Tebex account.
    
3.  Set up the wallet as an **individual** or a **registered business**.
    
4.  Add payout information (e.g., PayPal or bank details).
    
5.  Navigate to **Withdraw > Your Details** to find the **Wallet Reference**.
    
6.  Send the **Wallet Reference** to the Tebex store owner.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/creator-codes#settlement-period)

⏳ Settlement Period

Funds earned via Creator Codes are **settled after 30 working days** by default. This delay allows for transaction verification, refund windows, and chargeback processing.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/creator-codes#adding-creator-code-support-to-your-custom-template)

Adding Creator Code Support to Your Custom Template

To allow customers to enter Creator Codes in your Tebex store, insert the following HTML snippet in your custom template. This functionality is best placed within the `checkout.html` file, as Creator Codes require an active basket to work.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/creator-codes#academy-guide)

**Academy Guide**

Check out our video tutorial on Creator Codes:

[PreviousSaleschevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/sales)
[NextGift Cardschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/gift-cards)

Last updated 1 month ago

*   [Pricing & Revenue Share](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/creator-codes#pricing-and-revenue-share)
    
*   [How Creators Get a Wallet](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/creator-codes#how-creators-get-a-wallet)
    
*   [⏳ Settlement Period](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/creator-codes#settlement-period)
    
*   [Adding Creator Code Support to Your Custom Template](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/creator-codes#adding-creator-code-support-to-your-custom-template)
    
*   [Academy Guide](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/creator-codes#academy-guide)
    

Copy

    htmlCopyEdit<form method="post" action="/creator-code/add">
      <div class="input-group">
        <input type="text" class="form-control" name="code" placeholder="Enter a creator code" value="{{ basket.creator_code }}" {{ basket.creator_code ? 'disabled' }}>
        <div class="input-group-append">
          {% if basket.creator_code %}
            <a href="/creator-code/remove" class="btn btn-danger">Remove</a>
          {% else %}
            <button type="submit" class="btn btn-primary">Add</button>
          {% endif %}
        </div>
      </div>
    </form>

# Appearance | Creators

The [**Appearance**arrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/appearance)
 section of the Tebex Control Panel allows you to customize the **visual layout**, **styling**, and **behavior** of your store. From templates and themes to visibility settings, branding, and customer experience, this page is your one-stop-shop for customizing how your store looks and feels.

> 📍 Navigate to: [**Webstore** → **Appearance**arrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/appearance)
>  (in the left-hand sidebar)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/appearance#understanding-templates-and-themes)

**Understanding Templates and Themes**

Concept

Description

**Template**

Controls the **structure and layout** of your store. It's based on HTML. Templates define how components (like headers, product grids, and sidebars) are arranged.

**Theme**

Controls the **styling and color scheme** of your store. It's based on CSS. Themes change fonts, colors, and visual polish.

> 💡 Tebex's default free template is **Exo**, which includes several free themes like “Space.”

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/appearance#key-appearance-options)

**Key Appearance Options**

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/appearance#visibility-controls)

Visibility Controls

Limit who can view your store during setup or private testing:

*   Click **Visibility** beneath your template name.
    
*   Enable the toggle to **make your store private**.
    
*   Add **IPv4 addresses** to whitelist access. Separate multiple IPs with commas (e.g. `8.8.8.8,8.8.4.4`).
    
*   View your IP [herearrow-up-right](https://nordvpn.com/what-is-my-ip/)
    .
    

> Note: If your store isn't appearing online, check your **Dashboard** to ensure your store has passed the **Store Review** process.

* * *

Branding (Logo & Favicon)

Customize your store's branding:

*   **Logo**: Replaces your store's name text.
    
    *   PNG or WEBP, max 5MB, min width: 500px.
        
    
*   **Favicon**: Appears in the browser tab.
    
    *   PNG or WEBP, minimum size: 25px x 25px.
        
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/appearance#customer-experience-settings)

Customer Experience Settings

Control the behavior when customers interact with packages:

*   After adding a product to the basket:
    
    *   Redirect to the basket (default)
        
    *   Redirect to the category page
        
    *   Redirect directly to checkout
        
    

Control **package visibility** for guest users:

*   Allow guests to view packages (default)
    
*   Require login to view packages
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/appearance#template-options)

Template Options

If you're using a supported template (e.g., **Exo**), you may see extra configuration fields under **Template Options**, such as:

*   Store layout style
    
*   Header layout
    
*   Sale banner text
    
*   Store-wide display preferences
    

> Options vary by template. If you want to change something not available here, contact the original template creator. Tebex Support cannot assist with template customizations.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/appearance#managing-templates)

Managing Templates

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/appearance#change-your-template)

Change Your Template

1.  Go to **Appearance** → **Change Template**
    
2.  Preview and select from the following:
    
    *   **Exo** – Default (Free)
        
    *   **Night, Dusk, Noon, Combat, Flow** – Premium (£24.99 each)
        
    
3.  Click **Activate** to apply your chosen template
    

> Premium templates include a variety of color themes and are licensed per store. If you haven't edited the code, future updates will apply automatically.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/appearance#create-a-custom-template-tebex-plus-required)

Create a Custom Template _(Tebex Plus required)_

1.  Go to **Appearance** → **Change Template**
    
2.  Click **Create Custom Template**
    
3.  Name your template and select a base (we recommend **Exo**)
    
4.  Click **Create** to access the code editor
    
5.  Use the **Twig** templating language to build your layout
    
6.  Click **Save as Draft** or **Save and Publish**
    

> Learn more about [Twigarrow-up-right](https://twig.symfony.com/)
>  templating. Tebex does not provide support for custom code.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/appearance#managing-themes)

Managing Themes

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/appearance#change-your-theme)

Change Your Theme

1.  Go to **Appearance** → **Change Theme**
    
2.  Browse and preview available themes for your selected template
    
3.  Click **Activate** to apply the theme
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/appearance#create-a-custom-theme-tebex-plus-required)

Create a Custom Theme _(Tebex Plus required)_

1.  Go to **Appearance** → **Change Theme**
    
2.  Click **Create Custom Theme**
    
3.  Name your theme and paste or write your CSS
    
4.  Click **Create**, then **Preview**
    
5.  Click **Activate** to publish the theme
    

> You can also use third-party themes by pasting their CSS into the editor. Tebex does not support installing or debugging custom themes.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/appearance#support-limitations)

Support Limitations

*   Tebex does **not support** editing, troubleshooting, or maintaining custom template/theme code.
    
*   Deprecated templates like **Flat** and **Abstract** are no longer supported or updated.
    

* * *

[NextTebex Footerchevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/appearance/tebex-footer)

# Pages | Creators

The **Pages** feature allows you to create unlimited custom pages on your Tebex webstore. Use this to share content such as **Terms & Conditions**, **support guides**, **rank comparisons**, or **game server instructions**—all without needing to upgrade your store plan.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/pages#how-to-create-a-custom-page)

How to Create a Custom Page

1.  From the **left sidebar**, go to **Webstore → Pages**.
    
2.  Click **Create Custom Page** (or **Create Your First Page**, if none exist).
    
3.  Complete the fields as described below.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/pages#page-configuration-options)

Page Configuration Options

Field

Description

**Page Title**

The title that appears on your store and as the clickable link in navigation.

**Page Slug**

The custom URL path (e.g., `/my-custom-page`).

**Page Content**

The body content of the page. Use the built-in visual editor or click **Code View** to enter custom HTML.

**Disable This Page**

Hides the page from public view without deleting it.

**Only Show to Logged-In Users**

Restricts access to authenticated customers only.

**Do Not Add to Menu**

Prevents the page from showing in your navigation menu—ideal for link-only or private pages.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/pages#common-use-cases)

Common Use Cases

Custom pages can be used for a variety of purposes. Here are a few common examples:

*   **Support Contact Information** Provide an email address or Discord server for customer inquiries.
    
*   **Delivery Instructions** Explain how customers can redeem their packages in-game, especially if extra steps are required.
    
*   **Rank Comparison Charts** Help customers understand the differences between ranks or tiers before they make a purchase.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/pages#sitemaps)

Sitemaps

Sitemaps tell search engines like Google what pages are on your Tebex Store, where they're stored and what each page is about.

We generate sitemaps automatically for each Tebex Store using the information you provide on your pages and packages, such as page/package titles and descriptions.

*   It's not possible to manually edit the content of the sitemap itself.
    
*   You can see your store's sitemap at: https://example.tebex.io/sitemap (replace example.tebex.io with your own store's domain).
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/pages#tips)

Tips

*   Pages added without the “Do Not Add to Menu” option will appear in your store’s navigation bar.
    
*   HTML formatting is optional—most users can use the visual editor without needing code.
    
*   Changes take effect immediately after saving.

*   [Page Configuration Options](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/pages#page-configuration-options)
    
*   [Common Use Cases](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/pages#common-use-cases)

# Template Variables | Creators

Tebex supports a wide range of **template variables** for use within **custom templates** (written in Twig). These variables allow you to access and display dynamic content such as store details, basket contents, package info, and checkout status.

> Template variables are only available when you're using **Custom Templates**, which require a **Tebex Plus** subscription.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/appearance/template-variables#global-variables-available-across-all-pages)

Global Variables (Available Across All Pages)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/appearance/template-variables#store-variables)

**Store Variables**

Variable

Description

`store.plan`

The ID of the plan the store is subscribed to.

`store.branding`

Whether Tebex branding should be displayed.

`store.name`

The name of the store.

`store.currency`

The currency used by the store.

`store.googleAnalytics`

Google Analytics code (if set).

`store.theme`

The ID of the active theme.

`store.css`

The CSS for the active theme.

`store.logo`

The URL of the store logo.

`store.allowFreeBaskets`

Whether free baskets are allowed.

`store.categories`

Array of categories in the store.

`store.currencies`

Array of enabled currencies.

`store.userMessage`

Message shown to the user (e.g., success/error).

`store.pages`

Array of custom pages on the store.

`store.locales`

Available language/locale options.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/appearance/template-variables#basket-variables)

**Basket Variables**

Variable

Description

`basket.username`

Username of the logged-in player.

`basket.ign`

Alias of `basket.username`.

`basket.uuid`

UUID/ID of the logged-in player.

`basket.currency`

Currency code used in the basket.

`basket.price`

Total price of the basket.

`basket.packages`

Array of packages added to the basket.

`basket.coupons`

Array of coupons applied.

`basket.id`

ID of the basket.

`basket.copy_link`

Shareable basket URL.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/appearance/template-variables#miscellaneous)

**Miscellaneous**

Variable

Description

`modules`

Raw HTML of the sidebar modules.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/appearance/template-variables#package-modal-variables)

Package Modal Variables

Used within the **package modal popup** context.

Variable

Description

`package.id`

ID of the package.

`package.name`

Name of the package.

`package.description`

Package description.

`package.price`

Price of the package.

`package.type`

Type: single purchase or subscription.

`package.customPrice`

Whether the customer can enter a custom price.

`package.purchasable`

If the package can be purchased by the player.

`package.basket`

Whether the package is already in the basket.

`package.disable_gifting`

Whether gifting is disabled on this package.

`package.storeGiftingEnabled`

Whether gifting is enabled store-wide.

`package.image.url`

URL of the package image.

`package.image.uploaded`

If a custom image was uploaded.

`package.discount`

Array of applicable discount data.

`package.reason`

Reason the package cannot be purchased (if applicable).

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/appearance/template-variables#checkout-flow-variables)

Checkout Flow Variables

Variable

Description

`checkout.requiredFields`

Array of required fields in the checkout process.

`checkout.gateways`

Array of available payment gateways.

`checkout.unavailableGateways`

Array of disabled or unavailable payment gateways.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/appearance/template-variables#tips)

*   These variables can be used inside your **Twig templates** with double curly braces:
    
*   Always check for availability before outputting optional data (e.g. `package.discount`) using Twig conditionals:

    twigCopyEdit{{ store.name }}
    {{ basket.price }}

# Sidebar | Creators

The **Sidebar** on your Tebex store displays dynamic content modules to engage customers, showcase purchases, track goals, and more. It appears vertically on either the **left or right-hand side** of your store depending on your template.

To access the Sidebar settings: 📍 **Webstore → Sidebar** in your Tebex Control Panel.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/sidebar#default-modules)

Default Modules

When you first access the Sidebar page, you’ll see three modules already installed:

*   **Text Box**
    
*   **Top Customer**
    
*   **Recent Payments**
    

You can edit, remove, or reorder these—or add more modules.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/sidebar#adding-a-sidebar-module)

Adding a Sidebar Module

1.  Click **Add Module To Sidebar** (top right).
    
2.  Select your desired module and click **Create**.
    
3.  If the module requires configuration (e.g., Featured Package, Server Status), complete the settings on the next screen.
    
4.  Click **Create** again to confirm.
    

> You can drag and drop modules to rearrange the order in which they appear.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/sidebar#editing-a-module)

Editing a Module

1.  Locate the module in the list.
    
2.  Click **Edit**.
    
3.  Make your changes.
    
4.  Click **Update** to save.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/sidebar#deleting-a-module)

Deleting a Module

1.  Click **Delete** next to the module you want to remove.
    
2.  Confirm by clicking **Delete** again in the confirmation dialog.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/sidebar#available-sidebar-modules)

Available Sidebar Modules

Below is a breakdown of all available modules and their functions:

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/sidebar#community-goal)

**Community Goal**

> Requires a [Community Goalarrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/community-goals)
>  to be created first.

Displays progress toward a fundraising or support milestone. Configurable elements include:

*   Goal animation
    
*   Progress bar style
    
*   Start and end visibility dates
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/sidebar#featured-package)

**Featured Package**

Highlights a specific package—ideal for sales, limited-time offers, or seasonal promotions.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/sidebar#gift-card-balance-tebex-plus-required)

**Gift Card Balance** _(Tebex Plus required)_

Lets customers check their remaining balance by entering their gift card code.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/sidebar#payment-goal)

**Payment Goal**

Track progress toward a specific revenue milestone.

*   Set daily, weekly, or monthly goals
    
*   Useful for funding server costs or donation targets
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/sidebar#recent-payments)

**Recent Payments**

Displays the latest customer payments (recommended: max 5).

*   Includes usernames and avatars (game-dependent)
    
*   Builds social proof and promotes community support
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/sidebar#server-status-minecraft-only)

**Server Status** _(Minecraft only)_

Displays server status and player count.

*   Requires server IP and port
    
*   Shows online/offline status and current player count
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/sidebar#text-box)

**Text Box**

Custom content box to display HTML or text. Ideal for:

*   "About Us"
    
*   Store rules
    
*   Contact info
    
*   Announcements
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/sidebar#top-customer)

**Top Customer**

Highlights the customer who has spent the most during a defined period.

*   Recommended reset period: weekly
    
*   Helps encourage friendly competition and recognition
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/sidebar#notes)

Notes

*   Some modules may not appear on all templates depending on layout or custom modifications.
    
*   Tebex does not support template customization issues—reach out to your template creator for help with layout compatibility.
