# Custom Translations | Creators

Custom Translations allow you to personalize the text displayed across your Tebex store to better match your branding or support additional languages. Whether you're localizing your store or simply rewording interface strings, this feature gives you control over most of the platform's messaging.

> ⚠️ **Note:** Not all parts of the store are accessible via translation files. For full control, we recommend using a custom template.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/translations-and-languages/custom-translations#why-use-custom-translations)

Why Use Custom Translations?

*   Support a language that isn't included in the default 30+ languages.
    
*   Modify key phrases like **“Thank you for your purchase”** to align with your tone.
    
*   Adjust placeholder-based messages (e.g., `:username`) for clarity or brevity.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/translations-and-languages/custom-translations#how-translation-files-work)

How Translation Files Work

Translation files are written in **JSON** and include two main sections:

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/translations-and-languages/custom-translations#id-1.-meta-object)

1\. `meta` object

Describes the locale and rules:

Field

Description

`locale`

Language/region code (e.g., `fr_FR`, `en_GB`)

`pluralrule`

Rule for plural handling (see below)

`name`

Display name for the translation file (Control Panel only)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/translations-and-languages/custom-translations#id-2.-translations-object)

2\. `translations` object

Contains **key-value pairs** where the **key** is the original English string, and the **value** is your translated or customized version.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/translations-and-languages/custom-translations#sample-translation-file)

Sample Translation File

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/translations-and-languages/custom-translations#how-plurals-are-handled)

How Plurals Are Handled

The `pluralrule` field controls how plural forms are interpreted for the selected locale. Most users should:

1.  Download a standard translation file (e.g., `fr_FR.json`)
    
2.  Copy the `pluralrule` from that file into your custom version
    

📘 [Viewarrow-up-right](https://www.gnu.org/software/gettext/manual/html_node/Plural-forms.html)
 the full list of plural rules

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/translations-and-languages/custom-translations#creating-your-custom-file)

Creating Your Custom File

1.  Download a standard translation file (e.g., `en_US.json`) from your Control Panel.
    
2.  Open the file using a plain text editor such as **Notepad++**.
    
3.  Modify the `meta` values:
    
    *   Change the locale (e.g., `en_GB`)
        
    *   Update the `name` for internal reference
        
    
4.  Add your desired string overrides inside the `translations` object.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/translations-and-languages/custom-translations#example)

Example:

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/translations-and-languages/custom-translations#using-placeholders)

Using Placeholders

Some strings include **placeholders**, such as `:username` or `:amount`.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/translations-and-languages/custom-translations#example-1)

Example:

> ⚠️ **Do not remove placeholders** from your translations. They must remain in the correct position to avoid breaking messages.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/translations-and-languages/custom-translations#uploading-your-custom-translation)

Uploading Your Custom Translation

Once your file is complete:

1.  Return to **Webstore → Translations** in the Control Panel.
    
2.  Scroll to **Custom Translations**.
    
3.  Upload your `.json` file.
    

Your custom translations will override the default messages wherever applicable.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/translations-and-languages/custom-translations#tips)

Tips

*   Use valid JSON syntax—missing commas or brackets will prevent the file from uploading.
    
*   Only include strings you want to override; all other default strings will remain unchanged.
    
*   If a translation key changes due to platform updates, you’ll need to update your file manually.
    

* * *

[PreviousTranslations & Languageschevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/translations-and-languages)
[NextSubdomains & Custom Domainschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/subdomain-and-custom-domain)

Last updated 6 months ago

*   [Why Use Custom Translations?](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/translations-and-languages/custom-translations#why-use-custom-translations)
    
*   [How Translation Files Work](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/translations-and-languages/custom-translations#how-translation-files-work)
    
*   [How Plurals Are Handled](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/translations-and-languages/custom-translations#how-plurals-are-handled)
    
*   [Creating Your Custom File](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/translations-and-languages/custom-translations#creating-your-custom-file)
    
*   [Using Placeholders](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/translations-and-languages/custom-translations#using-placeholders)
    
*   [Uploading Your Custom Translation](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/translations-and-languages/custom-translations#uploading-your-custom-translation)
    
*   [Tips](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/translations-and-languages/custom-translations#tips)
    

Copy

    jsonCopyEdit{
      "meta": {
        "locale": "fr_FR",
        "pluralrule": "plural=(n > 1)",
        "name": "French Custom"
      },
      "translations": {
        "Welcome": "Salut"
      }
    }

Copy

    jsonCopyEdit{
      "meta": {
        "locale": "en_GB",
        "pluralrule": "plural=(n != 1)",
        "name": "English Custom"
      },
      "translations": {
        "Welcome": "Hey there!",
        "Thank you for your purchase": "Thanks for supporting us",
        "Gift this package": "Gift this to a friend"
      }
    }

Copy

    jsonCopyEdit{
      ":username has been banned from this webstore": ":username is banned"
    }

# Tebex Footer | Creators

The **footer** at the bottom of your Tebex store indicates that your store is **powered by Tebex** and that **Tebex is the reseller and merchant of record**. This footer **cannot be hidden** or removed.

> ⚠️ **Important:** Hiding or removing the footer is a **violation of Tebex Terms and Conditions** and will result in your store being disabled from public access.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/appearance/tebex-footer#why-the-footer-is-required)

Why the Footer Is Required

Tebex operates as a **merchant of record**, meaning we sell digital content on your behalf. To comply with strict requirements from payment networks (e.g., **Visa, Mastercard**), we must clearly display:

*   Who the customer is purchasing from (Tebex)
    
*   That Tebex is authorized to operate the store
    
*   That we are the legal seller of licensed digital content
    

This clarity is a regulatory obligation—not just a branding choice.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/appearance/tebex-footer#footer-appearance)

Footer Appearance

*   The footer **inherits its color** from your **checkout theme** (not the storefront theme).
    
*   By default, it appears in **light mode**, but you can enable **Dark Mode** [herearrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/payment-methods/settings)
    .
    
*   If you need a specific hex color to match your brand, contact [Creator Supportarrow-up-right](https://www.tebex.io/support-creator-form)
     and include your desired hex code(s).
    

* * *

[PreviousAppearancechevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/appearance)
[NextTemplate Variableschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/appearance/template-variables)

Last updated 6 months ago

*   [Why the Footer Is Required](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/appearance/tebex-footer#why-the-footer-is-required)
    
*   [Footer Appearance](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/appearance/tebex-footer#footer-appearance)

---

# Abandoned Basket Recovery | Creators

Abandoned Basket Recovery helps convert incomplete purchases by automatically following up with customers who have added items to their basket but have not checked out. This feature can send **automated emails** or **in-game messages** to prompt customers to complete their purchase—boosting conversion rates and increasing revenue.

> **Note:** Abandoned Basket Recovery links expire 48 hours after being sent. Statistics are available under **Statistics > Abandoned Baskets** in your Control Panel.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/abandoned-basket-recovery#how-to-set-up-abandoned-basket-recovery)

How to Set Up Abandoned Basket Recovery

1.  Navigate to **Engagement > Abandoned Basket Recovery** in your Tebex Control Panel.
    
2.  Enable the feature by ticking the checkbox at the top of the configuration form.
    
3.  Configure the following options:
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/abandoned-basket-recovery#configuration-options)

Configuration Options

Field

Description

**Email Delay**

Time (in minutes) to wait before sending the recovery email. A few hours (e.g. 180 minutes) is generally effective.

**Recovery Discount (%)**

Optional. Apply a percentage discount to incentivize the customer to complete their purchase.

**Categories**

Limit the recovery discount to specific categories. Leave blank to apply it store-wide.

**In-Game Messages**

Enable in-game messages to notify logged-in players about their abandoned cart and recovery discount.

**Minimum Days Since Last Purchase**

A minimum number of days that must have passed since the customer's last payment before they can be sent an abandoned basket recovery email.

**Maximum Discounts Received In Past 30 Days**

A maximum amount of discounts received via abandoned basket recovery within the past 30 days, after which no further discounts will be sent.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/abandoned-basket-recovery#customizing-the-recovery-email)

Customizing the Recovery Email

You can fully customize the design and content of the abandoned cart recovery email using HTML.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/abandoned-basket-recovery#steps)

Steps:

1.  Go to **Webstore > Appearance > Templates**.
    
2.  Edit your custom template or create one if needed.
    
3.  In the template editor, open the file: `email/abandonedcart.html`
    
4.  Edit the HTML to match your brand style and tone.
    

> ⚠️ **Note:** Tebex does not provide support for custom HTML edits. Knowledge of HTML and Twig templating is recommended.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/abandoned-basket-recovery#performance-tracking)

Performance Tracking

You can monitor the effectiveness of your recovery efforts by reviewing detailed metrics such as:

*   Number of recovery emails sent
    
*   Conversion rate from abandoned cart emails
    
*   Total revenue recovered
    

To access these statistics:

*   Go to **Statistics > Abandoned Baskets**
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/abandoned-basket-recovery#tips-for-success)

Tips for Success

*   Test different **email delays** (e.g., 1–3 hours) to find the most effective timing.
    
*   Use a **moderate discount** (e.g., 10–20%) to encourage conversions without overly impacting margins.
    
*   Customize the recovery email with a **clear CTA** (e.g., “Complete your purchase now and save 15%!”).
    
*   Enable **in-game messages** for real-time reach, especially in Minecraft or FiveM communities.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/abandoned-basket-recovery#academy-guide)

Academy Guide

[PreviousCommunity Goalschevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/community-goals)
[NextPurchase Follow Upschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/post-purchase-follow-ups)

*   [Customizing the Recovery Email](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/abandoned-basket-recovery#customizing-the-recovery-email)
    
*   [Performance Tracking](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/abandoned-basket-recovery#performance-tracking)
    
*   [Tips for Success](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/abandoned-basket-recovery#tips-for-success)
    
*   [Academy Guide](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/abandoned-basket-recovery#academy-guide)

# Community Goals | Creators

Community Goals provide an engaging way for your players to collectively support your project. When customers purchase qualifying packages, their contributions count toward a defined monetary target. Once the goal is met, you can trigger automatic actions such as server-wide events, global rewards, or even launch a store-wide sale.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/community-goals#what-can-community-goals-do)

What Can Community Goals Do?

*   Unlock **server-wide rewards** (e.g., global XP boosts, loot drops)
    
*   Automatically **activate a sale** on your store
    
*   Encourage **collective progress and engagement**
    
*   Display real-time **progress via sidebar modules**
    

> ❗ Manual payments do **not** count towards Community Goals and this behavior cannot be changed.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/community-goals#how-to-set-up-a-community-goal)

How to Set Up a Community Goal

1.  **Go to**: `Engagement > Community Goals`
    
2.  **Click**: `Create Community Goal`
    
3.  **Configure the fields:**
    

Field

Description

**Name**

Internal name; not visible to customers.

**Description**

Explain the goal, target amount, and the reward players can expect.

**Image**

Upload an image to visually represent the goal on your store.

**Target**

Set the monetary target (e.g., $50) that triggers the reward.

**Activate Sale on Goal**

(Optional) Select a sale to activate once the goal is met. This will be available to all customers.

**Community Goal is Repeatable**

Enable this if you want the goal to reset after completion for ongoing contributions.

**Packages**

Select one or more packages that will contribute to the goal when purchased.

**Commands**

Enter any global server commands to execute when the goal is reached (e.g., give all players a reward).

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/community-goals#displaying-community-goal-progress-on-your-store)

Displaying Community Goal Progress on Your Store

By default, community goals run in the background. To publicly display the goal and encourage contributions:

1.  **Go to**: **Webstore > Sidebar**
    
2.  **Click**: **Add Module to Sidebar**
    
3.  **Select**: **Community Goal,** then click **Create**
    
4.  **Configure display options:**
    

Field

Description

**Header**

Title displayed above the module (visible to users).

**Community Goal**

Select the goal to link with this module.

**Bar Style**

Choose between a solid or striped progress bar.

**Animate Goal Bar**

Enable animated effects on the progress bar.

**Display Goal Amount**

Show the actual currency target (e.g., $50) instead of just a percentage.

**Start/End Time**

(Optional) Set a visibility window for the module on your store. This does not affect the goal's functionality.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/community-goals#academy-guide)

Academy Guide

[PreviousGift Cardschevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/gift-cards)
[NextAbandoned Basket Recoverychevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/abandoned-basket-recovery)

Last updated 1 month ago

*   [How to Set Up a Community Goal](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/community-goals#how-to-set-up-a-community-goal)

# Gift Cards | Creators

Gift Cards allow you to sell digital codes that carry real currency value. These codes are emailed to the customer after purchase and can be redeemed on your Tebex store either by the buyer or as a gift to others.

Gift Cards are ideal for promotions, seasonal gifts, or as part of in-game reward systems.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/gift-cards#selling-gift-cards-via-packages)

Selling Gift Cards via Packages

To offer a gift card as part of a package purchase:

1.  Go to **Webstore > Packages**.
    
2.  Create a new package or edit an existing one.
    
3.  In the **Options** section, enable:
    
    *   **Create Gift Card Upon Purchase**: Enter the value you want the gift card to hold.
        
    

> **Tip:** Typically, you’ll want the gift card value to match the package price, but this is entirely configurable.

💡 Gift Card packages support commands just like any other package, making them fully customizable.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/gift-cards#creating-a-gift-card-manually)

Creating a Gift Card Manually

To create a gift card without linking it to a package:

1.  Go to **Engagement > Gift Cards**.
    
2.  Click **Create Gift Card**.
    
3.  Fill in the following fields:
    
    *   **Card Value**: The monetary value of the gift card.
        
    *   **Note**: Internal use only (for your team).
        
    *   **Expiry Date**: Optional—leave blank for no expiration.
        
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/gift-cards#how-customers-redeem-gift-cards)

How Customers Redeem Gift Cards

Customers receive an email with their unique gift card code. At checkout:

1.  Enter the code in the **coupon code field**.
    
2.  Click **Redeem**.
    
3.  If the gift card does not cover the full amount, the customer can pay the remaining balance using a standard payment method.
    

> ❗ Gift cards cannot be used to purchase certain restricted packages. If a package does not support gift card payment, customers will be unable to complete checkout with a gift card for that item.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/gift-cards#gift-card-balance-module-recommended)

Gift Card Balance Module (Recommended)

Enhance the customer experience by adding a **Gift Card Module** to your store sidebar:

*   Allows users to check their remaining gift card balance at any time.
    
*   Can be added via **Webstore > Sidebar**.
    

This is especially helpful if gift cards are a key part of your store offering.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/gift-cards#gift-card-video-guide)

Gift Card Video Guide

# Translations & Languages | Creators

Tebex supports over **30 languages by default**, helping you reach a global audience. You can also upload **custom translations** to support unsupported languages or personalize wording throughout your store.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/translations-and-languages#set-your-stores-default-language)

Set Your Store’s Default Language

To configure language settings:

1.  Go to **Webstore** → **Translations** in your Control Panel.
    
2.  Click **Enable** for each language you want your store to support.
    
3.  Choose a **default language**—this should reflect the primary language of your customer base.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/translations-and-languages#supported-languages)

Supported Languages

Tebex currently offers the following languages:

Copy

    Afrikaans, Catalan, Czech, Danish, German, Greek, English (UK), English (US), Spanish, Finnish, French, Croatian, Hungarian, Italian, Japanese, Korean, Latvian, Malay, Dutch, Norwegian, Polish, Portuguese (Brazil), Portuguese (Portugal), Romanian, Russian, Serbian, Swedish, Turkish, Ukrainian, Vietnamese, Chinese (Simplified), Chinese (Traditional)

> 📥 Each language is available as a [downloadable translationarrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/translations)
>  file.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/translations-and-languages#custom-translations)

Custom Translations

To modify specific phrases or add a language not listed above:

1.  Download the translation file for any language.
    
2.  Open it using a text editor like **Notepad++**.
    
3.  Update any line, word, or phrase as needed.
    
4.  Upload the modified file back to your store via the **Custom Translations** section.
    

> ⚠️ Only parts of the store are editable through translation files. For complete language customization, use a custom template.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/translations-and-languages#additional-notes)

Additional Notes

*   **Tebex Support is available in English only.** If you write to us in another language, we will respond in English. You may use a translation tool when corresponding with us.
    
*   Tebex is not responsible for third-party content or tools used during the translation process.

# Subdomains & Custom Domains | Creators

Your Tebex Store can be accessed using a default `.tebex.io` subdomain or a **custom domain** that you own. This guide will walk you through how to configure both options.

> ⚠️ **Note:** Custom domains require an active **Tebex Plus** subscription. If your Plus plan expires, your custom domain will stop working.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/subdomain-and-custom-domain#subdomains)

Subdomains

By default, your store will be created at a `.tebex.io` address—for example: `https://example.tebex.io`

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/subdomain-and-custom-domain#setting-a-.tebex.io-subdomain)

📍 Setting a .tebex.io Subdomain

1.  Go to **Webstore → Domain** in your Control Panel.
    
2.  Enter your desired subdomain in the `.tebex.io` field.
    
3.  Click **Save**.
    

> ⚠️ If the subdomain is already taken, you'll need to choose a different one. We cannot manually free up subdomains—even for inactive stores.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/subdomain-and-custom-domain#subdomain-faqs)

Subdomain FAQs

**Can I lose my** `**.tebex.io**` **subdomain?** Yes, but only if:

*   You're on the free **Starter** plan, and
    
*   Your store has received **no payments for over a year**
    

Paid **Plus** plan users retain their subdomains regardless of activity.

**Can I use a** `**buycraft.net**` **subdomain instead?** No. Tebex rebranded from Buycraft and new stores are not eligible to use legacy subdomains.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/subdomain-and-custom-domain#custom-domains-plus-plan-only)

Custom Domains (Plus Plan Only)

Want a store URL like `store.yourdomain.com`? With Tebex Plus, you can use your own custom domain.

Before starting:

*   Make sure you own the domain.
    
*   Have access to its DNS settings (e.g., via GoDaddy, Namecheap, Cloudflare, etc.).
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/subdomain-and-custom-domain#how-to-set-up-a-custom-domain)

How to Set Up a Custom Domain

1.  Go to **Webstore → Domain** in your Control Panel.
    
2.  Under **Custom Domain**, click **Setup**.
    
3.  Enter your custom domain (e.g. `store.yourdomain.com`).
    
4.  Tebex will provide a **CNAME target** (e.g. `abc123.webstore.tebex.io`). Save this value.
    
5.  In your domain provider's DNS settings, create a **CNAME** record:
    
    *   **Host**: `store` (or the subdomain portion you're using)
        
    *   **Value**: the CNAME target provided by Tebex
        
    
6.  Return to the Tebex Control Panel and click **Setup** again to confirm.
    

> You must create the CNAME before clicking Setup the second time.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/subdomain-and-custom-domain#registrar-specific-dns-instructions)

Registrar-Specific DNS Instructions

We’ve outlined steps for popular domain providers:

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/subdomain-and-custom-domain#cloudflare)

🔵 Cloudflare

1.  Go to the **DNS** tab.
    
2.  Add a **CNAME** record:
    
    *   **Name**: `store`
        
    *   **Target**: your Tebex CNAME (e.g., `abc123.webstore.tebex.io`)
        
    *   Disable the orange cloud (no proxying).
        
    
3.  Save the record and wait a few minutes to verify.
    

> 🚫 We recommend **disabling CNAME Flattening** to prevent resolution issues.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/subdomain-and-custom-domain#namecheap)

🟡 Namecheap

1.  Navigate to **Domain List → Manage → Advanced DNS**.
    
2.  Add a new **CNAME** record:
    
    *   **Host**: `store`
        
    *   **Value**: your Tebex CNAME.
        
    
3.  Save and test.
    

![](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1152203580-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LuI8PwvsHA79mTA-7bh%252Fuploads%252FYMjPv22pSqEWvVC3jmhs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D91036126-cc8e-4e17-844f-4bd0750b8bb2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6c0af41c&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/subdomain-and-custom-domain#godaddy)

🟠 GoDaddy

1.  Go to your domain's **DNS Settings**.
    
2.  Add a new **CNAME** record:
    
    *   **Host**: `store`
        
    *   **Points to**: your Tebex CNAME.
        
    
3.  Save and test.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/subdomain-and-custom-domain#domain.com-hostgator-bluehost-dreamhost)

🔵 Domain.com, HostGator, Bluehost, DreamHost

Follow the same pattern:

*   Add a **CNAME** record for the subdomain you're using.
    
*   Point it to your provided Tebex CNAME.
    
*   Save, wait for DNS propagation, and test.
    

![](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.endurance.com%2Fgif%2Fcname.gif&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a7272ad8&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/subdomain-and-custom-domain#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/subdomain-and-custom-domain#cloudflare-cname-cross-user-banned-error)

Cloudflare: CNAME Cross-User Banned Error

If you're using Cloudflare and see a **"CNAME Cross-User Banned"** error, it may be due to:

*   Expired Tebex Plus plan
    
*   Incorrect DNS settings
    
*   Proxying (orange cloud enabled)
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/subdomain-and-custom-domain#resolution-steps)

Resolution Steps

1.  Fix any billing issues via the [Billing Pagearrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/billing)
    .
    
2.  Fully remove your custom domain setup in:
    
    *   Tebex Control Panel
        
    *   Cloudflare DNS settings
        
    
3.  Wait 10 minutes.
    
4.  Re-add the domain from scratch, following the steps above.
    

Still stuck? [Contact Creator Supportarrow-up-right](https://www.tebex.io/support-creator-form)
.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore/subdomain-and-custom-domain#summary-table)

Summary Table

# Offers | Creators

**Tebex Offers** is an optional monetization feature that enables you to display curated partner offers to your customers **after checkout**, helping you generate **additional, passive revenue**—with no disruption to your store’s browsing or purchasing experience.

Enable this feature to generate incremental revenue of $0.02–$0.05 per transaction—potentially thousands annually—without disrupting checkout. Post-purchase offers on the confirmation page create a seamless experience, diversify revenue, and maximise transaction value.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/offers#why-use-offers)

Why Use Offers?

*   **Effortless Monetization**: Enable once and let Tebex generate additional income on your behalf.
    
*   **Non-Intrusive UX**: Offers are only shown on the **payment confirmation page**, never during browsing or checkout.
    
*   **Zero Setup Cost**: There are **no fees** for enabling Offers.
    
*   **Brand-Friendly**: Offers are integrated into your store's confirmation flow—no pop-ups, overlays, or redirects.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/offers#how-it-works)

How It Works

Once a customer completes a purchase, an **optional offer** is shown at the bottom of the **payment confirmation page**. Examples include well-known brands such as:

*   **Rakuten** – $10 welcome bonus
    
*   **SiriusXM Platinum**
    
*   **Harry’s Shaving Club**
    
*   **Flamingo**, and more.
    

![](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1152203580-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LuI8PwvsHA79mTA-7bh%252Fuploads%252F9kuDDNYpel6bcq676CrB%252Fframe_48.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db0cdf68f-c14b-441e-b639-879a05797922&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bbcfc971&sv=2)

These offers are dynamically chosen and do not impact your store's layout, speed, or conversion flow.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/offers#revenue-and-payments)

Revenue & Payments

*   **Revenue Source**: Payouts earned through Offers are categorized as **Advertising Revenue**.
    
*   **Payout Schedule**: Revenue is reported monthly and **settled to your USD Wallet 30 days later**.
    
*   **Transparency**: All earnings are visible in your **Tebex Wallet** and included in your transaction history.
    
*   **Hands-Free Earning**: There’s no need to manage affiliates or monitor performance—Tebex handles the logistics.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/offers#customer-experience-and-brand-safety)

Customer Experience & Brand Safety

*   Offers are displayed **only post-checkout**—never during browsing, package selection, or checkout.
    
*   The feature is fully **integrated**, meaning there are **no third-party redirects**, **no pop-ups**, and **no interference** with the customer’s journey.
    
*   If you prefer not to use Offers, you can **opt out at any time** by contacting [Tebex Supportarrow-up-right](https://www.tebex.io/support-creator-form)
    .
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/offers#enabling-or-disabling-offers)

Enabling or Disabling Offers

By default, Offers may be enabled on your store to help you begin generating supplemental revenue quickly. However, if you prefer not to use Offers:

![](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1152203580-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LuI8PwvsHA79mTA-7bh%252Fuploads%252FnwYlwad04W6Lw1OMglCI%252FScreenshot%25202025-07-15%2520at%252014.24.38.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De2465f10-d703-4f9d-abed-81c940d06b5f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=52be1173&sv=2)

*   You can [**opt out**arrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/offers)
     at any time—your customer experience remains fully in your control.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/offers#best-practices)

Best Practices

*   **Monitor Your Wallet**: Your additional revenue is listed under "Advertising Revenue"—check in monthly to track performance.
    
*   **Communicate Transparently**: Let your audience know they’re supporting you just by checking out—no action needed.
    
*   **Combine with Sales or Follow-Ups**: Use Offers alongside coupons, upsells, and follow-up emails for full-funnel optimization.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/offers#important-notes)

Important Notes

*   **Currency**: Offers revenue will always be paid out in **USD**.
    
*   **Data Privacy**: Offers are shown without transferring any personal customer data to the third-party brands.
    
*   **Brand Alignment**: Offers are curated to reflect high-trust consumer brands—no aggressive advertising tactics or mismatched promotions.
    

[PreviousUpsellingchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/upselling)
[NextGame Serverschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers)

Last updated 4 months ago

# Sales | Creators

Sales allow you to offer time-limited or conditional discounts on your Tebex store, either across the entire store, selected packages, or specific categories.

When configured correctly, sales can help increase engagement, reward loyal customers, and boost revenue — while maintaining transparent, lawful pricing practices.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/sales#overview)

Overview

Sales on Tebex allow partners to offer genuine, time-limited discounts while maintaining transparency with their customers.

Partners running sales must ensure their promotions comply with relevant consumer protection laws, including:

*   The FTC’s Guides Against Deceptive Pricing (U.S.)
    
*   The EU Price Indication Directive (Europe)
    

These regulations are designed to prevent misleading or 'fictitious' discounts by ensuring that all sale prices accurately reflect genuine reductions from the product’s established base price.

By following these standards, partners help ensure that their store’s pricing remains fair, trustworthy, and legally compliant.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/sales#eligibility-requirements)

Eligibility Requirements

Before a product can be discounted, it must meet the following criteria:

*   The product must have been sold at a **stable base price for at least 30 consecutive days** before the sale.
    
*   The product’s price must **not have changed** during that 30-day period.
    

These rules help avoid unfair, 'permanent' discounts and maintain transparent pricing for customers.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/sales#how-to-create-a-sale)

How to Create a Sale

To set up a sale:

1.  Navigate to **Engagement > Sales**.
    
2.  Click **Create Your First Sale** or **Create Sale**.
    
3.  Configure the following fields:
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/sales#sale-configuration-options)

Sale Configuration Options

*   **Name** Internal name for managing the sale. _Not shown to customers._
    
*   **Effective On** Choose what the sale applies to:
    
    *   Entire store
        
    *   Selected packages
        
    *   Selected categories _(You can select multiple items in each case.)_
        
    
*   **Customer Requirements** _(optional)_ Restrict access to the sale based on:
    
    *   **Minimum Spend** – Set a lifetime spend threshold (e.g., customers must have spent $25+ historically).
        
    *   **Purchased Packages** – Only customers who previously purchased specific packages will qualify. If no requirements are selected, the sale will apply to all customers by default.
        
    
*   **Discount Type** Choose one of:
    
    *   **Fixed Amount** – E.g., $5 off.
        
    *   **Percentage** – E.g., 25% off.
        
    *   **Command Only** – No price discount is shown, but custom commands are triggered instead (e.g., bonus items, perks).
        
    
*   **Start Date & Expiry Date** Set when the sale should begin and end. The sale will activate immediately if the start date is in the past.
    
*   **Commands** _(optional)_ Execute specific commands when a package is purchased during this sale period.
    
    *   These can be used to add bonus content or perks.
        
    *   If customer requirements are defined, commands only trigger for qualifying customers.
        
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/sales#duration-and-cooldown-rules)

Duration & Cooldown Rules

To align with global pricing transparency standards, Tebex recommends the following best practices:

*   A sale should run for a **maximum of 14 consecutive days.**
    
*   A **30-day cooldown** should be observed **before the same product goes on sale again.**
    
*   A sale should **not start within 30 days of a price change.**
    
*   A **new product** should only go on sale **after it has been live for at least 30 days.**
    

While Tebex does not currently enforce these limits automatically, partners are responsible for adhering to them when scheduling and managing their sales.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/sales#displaying-sales)

Displaying Sales

Tebex automatically handles how discounts are displayed on product pages to maintain consistency and transparency.

During a sale, your product page will show:

*   The **original price** with a strikethrough
    
*   The **discounted price** beside it
    
*   Optionally, the **discount percentage**
    

triangle-exclamation

Do not manually add “SALE”, “50% OFF”, or similar language to titles, thumbnails, or package descriptions. All savings indicators must use Tebex’s built-in pricing display to ensure clarity and compliance.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/sales#expiry-and-enforcement)

Expiry & Enforcement

When the sale’s end date & time is reached:

*   The discount will **automatically deactivate.**
    
*   The product will **return to its base price.**
    

Partners should monitor sale durations to ensure they do not exceed recommended limits and that cooldown periods are respected before reactivating a sale.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/sales#troubleshooting-sale-visibility)

Troubleshooting Sale Visibility

If your sale prices aren't showing to everyone, you may have enabled a **Customer Requirement** unintentionally.

To make the sale visible to all customers:

1.  Edit the sale.
    
2.  Uncheck all **Customer Requirements** _**'Optionally select the customer requirements for this sale**_' should be displayed if you've unchecked them all.
    
3.  Save changes. The discount will now apply universally.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/sales#best-practices)

Best Practices

*   Run sales around **major updates, community events, or holidays.**
    
*   Use **percentage-based discounts** for consistency and clarity.
    
*   Review your **price history** before scheduling a sale to ensure compliance.
    
*   Avoid **frequent or overlapping discounts**, which can reduce perceived value.
    
*   [Use the Statistics panels](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/statistics)
     to **evaluate performance and improve future promotions.**
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/sales#academy-video-guide)

Academy Video Guide

Learn how to use sales and understand the different types of sales. Start at timestamp **2:42** for the sales-specific section.

# Coupons | Creators

Coupons allow you to create discount codes for your Tebex store, offering a powerful way to incentivize purchases, promote campaigns, or reward loyal customers. You can create fixed or percentage-based discounts, target specific products or categories, and control usage limits.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/coupon-codes#creating-a-coupon)

Creating a Coupon

To create a new coupon:

1.  In your Control Panel, go to **Engagement > Coupons**.
    
2.  Click **Create Your First Coupon** or **Create Coupon**.
    
3.  Complete the following fields:
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/coupon-codes#coupon-details)

Coupon Details

*   **Code**: Enter your desired code or click **Generate Code** for a random one.
    
*   **Effective On**: Choose to apply the coupon to:
    
    *   All products
        
    *   Specific packages
        
    *   Specific categories
        
    
*   **Discount Type**:
    
    *   _Percentage_: Set a value (e.g. 10%)
        
    *   _Fixed Amount_: Set a currency value (e.g. $5)
        
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/coupon-codes#duration)

Duration

*   **Start Date**: When the coupon becomes valid.
    
*   **Expiry Date**: When the coupon expires. You can check **Never** to keep it active indefinitely.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/coupon-codes#usage-rules)

Usage Rules

*   **Redeem Limit** _(optional)_: Max total redemptions across all users.
    
*   **Redeem Limit Per Customer/IP** _(optional)_: Limits usage per individual customer or IP.
    
*   **Minimum Basket Value** _(optional)_: Sets a threshold before the coupon can be used.
    
*   **Username Restriction** _(optional)_: Restricts coupon usage to a specific username.
    
*   **Note** _(optional)_: Internal-only note for tracking purposes.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/coupon-codes#coupon-application-rules-explained)

Coupon Application Rules Explained

This setting determines how the coupon interacts with other discounts or sales. Here's how each rule works:

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/coupon-codes#id-1.-apply-to-each-qualifying-package-individually)

1\. **Apply to each qualifying package individually**

Discount is applied separately to each eligible item.

Example:

*   Package A: $5 → $4.50 (10% off)
    
*   Package B: $10 → $9.00 (10% off) **Total: $13.50**
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/coupon-codes#id-2.-apply-to-basket-containing-qualifying-packages-before-sales)

2\. **Apply to basket containing qualifying packages** _**before**_ **sales**

Coupon applies first, followed by any store-wide sales.

Example with 10% coupon and 20% sale:

*   $15 basket → $13.50 (10% off)
    
*   $13.50 → $10.80 (20% off) **Total: $10.80**
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/coupon-codes#id-3.-apply-to-basket-containing-qualifying-packages-after-sales)

3\. **Apply to basket containing qualifying packages** _**after**_ **sales**

Store-wide sales apply first, then the coupon.

Same example:

*   $15 basket → $12.00 (20% off)
    
*   $12.00 → $10.80 (10% off) **Total: $10.80**
    

_While the result may appear the same in percentage examples, fixed amount discounts and minimum basket rules can lead to differences._

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/coupon-codes#managing-coupon-settings)

Managing Coupon Settings

By default, customers will be able to use an unlimited number of coupons on their basket.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/coupon-codes#change-the-max-coupons-per-basket)

Change the Max Coupons Per Basket

1.  Go to **Engagement > Coupons**.
    
2.  Click **Settings** (top-right).
    
3.  Adjust the **Max Coupons Per Basket** setting.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/coupon-codes#advanced-options)

Advanced Options

You can also manage coupons through the [Tebex Plugin API,arrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/plugin/endpoints/coupons)
 ideal for automation or integrations.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/coupon-codes#best-practices)

Best Practices

*   Use short, memorable codes for marketing (e.g. `SUMMER10`).
    
*   Set redemption limits to avoid misuse.
    
*   Combine coupons with time-limited sales for greater urgency.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/coupon-codes#academy-video-guide)

**Academy Video Guide**

Check out our video tutorial on Sales, Coupons & Gift Cards.

# Purchase Follow Ups | Creators

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/post-purchase-follow-ups#purchase-follow-ups)

Purchase Follow-Ups


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sending follow-up emails after a purchase is a simple yet powerful way to re-engage your customers, show appreciation, and drive repeat purchases. Tebex lets you automatically send a thank-you email with an optional time-limited discount coupon to help encourage loyalty and impulse buys.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/post-purchase-follow-ups#how-to-set-up-purchase-follow-up-emails)

How to Set Up Purchase Follow-Up Emails

1.  Go to **Engagement > Purchase Follow-Ups** in your Control Panel.
    
2.  Enable the feature using the checkbox at the top.
    
3.  Configure the following options:
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/post-purchase-follow-ups#configuration-options)

Configuration Options

Field

Description

**Coupon Discount (%)**

Set the percentage discount you'd like to offer in the follow-up email.

**Coupon Duration**

Define how long the coupon should remain valid (e.g. 24 hours, 3 days). Shorter durations typically lead to higher conversion rates.

**Email Delay**

Choose how long after the purchase the follow-up email should be sent. You can define the delay in **hours**, **days**, or **weeks**.

**Email Subject**

Enter the subject line of the email. Use a compelling message, such as:

_“Thanks for your support – here’s a coupon just for you!”_

**Exclude Free Payments**

Optionally disable emails for purchases made using a 100% discount or gift card, where no payment was processed through a gateway.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/post-purchase-follow-ups#customizing-the-email-design)

Customizing the Email Design

You can fully personalize the appearance and content of your follow-up email using HTML and the Tebex template system.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/post-purchase-follow-ups#to-customize-the-follow-up-email)

To customize the follow-up email:

1.  Go to **Webstore > Appearance > Templates**.
    
2.  Edit an existing custom template or create a new one.
    
3.  In the template editor, open: `email/purchasefollowup.html`
    
4.  Edit the content using HTML or Twig templating to reflect your brand voice and design preferences.
    

> ⚠️ **Note:** Tebex does not provide support for custom HTML/CSS edits.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/post-purchase-follow-ups#performance-tracking)

Performance Tracking

Measure the effectiveness of your purchase follow-up strategy directly from your dashboard:

*   Navigate to **Statistics > Purchase Follow-Ups**
    
*   View key metrics such as:
    
    *   Number of emails sent
        
    *   Number of redemptions
        
    *   Revenue generated from follow-up discounts
        
    

Use this data to refine your timing, discount amounts, and email content for maximum engagement.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/post-purchase-follow-ups#academy-video)

Academy Video

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/post-purchase-follow-ups#best-practices)

Best Practices

*   **Use urgency**: Limit coupon duration to encourage immediate use.
    
*   **Personalize your email subject**: Increase open rates with relevant, friendly messaging.
    
*   **Pair with holidays or events**: Reinforce purchase behavior around specific campaigns.
    
*   **A/B test**: Try different delays and email copy to find what performs best.

# Supported Countries for Wire Transfers | Creators

Tebex supports wire transfers to over 150 countries worldwide. This article lists all supported regions where you can receive payouts via wire transfer. Note that wire transfers incur a flat fee of **£12 per transaction** and may be subject to additional processing time or intermediary bank fees.

Before requesting a wire transfer, ensure your bank details are accurate to avoid failed or returned payments.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/pricing-overview/tebex-fees-and-billing-overview/supported-countries-for-wire-transfers#full-list-of-supported-countries)

# Custom Variables | Creators

The Custom Variables feature allows you to collect input from customers during checkout—perfect for personalized product options such as custom name tags, ranks, item colors, and more.

For example, you could ask a player what **name tag color** they want when purchasing a VIP rank. You define a variable like `{colour}` and we’ll substitute the value your customer chooses during package delivery.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/custom-variables#academy-video)

Academy Video

Learn how to create and use variables to simplify package configuration and improve the buyer experience. Ideal for servers like Pixelmon, RPGs, or any setup where you want to collect custom data.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/custom-variables#how-to-create-a-custom-variable)

How to Create a Custom Variable

To get started:

1.  In your **Tebex Control Panel**, go to **Settings** > **Variables**.
    
2.  Click **Create Your First Variable** or **Create Variable**.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/custom-variables#define-the-variable)

Define the Variable

*   **Identifier:** This is what you'll reference in commands (e.g., `{colour}`).
    
*   **Description:** Shown to the customer during checkout. For example: _“Choose your tag color”_.
    
*   **Type:** Select one of the available types:
    
    *   Dropdown (used in this guide)
        
    *   Username
        
    *   Email
        
    *   Alphanumeric
        
    *   Numeric
        
    *   And more
        
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/custom-variables#example-dropdown-variable-for-name-tag-color)

Example: Dropdown Variable for Name Tag Color

Let’s create a `{colour}` variable with three color choices using a **Dropdown**:

1.  Add options using **Add Option**.
    
2.  For each option, specify:
    

Field

Description

**Name**

What the customer sees (e.g., `Red`, `Blue`, `Green`)

**Value**

The value used in your command (e.g., `red_tag`, `blue_tag`)

**Price**

(Optional) Add a flat amount or % surcharge for premium options

**Default**

(Optional) Select a default choice to pre-fill for customers

> Once set, click **Create** to save the variable.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/custom-variables#adding-the-variable-to-a-package)

Adding the Variable to a Package

To use the variable in a package:

1.  Go to **Packages** in your Control Panel.
    
2.  Select or create a package.
    
3.  Scroll to the **Variables** section and check the custom variable you created.
    
4.  Add the variable's **identifier** (e.g., `{colour}`) into the **Command section**.
    

> When a customer makes a purchase, Tebex automatically replaces `{colour}` with the value selected.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/custom-variables#why-use-custom-variables)

Why Use Custom Variables?

*   **Simplify package management**: Avoid creating dozens of variations for every customization.
    
*   **Improve customer experience**: Let players personalize purchases easily.
    
*   **Keep commands dynamic**: Inject values directly into delivery commands.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/custom-variables#summary)

Summary

Custom Variables let you gather custom input from your buyers at checkout, making your store more flexible and powerful. With just a few steps, you can:

*   Define dynamic variables (like `{colour}`)
    
*   Use them across multiple packages
    
*   Personalize command execution automatically
    

For servers with high personalization needs—like RPGs, modded servers, or roleplay communities—this feature helps reduce friction and scale package offerings effectively.

[PreviousEmailchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/email)
[NextTeam Accountschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/team-accounts)

Last updated 6 months ago

# Customers | Creators

Tebex offers tools to help you manage your customers more effectively—whether you're reviewing customer histories or blocking fraudulent or abusive buyers.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/customers#customer-lookup-tebex-plus-feature)

**Customer Lookup** _(Tebex Plus feature)_

The **Customer Lookup** tool allows you to search for and review detailed insights on individual customers. This is particularly useful for analyzing payment history, behavior, or managing disputes.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/customers#information-available)

**Information Available:**

*   **In-game username**
    
*   **First seen** (initial store visit or purchase date)
    
*   **Total amount spent** on your store
    
*   **Chargeback rate** (specific to your store)
    
*   **Ban history** (total number of bans across all Tebex stores)
    

> _Note: Customer Lookup is available only to Tebex Plus subscribers._

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/customers#customer-bans)

**Customer Bans**

You can use **Customer Bans** to prevent specific individuals from making purchases on your store.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/customers#ban-options)

**Ban Options:**

*   **Username Ban**: Prevents a user based on their in-game or store username.
    
*   **IP Address Ban**: Blocks users at the IP level to prevent evasion.
    

> _Banned users will no longer be able to access your store checkout._

[PreviousStatisticschevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/statistics)
[NextWebstorechevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/webstore)

Last updated 6 months ago

*   [Customer Lookup (Tebex Plus feature)](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/customers#customer-lookup-tebex-plus-feature)
    
*   [Customer Bans](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/customers#customer-bans)

# Upselling | Creators

Boost customer spend by offering relevant product recommendations at checkout. Tebex’s **Upselling** feature allows you to surface complementary or high-value items when a customer is most likely to convert—during the checkout flow.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/upselling#what-is-upselling)

What Is Upselling?

Upselling helps increase revenue by:

*   Recommending **additional products** during checkout.
    
*   Offering **discounted upgrades** or **bundle-friendly items**.
    
*   Encouraging customers to **increase quantities** or switch to **higher-value alternatives**.
    

![](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1152203580-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LuI8PwvsHA79mTA-7bh%252Fuploads%252FajzKZC5DaGdPgroKTeVS%252FScreenshot%25202022-06-10%2520at%252014.31.05.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df180277f-121e-4fcc-b59c-3fc1a73e26da&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c0375318&sv=2)

Upselling to customers during the checkout flow.

All upsell options respect purchasability conditions (e.g., user limits, required packages, global limits). **Subscription products cannot be upsold.**

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/upselling#store-wide-upselling)

Store-Wide Upselling

There are two ways to apply upselling across your entire webstore:

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/upselling#id-1.-top-products-automatic)

1\. **Top Products (Automatic)**

Surface your **three most popular products** to customers during checkout.

**How to Enable:**

1.  Go to **Engagement > Upselling**.
    
2.  Enable **Upsell Top Products** at the top of the page.
    

> Tebex will automatically exclude any products already in the customer’s basket and show the next most popular instead.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/upselling#id-2.-recommended-packages-manual)

2\. **Recommended Packages (Manual)**

Manually select which packages to upsell. This overrides the Top Products method.

**How to Configure:**

1.  Go to **Engagement > Upselling**.
    
2.  Click **Add Recommended Package**.
    
3.  Choose a package to recommend.
    
4.  _(Optional)_ Set a **discounted price**.
    
5.  Click **Add**.
    

Tebex will randomly display up to three eligible recommended packages during checkout.

![](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1152203580-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LuI8PwvsHA79mTA-7bh%252Fuploads%252FwqFpgjy0zrMzOGfXwLRF%252FScreenshot%25202022-06-10%2520at%252015.09.17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dae0dca11-7943-465e-93a2-8caafd91df84&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b4338760&sv=2)

The Upselling tab within the package editor.

> ℹ️ **Best Practice:** Add at least **5+ recommended packages** to ensure there are fallback options when customers aren’t eligible for some products.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/upselling#package-specific-upselling)

Package-Specific Upselling

You can also configure upsells tied to **individual packages**, offering more targeted personalization based on what's already in the basket.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/upselling#to-set-up)

To Set Up:

1.  Go to **Webstore > Packages**.
    
2.  Edit a package and select the **Upselling** tab.
    
3.  Choose from three types of upsells:
    
    *   **Additional Product**
        
    *   **Increase Quantity**
        
    *   **Alternative Product**
        
    

Tebex will randomly select up to **3 matching upsells** from your list. If none are available, the system falls back to store-wide upsells.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/upselling#types-of-package-upsells)

Types of Package Upsells

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/upselling#id-1.-additional-product)

1\. **Additional Product**

Recommend related or complementary products.

Option

Description

**Image**

Optional thumbnail image.

**Package**

The additional product to offer.

**Offer Price**

(Optional) Discounted upsell price.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/upselling#id-2.-increase-quantity)

2\. **Increase Quantity**

Encourage customers to purchase in greater volume.

Option

Description

**Image**

Optional thumbnail image.

**Quantity**

Quantity added if selected.

**Offer Price**

Discounted per-unit price (e.g., 10 units × $5 = $50).

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/upselling#id-3.-alternative-product)

3\. **Alternative Product**

Suggest an upgrade or different version of the current package.

Option

Description

**Image**

Optional thumbnail image.

**Package**

The replacement product.

**Offer Price**

Optional upsell discount.

> The original package is removed and replaced with this product if selected.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/upselling#tracking-performance)

Tracking Performance

To monitor the effectiveness of upselling:

*   Navigate to **Statistics > Upselling**.
    
*   View additional revenue and engagement from upsell activity.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/upselling#best-practices)

Best Practices

*   **Bundle intelligently:** Pair low-cost items with premium packages to increase AOV.
    
*   **Test offer prices:** A 10–20% discount is often enough to drive conversions.
    
*   **Use upgrades:** Offer tiered versions of your ranks or services.
    
*   **Avoid overload:** Limit upsells to three visible options to reduce choice fatigue.
    

[PreviousPurchase Follow Upschevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/post-purchase-follow-ups)
[NextOfferschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/offers)

Last updated 1 month ago

# Project | Creators

The **Project** page lets you configure your store’s essential settings, including branding, currencies, pricing policies, and API behavior. This guide outlines what you can set up and how each option works.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/project#store-branding-and-identity)

Store Branding & Identity

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/project#store-name)

Store Name

Set the public-facing name of your store. This name appears in your webstore and communications.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/project#logo)

Logo

Upload your store's logo. If you’re using the default **Exo** template, this will replace the store name in the header.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/project#webstore-management)

Webstore Management

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/project#enable-webstore-management-features)

Enable Webstore Management Features

If you're using Tebex’s **Headless** or **Checkout APIs** to run your own frontend, you can disable the Tebex-hosted webstore interface. This keeps all backend features (like package management and payment processing) active while turning off the default storefront.

> 💡 Use this only if you're managing your own frontend experience.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/project#refund-policy-settings)

Refund Policy Settings

Define how Tebex Buyer Support handles refund requests for your store. Choose the policy that fits your business model:

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/project#id-1.-no-refunds-default)

1\. No Refunds (Default)

Sales are final unless:

*   The product was not delivered, or
    
*   A technical issue prevents product access.
    

> Tebex allows studios to customize refund policies to align with their specific business needs.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/project#dashboard-preferences)

Dashboard Preferences

Customize how your Dashboard data is displayed:

*   **Exclude Free Payments from Dashboard Statistics** Enable this to hide free transactions from charts and reports. _(Note: Free payments still appear in the “Recent Payments” section.)_
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/project#transfer-project-ownership)

Transfer Project Ownership

[See Store Transfers for more information](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/project/store-transfers)
 on the process.

# FiveM (Server Wrapper) | Creators

The **Tebex Server Wrapper** for FiveM simplifies the process of delivering in-game rewards and perks to players, enhancing your Tebex Store experience. Once installed and configured, players can redeem their purchases using a unique Transaction ID directly in-game.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/fivem/fivem-server-wrapper#overview)

Overview

*   **Players use:** `/redeem [Transaction ID]`
    
*   **Transaction IDs look like:** `tbx-xxxxxxxx-xxxx`
    
*   **Found in:** Payment confirmation page and email
    
*   **Purpose:** To automatically deliver packages purchased via Tebex without relying on a direct Tebex plugin or RCON.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/fivem/fivem-server-wrapper#prerequisites)

Prerequisites

Before installing the wrapper:

1.  You must have a **Tebex Store** connected to your **FiveM server**. ➤ Follow the official setup guide to connect your server.
    
2.  Ensure your server supports **MySQL**, as the wrapper requires it for tracking transactions.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/fivem/fivem-server-wrapper#installation-instructions)

Installation Instructions

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/fivem/fivem-server-wrapper#id-1.-download-and-install-the-wrapper)

1\. Download and Install the Wrapper

*   Download the [wrapper from this linkarrow-up-right](https://github.com/najeetpie/nass_serverstore)
    .
    
*   Place the unzipped folder into your server’s `resources` directory.
    
    *   Rename the folder to:
        
        Copy
        
            nass_serverstore
        
    *   Remove any `-main` suffix from the folder name if present.
        
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/fivem/fivem-server-wrapper#id-2.-import-database-structure)

2\. Import Database Structure

*   Locate the `codes.sql` file inside the wrapper package.
    
*   Import it into your server's **MySQL database** using your preferred tool (e.g., phpMyAdmin, HeidiSQL).
    

![](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1152203580-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LuI8PwvsHA79mTA-7bh%252Fuploads%252FKhsCe4BPtKGs6STA3iA0%252FScreenshot%25202025-02-20%2520at%252011.44.42.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db664dbb4-e7f5-4e42-82d1-9d72b3f48534&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6c177038&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/fivem/fivem-server-wrapper#id-3.-configure-your-server)

3\. Configure Your Server

*   In your `server.cfg`, add:
    

![](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1152203580-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LuI8PwvsHA79mTA-7bh%252Fuploads%252FnX2oh4UtuuBSeSg94DT5%252FDBImports.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfb03a812-7630-4ba1-ae04-15dec75577d7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4bf181d6&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/fivem/fivem-server-wrapper#id-4.-configure-tebex-packages)

4\. Configure Tebex Packages

For each package you want to support with the wrapper:

*   In your Tebex Control Panel, go to **Packages > Edit Package > Commands**.
    
*   Add the following command:
    
    > ⚠️ **Important:** Do not modify the variable placeholders. Use them exactly as shown.
    
*   Click the ⚙️ gear icon next to the command and set:
    
    *   **Require Player to be Online:** `Execute the command even if the player is offline`
        
    
*   Press **Update** to save changes.
    

![](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1152203580-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LuI8PwvsHA79mTA-7bh%252Fuploads%252FNdIZ4r37HUtyCa69tQXh%252Fcommandsetup.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc1c82662-d65c-4eef-8a14-e5ea6af5c3aa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=40b899fd&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/fivem/fivem-server-wrapper#id-5.-configure-the-wrapper-script)

5\. Configure the Wrapper Script

*   Open the `config.lua` file located inside the `nass_serverstore` script folder.
    
*   Define your package details and settings there.
    

![](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1152203580-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LuI8PwvsHA79mTA-7bh%252Fuploads%252F372aPa5LCDhuKZBpjTjT%252Fconfiglua.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd17eb24d-0d99-4901-9573-59aa1d6a7a3a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d35b994a&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/fivem/fivem-server-wrapper#testing-the-setup)

Testing the Setup

Once everything is in place:

1.  Make a test purchase on your Tebex store.
    
2.  In the FiveM server, enter the following command as a player:
    

If set up correctly, the purchased items or commands will be delivered to the player.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/fivem/fivem-server-wrapper#notes)

Notes

*   This setup bypasses the need for direct command polling by using the redeem flow.
    
*   Ideal for creators who want a lightweight integration or custom control over redemptions.
    
*   For more advanced automation, consider combining this with Tebex Plugin or RCON options.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/fivem/fivem-server-wrapper#faqs)

FAQs

**Q: Can I use both this wrapper and the native FiveM Tebex integration?** A: It’s recommended to use one method consistently to avoid conflicts.

**Q: What if the command doesn’t work?** A: Verify:

*   The `tebexSecret` is set properly.
    
*   The database was imported successfully.
    
*   You’re using a valid `tbx-` transaction ID.

# Hurtworld | Creators

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/hurtworld#integrating-tebex-with-your-hurtworld-server)

**Integrating Tebex with Your Hurtworld Server**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Tebex supports official integration with **Hurtworld** using the **Oxide modding platform**, enabling automated monetization through in-game rewards and webstore commands.

> **Download the Plugin** Head to your [**Tebex Control Panel → Plugins**arrow-up-right](https://server.tebex.io/plugins)
>  section to download the official **Hurtworld (Oxide)** plugin.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/hurtworld#step-by-step-installation-oxide)

Step-by-Step Installation (Oxide)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/hurtworld#id-1.-download-the-tebex-plugin)

1\. **Download the Tebex Plugin**

*   Download the **Tebex Hurtworld Plugin** from your [Tebex Control Panelarrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/game-servers)
     under the **Plugins** tab.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/hurtworld#id-2.-place-the-plugin-file)

2\. **Place the Plugin File**

*   Copy the downloaded plugin file to your server’s **Oxide plugins directory**:
    

Copy

    <HurtworldServerPath>/oxide/plugins/

> ⚠️ _Note:_ This is different from the main plugins directory.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/hurtworld#id-3.-start-or-reload-the-plugin)

3\. **Start or Reload the Plugin**

*   If your server is already running, **Oxide will attempt to auto-load** the plugin.
    
*   If not, you can manually reload it via the server console:
    

Copy

    oxide.reload Tebex

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/hurtworld#id-4.-link-your-tebex-store)

4\. **Link Your Tebex Store**

*   In your console, enter the following command:
    

> You’ll find your **secret key** under **Game Servers → Edit** in your Tebex control panel.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/hurtworld#verify-installation)

Verify Installation

Once linked, you should receive a success message in your server console.

To confirm the plugin is functioning correctly, run:

This will return configuration details and a list of available plugin commands.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/hurtworld#advanced-integration-options)

Advanced Integration Options

Tebex supports additional methods for more complex setups or cross-platform integration:

*   **Webhooks** – Automate reward delivery or analytics
    
*   **RCON** – Remote console interaction
    
*   **MySQL** – Connect your webstore data to other backend services

# Hytale | Creators

Tebex supports seamless integration with the official Hytale server via a dedicated plugin. These integrations allow automated command execution, player-specific package fulfillment, and robust monetization for server operators.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/hytale#prerequisites)

Prerequisites


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   You must have a Hytale server running
    
*   Your Tebex store must be configured for **Hytale**
    
*   Access to your server's console and FTP / File system
    

You must authenticate your server with a secret key. Find your Tebex secret key from: [**Control Panel > Integrations > Game Servers > Edit**arrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/game-servers)
.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/hytale#installation-instructions)

Installation Instructions

1.  Download the plugin from [**Tebex > Plugins > Hytale**.arrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/game-servers)
    
2.  Place the `.jar` file into `/mods` in your server directory.
    
3.  Start your server. If it is already running, you can run:
    
    Copy
    
        plugin load Tebex:Tebex-Hytale
    
4.  In console, run:
    
    Copy
    
        tebex secret YOUR_SECRET_KEY
    
5.  In-game, run:
    
    Copy
    
        tebex info
    
    Confirm your store's details are displayed.
    

**You're all set!** Your Hytale server is now fully integrated with Tebex. Ready to start earning? Create packages and publish your store today!

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/hytale#commands-and-permissions)

Commands and Permissions


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To view a list of commands available, from the console, run:

Below is a breakdown of the available commands and their permissions:

Command

Permission

Notes

tebex forcecheck

_hytale.command.tebex.forcecheck_

Immediately checks for and runs commands that are due. **Note: use this only for testing, checks are performed every 2 minutes by default**

tebex secret <key>

_hytale.command.tebex.secret_

Connects the server to Tebex.

tebex info

_hytale.command.tebex.info_

For players, displays a clickable store URL.

tebex checkout <id>

_hytale.command.tebex.checkout_

Creates an instant checkout link for a package.

tebex sendlink <username> <id>

_hytale.command.tebex.sendlink_

Creates an instant checkout link and sends it to a player.

tebex debug <true/false>

_hytale.command.tebex.debug_

Toggles verbose logging on/off.

tebex goals

_hytale.command.tebex.goals_

Shows status to any goals on your store.

buy

_hytale.command.tebex.buy_

A customizable command and message shown to the player. See '_Configuration_'

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/hytale#configuration)

Configuration


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are more in-depth configuration options available in the plugin's configuration file at `mods/Tebex_Tebex-Hytale/config.json`

Below is a breakdown of each configuration parameter and its function:

Parameter

Description

SecretKey

The current secret key for the server's store.

BuyCommandName

The customizable name for the buy command. Note: permission will always be `tebex.buy`

BuyCommandEnabled

`true` by default. `false` to disable the buy command altogether

BuyCommandMessage

The message to show when a player runs the buy command. Use `{url}` to fill in with your store's domain.

DebugMode

`false` by default. `true` to enable more verbose logging.

After making changes to your configuration file, you can apply them with:

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/hytale#support)

Support


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you are having any issues with the Tebex Hytale plugin, please make sure to **toggle debug mode on** using the command `tebex debug true` . This shows more in-depth log messages that will help diagnose the problem.

When reaching to our support team, please include these debug logs with your ticket.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/hytale#feedback)

Feedback


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The plugin is in active development. Please do not hesitate to contact us with any questions or feedback which you may have.

We have a dedicated [Feedback Formarrow-up-right](https://wkf.ms/45PQwfE)
 if you have suggestions for new features with the plugin.
