[NextFiveMchevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/fivem)

Last updated 17 days ago

*   [Installation Instructions](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/hytale#installation-instructions)

# FiveM | Creators

Tebex offers a **direct integration with FiveM** via a built-in native module—no plugin installation required. This seamless connection ensures players receive their purchases quickly and reliably.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/fivem#prerequisites)

Prerequisites

Before beginning setup:

*   You must have a **Tebex store** created with the **FiveM** store type. ➤ You can check this in your Control Panel (under your store name). ➤ If your store is not of type _FiveM_, please create a new store before continuing.
    
*   Access to your FiveM server’s `server.cfg` file.
    
*   Basic knowledge of restarting your server (via your hosting provider or local setup).
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/fivem#setup-instructions)

Setup Instructions

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/fivem#step-1-locate-your-server.cfg)

Step 1: Locate your server.cfg

Open your `server.cfg` file—this is typically found in your `server-data` folder.

> 📝 If using FTP, make sure to save changes and upload the updated file back to the server.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/fivem#step-2-connect-your-server-via-the-tebex-control-panel)

Step 2: Connect your server via the Tebex Control Panel

1.  Go to **Integrations > Game Servers**.
    
2.  Click **"Connect Game Server"** (top-right).
    
3.  Choose the **Plugin** option.
    
    > 💡 Although this says “plugin,” no download is needed for FiveM—this is a direct native integration.
    
4.  Enter a recognizable **name for your server** and click **Continue**.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/fivem#step-3-add-the-secret-key-to-your-server.cfg)

Step 3: Add the secret key to your server.cfg

Copy the **secret key** shown in the instructions and paste the following line into your `server.cfg` file:

> 🛠 Place this line near the bottom of your config file for clarity.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/fivem#step-4-restart-your-fivem-server)

Step 4: Restart your FiveM server

Restart your server as you normally would via your control panel or console.

> 🧠 If you're unsure how to restart your server, refer to your hosting provider’s documentation.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/fivem#step-5-verify-the-integration)

Step 5: Verify the integration

Return to the Tebex Control Panel and press **Continue**. If successful, your server is now linked to your Tebex store.

*   If the **Continue** button doesn’t activate, check your FiveM **server console for errors**, correct any issues, and try again.
    
*   If needed, click **Skip** and return to test later.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/fivem#final-step-test-your-setup)

Final Step: Test your setup

We recommend testing a package purchase to ensure everything is working correctly.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/fivem#notes)

Notes

*   This integration polls the server every 60 seconds for new purchase commands.
    
*   Commands support offline delivery when using FiveM’s native Tebex integration.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/fivem#faqs)

FAQs

**Q: Do I need to download a plugin?** A: No, FiveM has native Tebex support built in—no external files required.

**Q: Can I use RCON or MySQL instead?** A: While those options exist, the native plugin integration is strongly recommended for FiveM servers for maximum reliability.

**Q: Why is my package not delivering?** A: Check that your `tebexSecret` is correct, your server has restarted successfully, and that the server console doesn’t show any errors.

[PreviousHytalechevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/hytale)
[NextFiveM (Server Wrapper)chevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/fivem/fivem-server-wrapper)

Last updated 6 months ago

*   [Prerequisites](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/fivem#prerequisites)
    
*   [Setup Instructions](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/fivem#setup-instructions)
    
*   [Notes](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/fivem#notes)
    
*   [FAQs](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/fivem#faqs)
    

Copy

    sv_tebexSecret "YOUR_TEBEX_SECRET_KEY"

# Conan Exiles | Creators

Tebex officially supports **Conan Exiles** integration through our **RCON Adapter**. This allows you to run in-game commands tied to Tebex purchases, such as granting items, teleporting players, adjusting stats, and more.

> 📘 **Before You Begin** Ensure your **RCON Adapter** is properly installed and tested. 👉 View the [RCON Adapter arrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/rcon-adapter)
> Setup Guide →

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/conan-exiles#setting-up-store-commands-for-conan-exiles)

Setting Up Store Commands for Conan Exiles

Conan Exiles uses the `con` RCON command to run **console (admin) commands** **targeted at individual players**. This is different from global RCON commands.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/conan-exiles#command-format)

Command Format

Each command that targets a player **must start with**:

Copy

    con {id}

*   `{id}` is dynamically resolved by the RCON Adapter.
    
*   The adapter maps the player’s Steam/username to the internal player index automatically.
    

> 💡 _No manual indexing is needed._

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/conan-exiles#example-give-an-item-to-a-player)

Example: Give an Item to a Player

To give **5 units of Stone** (Item ID: `10001`), configure your store package command as:

Copy

    con {id} spawnitem 10001 5

This will issue the command to the correct player automatically.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/conan-exiles#common-console-commands-for-store-packages)

Common Console Commands for Store Packages

These are commonly used Conan Exiles commands you can use in your store packages:

**Action**

**Command**

Learn Emote

`LearnEmote [EmoteName]`

Toggle God Mode

`God`

Enable Build Anywhere

`PlayerCanBuildEverywhere [PlayerName]`

Level Up Follower

`LevelFollowerUpTo [Value]`

Modify Follower Stat

`SetFollowerStat [Stat] [Value]`

Modify Player Stat

`SetStat [Stat] [Value]`

Teleport Player

`TeleportPlayer X[float] Y[float] Z[float]`

Toggle Sprint Cost

`NoSprintCost`

Enable Invisibility

`Invisibility`

Fill Purge Meter (Player)

`FillPlayerPurgeMeter`

Fill Purge Meter (Clan)

`FillPlayerClanPurgeMeter`

Start Purge

`StartPlayerPurge`

End Purge

`EndPurge`

Broadcast Server Message

`BroadcastMessage [Message]`

Spawn Item

`SpawnItem [ItemID] [Quantity]`

Set Server Setting

`SetServerSetting [Setting] [Value]`

> 🗂️ For a complete command list, visit the [**Official Conan Exiles Wiki**arrow-up-right](https://conanexiles.fandom.com/wiki/Admin_Panel)
> .

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/conan-exiles#important-behavioral-notes)

⚠ Important Behavioral Notes

When using the RCON Adapter with Conan Exiles, keep the following in mind:

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/conan-exiles#command-execution-behavior)

Command Execution Behavior

*   All plugin-issued commands will appear in the server console as:
    
*   **RCON commands** provide proper success/failure reporting.
    
*   **Console/Admin commands** (`con {id} ...`) may return a success **even if the command failed**.
    

> Example: `con {id} spawnitem 1001 5` may show "success" even if `1001` is not a valid item.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/conan-exiles#command-execution-safety)

Command Execution Safety

To avoid duplicate executions:

*   Tebex assumes a **successful delivery** as long as the **target player is online**.
    
*   Commands are not re-issued unless explicitly retried or modified.
    

[PreviousTeam Fortress 2chevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/team-fortress-2)
[NextRCON (Legacy)chevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/rcon)

Last updated 6 months ago

*   [Setting Up Store Commands for Conan Exiles](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/conan-exiles#setting-up-store-commands-for-conan-exiles)
    
*   [Common Console Commands for Store Packages](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/conan-exiles#common-console-commands-for-store-packages)
    
*   [⚠ Important Behavioral Notes](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/conan-exiles#important-behavioral-notes)
    

Copy

    Received Rcon:

# Email | Creators

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/email#accessing-email-settings)

Accessing Email Settings

To update your email preferences:

1.  Go to your **Tebex Control Panel**.
    
2.  Click **Settings** from the left sidebar.
    
3.  Select **Emails**.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/email#manage-notification-recipients)

Manage Notification Recipients

You can define who should receive the following email types:

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/email#seller-receipt-emails)

Seller Receipt Emails

These are internal receipts for store creators—summarizing transaction details from the seller’s perspective. **Not intended for customers.**

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/email#customer-receipt-emails)

Customer Receipt Emails

These are automatically sent to customers as purchase confirmations and should include all necessary purchase and payment details.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/email#adding-multiple-recipients)

Adding Multiple Recipients

To send seller or customer receipts to additional recipients:

*   Enter multiple email addresses into the appropriate field.
    
*   Separate each email address with a comma.
    

**Example:**

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/email#disable-payment-received-emails)

Disable Payment Received Emails

If your store receives a high volume of transactions and you prefer not to get real-time email alerts:

*   Use the toggle at the top of the **Emails** settings page to turn off **Payment Received** notifications.
    
*   This affects only the **notification email** to the primary account holder and does **not disable receipts** for customers.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/email#summary-of-email-types)

Summary of Email Types

Email Type

Description

Intended For

**Seller Receipt**

Internal purchase summary with payment breakdown

Store Owners / Admins

**Customer Receipt**

Customer-facing receipt after a successful purchase

Buyers

# Minecraft: Bedrock Edition | Creators

Tebex offers official plugin support for Minecraft: Bedrock Edition, including authentication via Xbox accounts. You can integrate your Bedrock server using one of the following modding platforms:

*   [PocketMinearrow-up-right](https://www.pocketmine.net/)
    
*   [Nukkitarrow-up-right](https://github.com/Nukkit/Nukkit)
    

> **Note:** Our Minecraft plugins still use the name **Buycraft** (our former brand). Any mention of "Buycraft" in logs or commands refers to the Tebex plugin.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/minecraft-bedrock#step-by-step-plugin-installation)

**Step-by-Step Plugin Installation**

**1\. Download the Plugin**

Visit the [**Plugins**arrow-up-right](https://server.tebex.io/plugins)
 section of your Tebex Store control panel and download the appropriate plugin for your modding platform (PocketMine or Nukkit).

**2\. Install the Plugin**

*   Place the downloaded `.phar` or `.jar` file into your server’s `plugins` folder: `/plugins` (in your Minecraft Bedrock server root directory)
    

**3\. Start the Server**

Start or restart your server to load the plugin. Watch the server logs to confirm that the plugin loaded successfully.

**4\. Link Your Server to Tebex**

In your server console, run the following command (replacing with your **secret key**, found on the [**Game Servers**arrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/game-servers)
 page in the Tebex control panel):

Copy

    /buycraft secret YOUR_SECRET_KEY

**5\. Verify Setup**

*   In-game, type `/buycraft`. If store information is displayed, your plugin is installed and configured successfully!
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/minecraft-bedrock#advanced-integrations)

**Advanced Integrations**

Tebex supports additional integration options for advanced setups:

*   **Webhooks**
    
*   **RCON**
    
*   **MySQL**
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/minecraft-bedrock#minecraft-eula-compliance)

**Minecraft EULA Compliance**

✅ **Tebex is fully compliant with the Minecraft EULA.** We recommend reviewing [Minecraft’s EULAarrow-up-right](https://www.minecraft.net/en-us/eula)
 to ensure your monetization practices remain within the guidelines.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/minecraft-bedrock#academy-video)

**Academy Video**

[PreviousARK: Survival Evolvedchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/ark-survival-evolved)
[NextSpace Engineerschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/space-engineers)

# Billing | Creators

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/billing#plan-details)

Plan Details

On the **Billing > Plans** page, you can:

*   View your current plan status and expiration date (including trials)
    
*   Upgrade or downgrade your plan
    
*   Compare available plans and their features
    

> 📘 Learn how [plan downgradesarrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/pricing-overview/starter-and-plus-plans#plus-plan-expiry-and-cancellation)
>  are handled.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/billing#payment-method)

Payment Method

Choose how you pay for your Tebex plan:

*   Supported options: **Credit/Debit Card** and **PayPal**
    
*   Accepted cards: Visa, Mastercard, Discover, JCB, American Express
    
*   All transactions are **SSL encrypted**
    
*   **Credit card numbers are never stored** on our servers
    

> 💡 To change your payment method, visit [**Billing**arrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/billing)
>  **> Payment Method**.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/billing#vat-number-eu-stores-only)

VAT Number (EU Stores Only)

If you operate in the **European Union**, you can add your VAT number for tax compliance.

*   Must match the **billing country** of your Tebex account
    
*   Can be managed from the **Billing > VAT Number** section
    

> This helps ensure your invoices meet EU VAT regulations.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/billing#plan-receipts)

Plan Receipts

All receipts for your Tebex store subscriptions are accessible via the **Billing > Receipts** tab.

Each receipt includes:

*   ID and status
    
*   Product name (plan tier)
    
*   Date of purchase
    
*   Price
    
*   PDF download option
    

You can also **search receipts by date range** for easier tracking.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/billing#summary)

Summary

The **Billing** section centralizes your plan, payment, VAT, and receipt settings. Make sure your payment method is up to date, and don’t forget to download receipts for bookkeeping or tax filing when needed.

# Mod Guidelines and FAQs | Creators

We’re proud of the creativity and dedication of the modding community across **Steam Workshop**, **mod.io**, and our partnered platforms like **Tebex**. This guide outlines how to respect mod creators’ rights while monetizing your Space Engineers server or content.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/space-engineers/mod-guidelines-and-faqs#content-use-guidelines)

**Content Use Guidelines**

Respecting modders means respecting their rights:

*   **Do not reuse, copy, or distribute** another creator’s work — on Steam, mod.io, Tebex, or elsewhere — **without explicit permission.**
    
*   You must **not sell or offer** content you did not create unless the original author has granted permission.
    
*   Modders **have the right** to request the removal of their content from your webstore.
    

> 💡 If you’re unsure whether you can use something in your store, always ask the original author.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/space-engineers/mod-guidelines-and-faqs#banned-items-what-you-cannot-sell)

**Banned Items – What You Cannot Sell**

You **may not sell** the following through your Tebex webstore:

*   Physical products (anything requiring shipping)
    
*   Client-side mods or plugins that provide **unfair gameplay advantages**
    
*   Anything exchangeable for **real-world currency** (fiat)
    
*   Any form of **gambling** (e.g., loot boxes, skin gambling, random cash prizes)
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/space-engineers/mod-guidelines-and-faqs#violating-these-guidelines)

**Violating These Guidelines**

If your webstore violates any of the above rules:

1.  Your store will be **taken offline**.
    
2.  You will receive a **notice of violation** with instructions to resolve it.
    
3.  Your store can only be reopened after all violations are addressed.
    

> ⚠️ Repeated violations may result in a **permanent ban** from the Tebex platform.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/space-engineers/mod-guidelines-and-faqs#reporting-violations)

**Reporting Violations**

If you believe a webstore is using someone else's content without permission, you can report it in the following ways:

*   Contact a **moderation team member** via our [official Discordarrow-up-right](https://discord.gg/KeenSWH)
    
*   Email us: [\[email protected\]](https://docs.tebex.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
    
*   Use our [support portalarrow-up-right](https://support.keenswh.com/)
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/space-engineers/mod-guidelines-and-faqs#frequently-asked-questions)

**Frequently Asked Questions**

> Still have questions? Contact Keen Software House at [\[email protected\]](https://docs.tebex.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)

**Q: Can I make my server “pay-to-win”?** **A:** Yes — but be mindful of the Minecraft EULA, modding community standards, and your players. Abuse of this model may damage trust or lead to moderation if guidelines are violated.

**Q: Does the Tebex integration work on all servers?** **A:** Currently, it supports **Steam-based Space Engineers servers only**. Support for other platforms may come later.

**Q: Can I sell access to my server?** **A:** Yes. You can configure packages that offer **VIP slots, whitelist access**, or **priority joining**.

**Q: Can I sell perks like Discord roles or in-game ranks?** **A:** Yes, as long as the reward is clearly defined and doesn't breach other guidelines.

**Q: Can I sell loot boxes or randomized rewards?** **A:** No. All products sold through Tebex must be **clearly labeled and deterministic**. Players must know exactly what they’re buying.

**Q: I’m a modder. Can I sell paid modding services on Tebex?** **A:** Not at this time. Tebex is intended for **in-game monetization** linked to gameplay services — not freelance development.

[PreviousHow the Legacy Space Engineers Vanilla Integration Workschevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/space-engineers/how-the-space-engineers-vanilla-integration-works)
[NextUnturnedchevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/unturned)

Last updated 6 months ago

*   [Content Use Guidelines](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/space-engineers/mod-guidelines-and-faqs#content-use-guidelines)
    
*   [Banned Items – What You Cannot Sell](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/space-engineers/mod-guidelines-and-faqs#banned-items-what-you-cannot-sell)
    
*   [Violating These Guidelines](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/space-engineers/mod-guidelines-and-faqs#violating-these-guidelines)

# Seller Support Guidance | Creators

As a Tebex Checkout seller, you may occasionally be contacted by customers for help with the products you've sold. This guide outlines best practices, response expectations, and standards of professional conduct when handling customer support.

Our goal is to empower you to provide fast, effective, and respectful support—building customer trust and strengthening your store’s reputation.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/seller-support-guidance#key-responsibilities)

Key Responsibilities

Before offering support, make sure your store:

*   Provides **clear, accurate, and detailed product descriptions**.
    
*   Avoids “coming soon” or vague descriptions.
    
*   Clearly states compatibility, use cases, and limitations (e.g., specific frameworks or mods supported).
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/seller-support-guidance#when-tebex-contacts-you-about-a-customer)

When Tebex Contacts You About a Customer

Sometimes, a buyer may reach out to **Tebex Support**. If Tebex determines the issue needs your involvement, we will:

*   Add you to an **email thread** with the customer.
    
*   Expect your **response within 3 business days**.
    

> If you need more time (e.g., programming fixes), you must **acknowledge the thread and share an updated resolution timeframe**—not to exceed 14 days.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/seller-support-guidance#response-time-guidelines)

Response Time Guidelines

Acceptable

Unacceptable

Responding within 3 business days.

Ignoring or delaying replies.

Requesting more time (with reason and ETA).

Accepting payments while offering no support availability.

Communicating delays or escalations clearly.

Providing support outside the shared thread (invisible to Tebex).

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/seller-support-guidance#where-to-provide-support)

Where to Provide Support

All communication **must stay within the original Tebex support thread**. This helps:

*   Maintain transparency between you, the buyer, and Tebex.
    
*   Prevent misunderstandings or duplicate support efforts.
    
*   Ensure Tebex can verify your engagement if a refund is requested.
    

> ⚠️ **If Tebex sees no reply in the thread**, the payment may be refunded.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/seller-support-guidance#customer-support-etiquette)

Customer Support Etiquette

Professional, polite communication is non-negotiable.

✅ Do:

*   Use a friendly and helpful tone.
    
*   Thank customers for their purchases.
    
*   Offer clear instructions and follow-ups.
    
*   Train your team in respectful customer interactions.
    

❌ Do Not:

*   Use rude, insulting, or dismissive language.
    
*   Leak or expose any customer personal information.
    
*   Ignore repeat inquiries without resolution.
    

> Repeated violations may result in platform penalties.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/seller-support-guidance#if-you-cant-resolve-the-issue)

If You Can’t Resolve the Issue

Here are your options:

1.  **Contact Tebex Support** (with the transaction ID) for guidance.
    
2.  **Offer a refund** via:
    
    *   Tebex gift card (especially if the payment is old or via Paysafecard).
        
    *   Original payment method (if supported).
        
    
3.  **Offer an alternative product** of equal or greater value.
    
4.  **If your wallet lacks sufficient funds**, email [\[email protected\]](https://docs.tebex.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
     for next steps.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/seller-support-guidance#create-help-resources)

Create Help Resources

To reduce repetitive questions, we recommend adding:

*   A **FAQ page** on your store.
    
*   An **external wiki** or **forum post** with setup instructions, commands, and expected behavior.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/seller-support-guidance#support-example-scenarios)

Support Example Scenarios

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/seller-support-guidance#example-issue-with-rank-delivery)

Example: Issue with Rank Delivery

> _Hi Notch,_ Sorry to hear you're having trouble using your VIP rank! Everything looks correctly delivered on our end. Please try the `/vip` command in-game to join the VIP channel and use `/warp vip` to access the map. Here’s a link to our setup instructions: \[<url>\]. If it’s still not working, reply here or ask any in-game admin to assist. — _Server Admin_

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/seller-support-guidance#example-product-compatibility-issue)

Example: Product Compatibility Issue

> _Hi Notch,_ Thanks for purchasing our script. Sorry it's not working with your server setup. As mentioned in the description, this script supports QBCore vX.X and may not be compatible with other frameworks. Here's the listing for reference: \[<url>\]. Because the script works as intended and the issue is a compatibility mismatch, I won’t be offering a refund. Let me know if you have other questions! — _Server Admin_

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/seller-support-guidance#if-you-cant-locate-a-payment)

If You Can’t Locate a Payment

Rarely, a customer may report a missing payment you can’t find. In this case:

1.  **Do not issue a refund.**
    
2.  Direct the customer to **Tebex Support**.
    
3.  Inform them that you cannot assist with missing or unverified transactions.
    

> Tebex has access to deeper payment verification tools. If a screenshot is forged or details don’t match, we’ll handle it. If the error is legitimate, we’ll fix it on your behalf.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/seller-support-guidance#final-reminders)

Final Reminders

*   **Never refund externally.**
    
*   **Do not give login access to others.**
    
*   **Always remain courteous and professional.**
    
*   **Contact Tebex Support** if you’re unsure about how to proceed.

# ARK: Survival Evolved | Creators

You can connect your Tebex Store to your ARK: Survival Evolved server using our official **ArkServerAPI plugin**. This allows for automated in-game item delivery and enhanced monetization features.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/ark-survival-evolved#step-by-step-installing-the-plugin)

**Step-by-Step: Installing the Plugin**

**1\. Ensure ArkServerAPI Is Running**

Make sure your ARK server is running the ArkServerAPI framework. If it's not installed, refer to the ArkServerAPI installation guide.

**2\. Download the Tebex Plugin**

*   Navigate to the [**Plugins**arrow-up-right](https://server.tebex.io/plugins)
     section in your Tebex Store control panel.
    
*   Download the **ARK Tebex plugin** archive.
    

**3\. Install the Plugin**

*   Unzip the downloaded file.
    
*   Copy the entire `TebexArk` folder into your plugins directory: `ShooterGame\Binaries\Win64\ArkApi\Plugins\`
    

**4\. Restart Your Server**

This will load the TebexArk plugin. Check the server logs to confirm successful initialization.

**5\. Link Your Server with Tebex**

In your server console, enter the following command (replacing with your actual secret key from the control panel):

Copy

    cheat tebex:secret YOUR_SECRET_KEY

You can find your secret key in the [**Game Servers** arrow-up-right](https://server.tebex.io/game-servers)
section of your control panel. Click **Edit** next to your ARK server.

**6\. Verify Installation**

*   Check the server log for any plugin load errors.
    
*   Or type `!donate` in the in-game chat. If a link to your Tebex store appears, setup was successful!
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/ark-survival-evolved#advanced-integration-options)

**Advanced Integration Options**

Tebex also supports additional integration methods:

*   **Webhooks**
    
*   **RCON**
    
*   **MySQL**
    

These can be used for deeper integration with your server or web-based tools. Refer to our [Developer Integration Guidearrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/developers/game-server-api/overview)
 for full setup instructions.

**Academy Tutorial** Check out our video walkthrough demonstrating how to:

*   Set up Tebex with ARK
    
*   Deliver in-game items
    
*   Spawn dinosaurs using commands
    

[PreviousBuycraftXchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/minecraft-java-edition/buycraftx)
[NextMinecraft: Bedrock Editionchevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/minecraft-bedrock)

Last updated 6 months ago

# Store Transfers | Creators

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/project/store-transfers#before-you-begin)

Before You Begin

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/project/store-transfers#id-1.-id-verification)

1\. ID Verification

The **new owner** must complete identity verification **before** the transfer can take place.

1.  Visit 👉 [https://accounts.tebex.io/profilearrow-up-right](https://accounts.tebex.io/profile)
    
2.  Click **"Get Started"** under **Identity Verification**
    
3.  Follow the instructions to complete the process
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/project/store-transfers#id-2.-wallet-linked-stores-cannot-be-transferred)

2\. Wallet-Linked Stores Cannot Be Transferred

If your store is linked to a **Tebex Wallet**, it must be unlinked before proceeding.

To request this:

*   Email our **Payments & Compliance Team** at [\[email protected\]](https://docs.tebex.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
    
*   Use the **email address associated with the wallet**
    
*   Include your **store name** and a request to unlink the wallet for ownership transfer
    

Once the wallet is unlinked, you can begin the transfer process.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/project/store-transfers#how-to-transfer-store-ownership)

How to Transfer Store Ownership

1.  Go to 👉 [https://creator.tebex.io/projectsarrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/projects)
     and log in to the project you wish to transfer
    
2.  In the left-hand navigation, go to: **Settings** → **Project** → **Transfer Project Ownership**
    
3.  Click the **Transfer** button
    
4.  Enter the **email address** of the new owner
    
    > 🔐 Must be associated with an existing Tebex account
    
5.  Tebex will send **confirmation emails** to both parties:
    
    *   Click the link in **your** email to confirm
        
    *   The new owner must also confirm via their email
        
    
6.  Once both confirmations are completed, return to the **Transfer Ownership** page
    
7.  Click **Confirm** one final time to complete the transfer
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/project/store-transfers#transfer-complete)

Transfer Complete

After this step, ownership of the store will be transferred to the new account. All permissions and management access will move to the new owner.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/project/store-transfers#need-help)

Need Help?

If you experience issues during the transfer process, please contact our [support teamarrow-up-right](https://www.tebex.io/support-creator-form)

[PreviousProjectchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/project)
[NextCheckoutchevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/checkout)

Last updated 3 months ago

*   [Before You Begin](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/project/store-transfers#before-you-begin)
    
*   [How to Transfer Store Ownership](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/project/store-transfers#how-to-transfer-store-ownership)

# Rust | Creators

Tebex supports direct integration with **Rust** servers through our official plugin built for the **Oxide modding platform**.

> **Plugin Download:** Visit your **Tebex Control Panel → Plugins** section, or access the GitHub release (if applicable).

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/rust#supported-modding-platform)

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/rust#step-by-step-installation-oxide-plugin)

Step-by-Step Installation (Oxide Plugin)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/rust#id-1.-download-the-tebex-plugin)

1\. **Download the Tebex Plugin**

Download the **Rust (Oxide)** plugin from the [**Plugins**arrow-up-right](https://server.tebex.io/plugins)
 section of your Tebex Control Panel.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/rust#id-2.-install-the-plugin)

2\. **Install the Plugin**

Move the downloaded file into the following directory:

Copy

    <YourRustServer>/oxide/plugins

> Note: This is different from the main plugins folder if your server uses other modding frameworks.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/rust#id-3.-start-or-reload-the-plugin)

3\. **Start or Reload the Plugin**

If your server is already running, Oxide should auto-load the plugin. If not, reload manually using the Oxide console:

Copy

    oxide.reload Tebex

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/rust#id-4.-link-your-tebex-store)

4\. **Link Your Tebex Store**

In the server console, run the following command (replace with your actual secret key):

> You can find your **secret key** in your **Tebex Control Panel** under [**Game Servers**arrow-up-right](https://server.tebex.io/game-servers)
>  **→ Edit**.

Once linked, the plugin will display a confirmation message in your console.

To verify everything is installed correctly:

This command will display store configuration and a list of available Tebex plugin commands.

*   **Webhooks**

These can be used for syncing data across websites, CRMs, Discord bots, or analytics dashboards.

# How the Legacy Space Engineers Vanilla Integration Works | Creators

> ⚠️ **This guide is for legacy use only.** For the latest and easiest setup, we recommend the [current Tebex Vanilla pluginarrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/game-servers)
>  and our TorchAPI version.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/space-engineers/how-the-space-engineers-vanilla-integration-works#overview)

Overview

The legacy Tebex plugin for **Space Engineers Vanilla** allows you to reward players without relying on console commands — giving you flexibility when building custom server experiences.

You can integrate Tebex in two ways:

1.  **Using the Companion Plugin**: Trigger prebuilt reward commands like `!giveitem` and `!givemoney`.
    
2.  **Creating a Custom Plugin**: Listen for purchase events and write your own logic.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/space-engineers/how-the-space-engineers-vanilla-integration-works#tebex-event-communication)

Tebex Event Communication

The main plugin (`TebexSE.dll`) notifies your server of incoming purchases via:

*   An **event**: `TebexSE.TebexSE.tebexPurchaseEvent.TebexPurchaseReceived` (Recommended for plugin developers)
    
*   A **chat message** in the `GlobalScripted` channel (Use this for modding or scripts that respond to chat)
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/space-engineers/how-the-space-engineers-vanilla-integration-works#option-1-use-the-companion-plugin)

Option 1: Use the Companion Plugin

We provide a prebuilt plugin that supports several basic reward commands:

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/space-engineers/how-the-space-engineers-vanilla-integration-works#available-commands)

Available Commands

> Replace anything in `[square brackets]` with actual values. Keep `{id}` as-is — it auto-inserts the Steam64 ID of the purchaser.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/space-engineers/how-the-space-engineers-vanilla-integration-works#download)

Download

Get the companion plugin from GitHub: [**Tebex-SE-Consumer on GitHub**arrow-up-right](https://github.com/tebexio/Tebex-SE-Consumer)

> 💡 This is the fastest way to get started. You can also extend this plugin with your own commands (see below).

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/space-engineers/how-the-space-engineers-vanilla-integration-works#option-2-create-a-custom-plugin)

Option 2: Create a Custom Plugin

To build your own reward system, subscribe to the Tebex purchase event and handle the received command.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/space-engineers/how-the-space-engineers-vanilla-integration-works#example-code-snippet)

Example Code Snippet

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/space-engineers/how-the-space-engineers-vanilla-integration-works#integration-notes)

Integration Notes

*   Add `TebexSE.dll` as a reference in your plugin project.
    
*   Commands from Tebex are passed **as strings**, so it’s up to you to **parse and process them** appropriately.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/space-engineers/how-the-space-engineers-vanilla-integration-works#extending-the-companion-plugin)

Extending the Companion Plugin

Prefer modifying instead of starting from scratch? Extend the [Tebex-SE-Consumerarrow-up-right](https://github.com/tebexio/Tebex-SE-Consumer)
:

*   Update the plugin references:
    
    *   DLLs from your **Space Engineers server**
        
    *   `TebexSE.dll` from your **Tebex control panel**
        
    

This lets you add new commands or logic without rewriting the whole system.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/space-engineers/how-the-space-engineers-vanilla-integration-works#academy-video)

Academy Video

[NextMod Guidelines and FAQschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/space-engineers/mod-guidelines-and-faqs)

Copy

    !giveitem {id} [ItemID] [Amount]         // e.g. !giveitem {id} Ingot/Iron 10
    !givemoney {id} [Amount]                 // e.g. !givemoney {id} 1000
    !reserveslot {id}
    !unreserveslot {id}
    !rank {id} [RankName]                    // e.g. !rank {id} Scripter
    !say [Message]                           // e.g. !say Thanks for your purchase

Copy

    csharpCopyEdit// Called by Space Engineers when the server is ready
    public void Init(object gameInstance) {
        TebexSE.TebexSE.tebexPurchaseEvent.TebexPurchaseReceived += TebexPurchaseEvent_TebexPurchaseReceivedHandler;
    }
    
    private void TebexPurchaseEvent_TebexPurchaseReceivedHandler(string details) {
        if (details.StartsWith("!myplugin")) {
            // Handle your custom command
        }
    }

# FiveM Beta Assets Best practices | Creators

* * *

A FiveM script creator may want to create a “Beta” asset—a temporary asset given to a buyer to test, review, or use. Cfx and Tebex policies don’t allow assets to be revoked, so the asset given to the buyer is final and stays with the buyer.

Below are Creator Success' best practices when it comes to Beta Assets:

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/fivem-beta-assets-best-practices#assets-are-final-and-non-revocable)

Assets are final and non-revocable

When giving an asset to a buyer, they will keep it indefinitely. **There is no way for the seller, Tebex, or Cfx to revoke it.**

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/fivem-beta-assets-best-practices#trust)

Trust

Only grant beta assets to a buyer you fully trust. If you are worried about the asset being leaked, re-sold, shared, etc. - **do so at your own risk.**

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/fivem-beta-assets-best-practices#hidden-packages)

Hidden packages

When creating these beta assets, keep them hidden in your Tebex store so other buyers won’t be able to buy them. You can still change and grant them, but they won't be visible in your public store.

[PreviousFiveM Best Practices for Packageschevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/fivem-best-practices-for-packages)
[NextCreator Success: Case Studieschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/creator-success-case-studies)

Last updated 7 months ago

# Trustpilot reviews incentives best practices | Creators

**1\. Follow Trustpilot’s Guidelines**

*   **Allowed**: Offering a reward (e.g., gift card, coupon) in exchange for submitting a review of their experience.
    
*   **Not Allowed**:
    
    *   Rewarding customers only for leaving a positive or 5-star review.
        
    *   Asking exclusively satisfied customers to review while excluding others.
        
    

* * *

**2\. Structuring Incentives Correctly**

*   Rewards must apply to **any review,** positive, neutral, or negative.
    
*   Example message (compliant): _“We’d love your feedback on your recent purchase. As a thank-you for your time, you’ll receive a $5 gift card once you share your review on Trustpilot.”_
    

Keep language neutral. Avoid phrases like “Leave us a great review” or “Help us get 5 stars.”

* * *

**3\. Communicate Transparently**

When requesting reviews, always make it clear that:

*   Writing a review is **optional**.
    
*   Rewards are provided regardless of rating or sentiment.
    
*   Customers will be informed how and when the reward (e.g., gift card) will be delivered.
    

* * *

**4\. Timing Review Requests**

*   Best practice: Send review requests shortly after the customer’s experience.
    
*   Suggested timing:
    
    *   **Game server purchases**: 1–2 days later.
        
    *   **Script or software purchases**: ~14 days later.
        
    
*   Automating this process (via email flows or in-platform messaging) helps capture feedback while the experience is fresh.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/trustpilot-reviews-incentives-best-practices#compliance-checklist)

Compliance Checklist

✅ Rewards apply to all reviews, regardless of sentiment ✅ Neutral, non-leading messaging ✅ Transparent reward terms and delivery details ✅ Requests sent at an appropriate time after purchase ❌ No rewards tied only to positive/5-star reviews ❌ No selective outreach to only “happy” customers

[PreviousSubscription Stability and Growthchevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/creator-success-case-studies/subscription-stability-and-growth)
[NextAn Introduction To Commandschevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/command-management/an-introduction-to-commands)

Last updated 4 months ago

# MySQL Depreciation | Creators

If your store currently uses MySQL Commands to deliver packages, you will need to **transition to a supported integration type** to ensure continued functionality.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/mysql#recommended-replacement-webhooks)

Recommended Replacement: Webhooks

For most creators, the best replacement for MySQL Commands is our **Webhooks integration**.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/mysql#what-are-webhooks)

💡 What are Webhooks?

Webhooks allow Tebex to send **real-time HTTP requests** to an endpoint (a script or application you host). These requests contain all the relevant payment data, such as:

*   Transaction ID
    
*   Purchased items
    
*   Player details
    
*   Pricing and timestamp info
    

You can then process this data however you like — including executing the **same MySQL logic** you previously used.

> **More flexible and secure than raw SQL execution**

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/mysql#other-integration-options)

🔀 Other Integration Options

Depending on your game and infrastructure, you may prefer one of our other supported methods:

**Integration Type**

**Use Case**

**Webhooks**

Real-time event handling with full control over command logic

**RCON (via RCON Adapter)**

Direct command execution for RCON-compatible game servers

**Game Plugins**

Official plugin support for games like Minecraft, Rust, ARK

**File Downloads**

Deliver game files, configurations, or mods to customers

**License Keys**

Sell and distribute product keys for third-party software

**CFX KeyMaster Assets**

Monetize assets for **FiveM** servers via KeyMaster integration

> 🔍 You can explore and configure these integration types from your **Tebex Control Panel**.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/mysql#getting-started-with-your-migration)

Getting Started with Your Migration

To begin your transition:

*   **Set up Webhooks** directly from your Control Panel.
    
*   **Need help with your existing MySQL logic?** Webhooks allow you to replicate this functionality by executing MySQL queries on your own backend after parsing incoming webhook data.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/mysql#prefer-a-different-integration-type)

🔀 Prefer a Different Integration Type?

You can also choose from any of our other supported methods, depending on your game or workflow needs:

*   [**RCON**arrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/rcon-adapter)
     – using our modern RCON Adapter for improved reliability
    
*   [**Official Plugins**arrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/plugins)
     – available for selected games (check compatibility here)
    
*   [**File Downloads**arrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/product-deliverables-configuration#file-downloads)
     – deliver server files, mods, or resources
    
*   [**License Keys**arrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/product-deliverables-configuration#license-keys)
     – distribute product keys or activation codes
    
*   [**CFX KeyMaster Assets**arrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/product-deliverables-configuration#fivem-assets)
     – for monetizing FiveM content through KeyMaster
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/mysql#need-help)

Need Help?

[Contact Tebex Support arrow-up-right](https://www.tebex.io/support-creator-form)

# Checkout | Creators

The [**Checkout Settings**arrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/payment-methods/settings)
 page lets you customize how your Tebex store handles transactions, gifting, sales tax, and testing. These controls help align your checkout experience with your branding, tax compliance, and operational preferences.

> To access this page: In your **Tebex Control Panel**, click **Settings** at the bottom of the left sidebar, then select **Checkout**.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/checkout#customer-support-email)

Customer Support Email

Specify the email address Tebex should use when forwarding **customer support queries**.

*   This is **only** used for support—not for billing or system notifications.
    
*   You may use a different email than your Tebex login.
    

> Want to give support access to your team? Learn more about [Team Accountsarrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/team-accounts)
> .

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/checkout#currency-settings)

Currency Settings

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/checkout#default-currency)

Default Currency

Select the primary currency used in reports and pricing. Customers will see this currency unless **Regional Pricing** is enabled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/checkout#supported-currencies)

Supported Currencies

Add additional currencies to allow localized transactions. Tebex will automatically detect a customer's location and charge them in their local currency when possible.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/checkout#regional-pricing)

Regional Pricing

Enable pricing adjustments based on customer location. This feature helps you localize prices and optimize revenue across different markets. [Learn more about Regional Pricingarrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/project/regional-pricing)
.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/checkout#rounding)

Rounding

This setting applies to any additional currencies you choose to support. Since currency conversion can sometimes result in prices with irregular decimals, you can configure rounding options to ensure that prices appear clean and customer-friendly. The available options are:

*   No Rounding
    
*   Round to nearest whole unit
    
*   Round to nearest half
    
*   Round to nearest .99
    
*   Round to nearest .97
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/checkout#allow-gifting)

Allow Gifting

Enable gifting to let customers purchase packages for other users.

*   When enabled, customers see a **“Purchase as Gift”** option during checkout.
    
*   You can disable gifting for specific packages in the **Gifting section** during package creation/editing.
    

> ⚠️ **Note for Minecraft Servers:** Due to username-based verification, customers could technically purchase using someone else's username—even if gifting is disabled. This limitation is inherent to how usernames are processed.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/checkout#dark-mode)

Dark Mode

If you’re using a dark storefront theme, you can enable **Dark Mode** for the checkout interface.

*   This changes the checkout background to a dark variant to match your branding.
    
*   Only affects the **payment flow**, not the full storefront.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/checkout#sales-tax-mode)

Sales Tax Mode

Control how sales tax is displayed to customers:

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/checkout#inclusive-pricing)

Inclusive Pricing

*   Tax is **included** in the listed package price.
    
*   Common outside the U.S.
    
*   Creates “what you see is what you pay” pricing.
    
*   May **reduce your earnings per sale**.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/checkout#exclusive-pricing)

Exclusive Pricing

*   Tax is **added** at checkout.
    
*   Standard in the U.S.
    
*   Preserves margins, but may **increase cart abandonment** due to higher total prices.
    

> Learn more in our [Sales Taxarrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-checkout/vat)
>  Guide.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/checkout#test-mode)

Test Mode

Use **Test Mode** to simulate purchases without making real transactions.

*   Test the full checkout flow, including package delivery.
    
*   No actual payment method required.
    

> Need help testing package delivery? See our [How to Test a Package](https://docs.tebex.io/welcome)
>  article.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/checkout#removing-test-payments)

Removing Test Payments

Once testing is complete, use **Remove Test Payments** to delete all test entries from your Payments list.

*   This **does not undo deliveries** triggered during tests.
    
*   Remember to **disable Test Mode** before going live, or your store will not charge real customers.
    

[PreviousStore Transferschevron-left](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/project/store-transfers)
[NextRegional Pricingchevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/checkout/regional-pricing)

Last updated 1 month ago

# Discord Servers | Creators

Tebex allows you to monetize your Discord community by selling access to roles through your store. With our official Discord bot, you can automatically assign or remove roles and send customized messages when users make purchases—creating seamless integration between your store and your Discord server.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/discord-bot#connecting-your-discord-server)

Connecting Your Discord Server

To link your Discord server to your Tebex store:

1.  Log in to the **Tebex Control Panel**.
    
2.  Navigate to **Discord Servers**.
    
3.  Click **Connect Discord Server**.
    
4.  Follow the on-screen instructions to authorize the connection.
    

> Once successfully connected, you can define Discord Actions when creating packages on your Tebex store.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/discord-bot#discord-actions)

Discord Actions

After setting up your Discord server in the control panel, you can assign **Discord Actions** to individual packages. These actions will execute automatically upon purchase.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/discord-bot#available-actions)

Available Actions

*   **Assign Role** Automatically assign a role to the customer upon purchasing a package.
    
*   **Remove Role** Remove a specific role from the customer—useful for time-limited access or subscription-based content.
    
*   **Send Message** Send a customized message to any channel in your Discord server. Messages can include dynamic variables (see below).
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/discord-bot#discord-specific-variables)

Discord-Specific Variables

When configuring a message in a Discord Action, you can use both [**Tebex standard variables**arrow-up-right](https://docs.tebex.io/store/command-management/an-introduction-to-commands#variables-to-customise-your-commands)
 and the following **Discord-specific variables**:

*   `{discordId}` – The customer’s Discord ID ([snowflake format)arrow-up-right](https://discord.com/developers/docs/reference#snowflakes)
    . ➤ To mention the user, use: `<@{discordId}>`
    
*   `{discordTag}` – The customer’s Discord tag (e.g., `TestUser#0001`)
    

> To include a clickable link to a specific Discord channel, use: `<#channelID>` Example: `<#696748377349681212>`

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/discord-bot#tebex-discord-bot)

Tebex Discord Bot

*   **Bot Username**: `Tebex#8323`
    
*   **Bot ID**: `695664615534755850`
    

Our bot must be present in your Discord server for actions to function properly. It handles all role assignments, message deliveries, and slash commands.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/discord-bot#watch-the-setup-tutorial)

Watch the Setup Tutorial

Want to see it in action? Watch our official tutorial on how to set up and install the Tebex Discord Bot:

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/discord-bot#using-slash-commands)

Using Slash Commands

Tebex's Discord bot supports modern **slash commands** for customer interactions. Type `/` in any server channel to see available options:

Command

Description

`/buy`

View available packages

`/claim`

Claim a recent purchase

`/refresh`

Refresh Discord actions and roles

`/id`

Retrieve your Discord-linked Tebex ID

`/link`

Link your Discord account to Tebex

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/discord-bot#tips-and-best-practices)

Tips and Best Practices

*   Ensure the bot has **Manage Roles** permission.
    
*   Place the bot’s role **above** the roles it needs to assign/remove.
    
*   Use separate channels for bot messages to keep things clean.
    
*   Test actions with a sample package before going live.

# Space Engineers Item IDs | Creators

To create a Tebex package that gives an in-game item to a player, you’ll need to specify the item’s **ID**. Item IDs are required when configuring the `give_item` command in your Tebex plugin.

*   **Format:** `Category/ItemName` _(e.g.,_ `_Ingot/Iron_`_,_ `_Component/Motor_`_)_
    
*   **Mod Support:** Modded item IDs are supported as well. Please refer to your mod’s documentation for those values.
    

> **Tip:** You can enable **Debug Mode** in the Tebex plugin settings to print a full list of available item IDs in your server console at startup.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/space-engineers/space-engineers-item-ids#how-to-use-item-ids-in-tebex-packages)

**How to Use Item IDs in Tebex Packages**

Here’s an example of a Tebex command using an item ID:

Copy

    give_item Ingot/Iron 100

This will deliver **100 units of Iron Ingots** to the player.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/game-servers/space-engineers/space-engineers-item-ids#vanilla-space-engineers-item-ids)

# Gift Cards | Creators

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/gift-cards#what-are-gift-cards)

What are gift cards?


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Gift Cards allow you to sell unique codes that can only be used on your Tebex webstore, which contain a balance of real currency.

The customer will enter the code into the same box as coupon codes and then click redeem. If the Gift Card balance is lower than the total basket value, they can pay the rest using a payment gateway.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/gift-cards#why-use-gift-cards)

Why use gift cards?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Allows for potential buyers and frequent spenders to feel more comfortable purchasing via budgeting with Gift Cards and to “trial” your store.

Minimises buyer’s anxiety - especially in the instances where an established player gifts a potential new player, a gift card to have a look around with.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/gift-cards#how-to-set-up-gift-cards)

How to set up Gift Cards


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Go to Webstore > Packages and create a package as you normally would.
    
2.  Enter the following options to automatically send the customer a Gift Card once they purchase the package:
    
    *   Create Gift Card Upon Purchase - Enter the value of the Gift Card you'd like the customer to receive.
        
    

circle-info

You would normally enter the package price as the amount the Gift Card should be valued at. You can also set the packages to execute commands; they're no different than any other package you would normally create.

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/gift-cards#tips)

Tips


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/gift-cards#pricing)

Pricing

We recommend having 3 gift cards at 3 different price points:

*   **Entry-level gift card**
    
    *   This should be priced so buyers can buy something from your store but not your most sold package.
        
    
*   **Value price gift card**
    
    *   This is the gift card you aim to sell the most of. It should cover the price of your most sold package and be higher than your average transaction value.
        
    
*   **High-value gift card**
    
    *   This gift card should be a high gift card that allows buyers to buy multiple items from the store.
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/gift-cards#example)

Example

circle-info

Demo Store wants to start selling gift cards. Their most sold package is an MVP rank that costs $21.99. The store’s average transaction is $19.93.

Gift card prices:

*   $10.99 (buyers can still buy an item from the store)
    
*   $26.99 (buyers can buy the MVP Rank and higher than the average transaction)
    
*   $50 (buyers can buy multiple items using this gift card)
    

![](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1152203580-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LuI8PwvsHA79mTA-7bh%252Fuploads%252FmIAsnw0FzqEQoERrnFEJ%252Fchrome_38HNUjRV9i.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3093a569-6191-4fce-a3f6-c7bd25bac99d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=94827685&sv=2)

Example gift card

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/gift-cards#success-tips)

Success Tips


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Analyze your target audience:**

*   What is their typical spending behaviour?
    
*   Are they price-sensitive or willing to pay a premium for convenience or experience?
    
*   Offer a range of options to cater to different budgets.
    

**Competitive landscape:**

*   Research the price of gift cards at similar stores or platforms.
    
*   Highlight any unique features or benefits your gift cards offer to justify a higher price.

[NextCommunity Engagement chevron-right](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/community-engagement)

# Sales Calendar - 2026 | Creators

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/sales-calendar-2026#sales)

Sales


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sales for webstores are all about fueling growth and increasing revenue:

*   More sales, more money: Plain and simple sales directly translate to increased revenue and profit. Every purchase is a shot of rocket fuel propelling your webstore forward.
    
*   New customer deals: they act like magnets, drawing in new customers who might become loyal fans down the line. Sales are your chance to welcome aboard a whole new fleet of happy shoppers.
    
*   Loyalty: Strategic sales show your existing customers some love, rewarding them for their support and encouraging them to come back for more.
    
*   Data: Sales are great data points, revealing valuable insights into customer behaviour and buying preferences. Use this data to refine your marketing tactics.
    

**Remember:** Sales are a powerful tool, but wield them wisely. Tailor your offers, communicate clearly, and always prioritize quality over quantity. With thoughtful planning and execution, sales can be your secret weapon for unlocking explosive webstore growth!

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/sales-calendar-2026#tips)

Tips


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Start planning your sales early**. This will give you time to create a budget, develop marketing materials, and prepare your inventory. Tebex allows you to [schedule salesarrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/sales)
     by setting start and end dates.
    
*   **Promote your sales heavily**. Use social media, email marketing and other channels to inform your customers about your upcoming sales.
    
*   **Create a sense of urgency**. Use countdown timers, limited-time offers, and flash sales to encourage customers to shop during your promotions.
    
*   **Track your results**. Use analytics tools to track your sales results and see what's working and what's not; [view Tebex analytics here.arrow-up-right](https://creator.tebex.io/statistics)
    

> If you require more assistance, please reach out to [\[email protected\]](https://docs.tebex.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/sales-calendar-2026#tools)

Tools


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Tebex has a variety of tools you can use to setup promotions during these times:

*   [Sales](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/sales)
     offer discounted prices on selected packages.
    
*   [Coupon Codes](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/coupon-codes)
     offer more specific targeting and can make for effective call-to-actions.
    
*   [Gift Cards](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/engagement/gift-cards)
     are great for seasonal giveaways, encouraging spend on-top of their use.
    
*   [Regional Pricing](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/tebex-control-panel/settings/checkout/regional-pricing)
     can help you celebrate region-specific occasions and offer more targeted discounts.
    

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/sales-calendar-2026#global-sales-calendar)

Global Sales Calendar


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1152203580-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LuI8PwvsHA79mTA-7bh%252Fuploads%252F6bb9G2GMmeL2b1dFc73U%252FSales%2520Calendar%2520Dates%2520-%25202026.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D812091a1-3dad-4449-93ea-95efd36a2160&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=678237ea&sv=2)

circle-info

Above are examples of recommended times to create sales for your store. If your game server has specific region players, you can also create specific regional sales.

# Community Engagement  | Creators

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/community-engagement#tips)

Tips:


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/community-engagement#your-customers-come-from-somewhere)

Your Customers Come from Somewhere.

Social media and Discord are your greatest tool in getting people to at least look at or, interact with your store.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/community-engagement#community-management-is-just-as-important-as-development-and-design)

Community management is just as important as Development and Design.

Making sure you have a healthy customer base who is welcoming to new customers and keeps old ones is how we grow our stores.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/community-engagement#stuck-ask-your-community)

Stuck? Ask your community.

No one knows what the customer wants better than the customer. Having a platform to interact with them is a great way to pick their brain.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/community-engagement#if-a-tree-falls-in-the-woods)

If a tree falls in the woods...

If no one knows about your new product/sale - was there even a new product or sale?

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/community-engagement#platforms)

Platforms:


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/community-engagement#discord)

Discord

Amazing way to foster a community and there a plethora of plugins and tools such as support ticketing systems, auto mods and events (sales/coupons). Almost a requirement in this day and age.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/community-engagement#twitter-or-x-im-going-to-keep-calling-it-twitter)

Twitter or “X” (I’m going to keep calling it Twitter.)

Albeit not the industry giant it once was, it’s an easy platform to announce and get updates on your store regularly.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/community-engagement#youtube)

YouTube

Great way to produce marketing/support resources for you and your product - algorithm also helps getting outreach for your community that you might not have reached before.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.tebex.io/creators/growth-and-success/community-engagement#anything-really)

Anything Really!

Any marketing or opportunity to show your stuff should be taken - Reddit, Instagram etc. Having more presence online, always helps.
